### [1] [Improving Heart-Focused Medical Question Answering in LLMs via Variance-Aware Rubric Rewards with GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05174)
*Arash Ahmadi,Parisa Masnadi,Sarah Sharif,Charles Nicholson,David Ebert,Mike Banad*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对医疗领域小模型部署难题，提出了一种基于方差感知的GRPO优化框架，通过引入连续化的准则奖励机制，显著提升了模型在心脏医学问答任务中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用大语言模型在医疗领域的部署面临隐私限制、推理成本高及难以在边缘/终端设备运行等挑战。因此，需要开发更小、更高效的模型，并配合稳健的后训练策略以确保其具备可靠的医学推理能力。

Method: 本文引入了群组相对策略优化（GRPO），并提出了“方差感知奖励框架”（Variance-Aware Reward Framework）。该框架通过将基于准则的评估结果转化为连续的分析奖励函数，取代了传统的加权二元聚合或单一整体评分，从而为稀疏且复杂的多准则反馈提供更丰富的优化信号，以增强策略优化过程的稳定性。

Result: 在HealthBench的心脏医学子集上，使用该方法训练的Qwen3-14B模型性能显著提升，准确率从0.362提高至0.502，F1分数从0.532提高至0.668，性能表现足以媲美拥有1200亿参数的GPT-OSS模型。

Conclusion: 本文验证了通过精心设计的基于准则的奖励机制（Rubric-based rewards），可以有效提升中小型大语言模型在特定医疗领域（如心脏医学）的问答推理能力。该方法不仅展示了在资源受限环境下的应用潜力，还为多准则、难以自动验证的任务提供了一种稳定且高效的强化学习优化范式。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown strong promise in healthcare applications. Yet deploying general-purpose models in real-world settings remains difficult due to data privacy constraints, inference costs, and limited suitability for edge or on-device use. These challenges motivate the development of smaller, more efficient models that require robust post-training strategies to ensure reliable medical reasoning. In this work, we investigate Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for post-training LLMs on heart-focused medical question answering with rubric-based supervision derived from RaR-Medicine. We propose a Variance-Aware Reward Framework that extends the Explicit Aggregation and Implicit Aggregation strategies of Rubrics as Rewards by replacing weighted binary criterion aggregation and single overall Likert-style scoring with continuous analytical reward functions derived from criterion-level rubric outcomes. This formulation provides richer optimization signals for feedback that is sparse, multi-criteria, and difficult to verify automatically, and enables more stable on-policy reinforcement learning. On a held-out heart-related subset of HealthBench, our best GRPO variant improves accuracy from 0.362 to 0.502 and F1 from 0.532 to 0.668 relative to the Qwen3-14B base model, while remaining competitive with GPT-OSS-120B (0.508 accuracy, 0.674 F1). Our findings show that carefully designed rubric-based rewards provide a practical strategy for improving heart-focused medical question answering in LLMs, with potential to extend to other rubric-based tasks.

</details>


### [2] [Generic Triple-Latent Compression with Gated Associative Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05175)
*Liu Xiao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究引入了一种通用三重潜在序列模型，通过运行状态与压缩内存路径捕获高阶标记交互，在基础语言模型基准上优于小型Transformer，尽管其增强版检索功能仍面临效率与稳定性挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的序列建模方法在处理高阶标记交互时往往依赖于特定的基准解析，缺乏通用性。作者旨在探索一种无需特定解析的通用架构，能够在保持计算效率的同时，更好地捕捉序列数据中的复杂依赖关系。

Method: 研究提出了一种通用的三重潜在序列模型。该架构的核心在于维护一个运行中的标记状态（running token state）和一个压缩的对内存路径（compressed pair-memory pathway），旨在无需特定任务解析的情况下，直接捕获序列中的高阶标记交互。此外，研究还引入了基于门控的键值（Key-Value）检索扩展，以增强模型的关联记忆检索能力。

Result: 该模型在字节级WikiText-2和基于标记器的MiniMind基准测试中，相比小型Transformer基线模型取得了性能提升。针对关联检索的扩展版本虽然提升了记忆能力，但目前在参考实现中存在计算速度较慢以及对随机种子较为敏感的问题。

Conclusion: 三重潜在序列模型（Triple-latent sequence models）为处理长序列和高阶交互提供了一种通用且有效的架构思路。尽管该方法在基准测试中表现出潜力，但扩展版本仍面临效率和训练稳定性（种子敏感性）方面的挑战，未来需进一步优化实现以提升其实用性。

Abstract: We study generic triple-latent sequence models that maintain a running token state and compressed pair-memory pathway to capture higher-order token interactions without benchmark-specific parsing. The triple-latent family improves a small Transformer baseline on byte-level WikiText-2 and on a tokenizer-based MiniMind language-model benchmark, while a recall-focused gated key-value retrieval extension improves associative recall but remains seed-sensitive and much slower in the current reference implementation.

</details>


### [3] [From Scoring to Explanations: Evaluating SHAP and LLM Rationales for Rubric-based Teaching Quality Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05180)
*Ivo Bueno,Babette Bühler,Philipp Stark,Tim Fütterer,Ulrich Trautwein,Dorottya Demszky,Heather Hill,Enkelejda Kasneci*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于SHAP和LLM的自动化评分可解释性框架，研究发现SHAP在解释评分依据时比LLM生成的推理更准确、忠实且具有更好的模型迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动化评分模型虽然广泛应用于复杂的语言评估，但通常缺乏可解释性，无法提供关于评分依据的深入洞察。现有研究缺乏对评分模型解释忠实度和逻辑一致性的系统评估框架。

Method: 提出了一种结合模型无关的Shapley值（SHAP）归因与大型语言模型（LLM）生成推理的解释性框架。利用NCTE语料库，在CLASS框架的反馈质量维度上，系统对比了微调的预训练语言模型（PLMs）与提示工程LLM在评分准确性和解释忠实度（通过基于删除的测试）上的表现。

Result: 1. 在预测准确性上，微调后的PLMs优于LLM，但在中等评分上存在标签压缩问题；2. 基于删除的测试显示，SHAP识别出的句子更能驱动模型预测，且比LLM推理产生更显著、连贯的预测偏移；3. SHAP归因在不同架构间具有稳健的迁移性，而LLM推理的影响则有限且不一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明，SHAP（沙普利值）在提供基于量规的评分解释方面，比LLM生成的推理更具忠实度和可迁移性。提出的评估框架为高风险教育环境下的评分模型及其解释的可信度评估提供了严谨的方法论基础。

Abstract: Automated scoring models are increasingly used to assign rubric-based quality ratings to complex language performances, including classroom transcripts, yet they typically provide little insight into why a particular score is produced. We propose a general framework for sentence-level interpretability of rubric-based scoring that combines model-agnostic Shapley-value attributions with rationales generated by large language models (LLMs). Instantiated on the Quality of Feedback dimension of the CLASS framework using the NCTE corpus, the framework enables systematic comparison of fine-tuned pretrained language models (PLMs) and prompted LLMs on both scoring performance and explanation faithfulness. Across 6k annotated transcript segments, fine-tuned PLMs outperform LLMs in prediction accuracy but exhibit label compression toward mid-scale scores. Deletion-based tests show that SHAP identifies sentences that reliably drive model predictions, producing typically larger and more coherent prediction shifts than LLM-generated rationales. Cross-model analyses further reveal that SHAP attributions transfer robustly across architectures, whereas LLM rationales exert limited and inconsistent influence. Overall, the findings demonstrate that SHAP provides more faithful and transferable explanations for rubric-based scoring, and that the proposed framework offers a principled basis for evaluating both scoring models and their explanations in high-stakes educational settings and other rubric-based language assessment tasks.

</details>


### [4] [When Evidence is Sparse: Weakly Supervised Early Failure Alerting in Dialogs and LLM-Agent Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05414)
*Avinash Baidya,Xinran Liang,Ruocheng Guo,Xiang Gao,Kamalika Das*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对多轮对话中失败证据稀疏且滞后的难题，本文提出了一种基于注意力机制的稀疏证据检测方法与可控停止策略（α-STOP），有效提升了早期失败预警的准确性与灵活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的早期分类方法通常错误地假设对话的每一个片段（prefix）都携带相同的失败标签，而这在多轮语言交互中并不适用，因为失败的证据往往是稀疏且滞后的。因此，需要一种能够从稀疏证据中学习并实现可控预警的方法。

Method: 1. 引入两阶段建模方法：首先使用基于注意力机制的预测器，从轨迹级标签中学习稀疏的轮次级失败证据，从而估计部分交互的失败风险。2. 设计了 α-STOP 策略：一种偏好条件化的停止策略，能够在推理阶段动态选择准确率与及时性的权衡点，避免了针对每个偏好重复训练模型。

Result: 1. 实验发现关键失败证据仅出现在 4.7-11.3% 的对话轮次中，且通常出现在对话后期。2. 所提出的注意力预测器在帕累托前沿质量上比传统方法提升了 1-10%。3. 完整系统在多项基准测试中将帕累托前沿质量提升了 3-42%，并将训练成本降低了 1-3 个数量级。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于稀疏证据检测和可控策略的早期预警框架，证明了在多轮交互中，失败证据通常是稀疏且滞后的，通过准确识别关键证据并配合自适应停止策略，可以显著提升系统在准确率与及时性之间的权衡表现。

Abstract: Early failure alerting requires deciding, while a dialog or agent trajectory is still unfolding, whether to flag it as likely to fail. This is challenging because supervision is typically available only as a trajectory-level success/failure label while alerts must be raised from partial interactions. Prior early-classification methods often bridge this gap by assigning the terminal label to every prefix, treating every turn as failure evidence. We hypothesize that this prefix-label assumption is poorly matched to multi-turn language interactions, where evidence of eventual failure is sparse and often delayed. In this paper, we introduce a two-stage approach that learns from this sparse evidence structure and uses the resulting risk estimates for controllable early alerting. Specifically, our attention-based failure predictor learns sparse turn-level failure evidence from trajectory labels and uses it to estimate failure risk from partial histories. We then pair this predictor with $α$-STOP, a single preference-conditioned stopping policy that selects an accuracy-earliness operating point at inference time rather than training a separate trigger for each preference. Across five benchmarks spanning customer support, task-oriented dialog, persuasion, tool use, and planning, we first show that high-relevance failure evidence occupies only 4.7-11.3% of turns and first appears after 59.0-83.6\% of trajectories on average. We further show that the attention-based predictor improves Pareto-frontier quality (hypervolume) by 1-10\% over naive prefix supervision, and that the full system improves frontier quality by 3-42\% over state-of-the-art trigger policies while reducing training cost per operating point by 1-3 orders of magnitude.

</details>


### [5] [AURA: Intent-Directed Probing for Implicit-Need Surfacing in Situated LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05557)
*Yang Li,Jiaxiang Liu,Jiang Cai,Mingkun Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AURA 是一款能理解用户查询背后隐含意图的智能体，通过引入“意图框架”进行推理和差距评估，在提高需求响应覆盖率的同时，显著降低了工具调用成本并强化了隐私保护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的工具使用智能体（如 ReAct 风格）通常只回答用户的字面查询，而忽略了查询背后往往包含的隐含意图（如询问某人在哪其实是为了判断是否方便打扰）。作者旨在构建一种能够识别并处理这些隐含需求的智能体。

Method: 提出了一种名为 AURA 的智能体架构，核心是在场景感知与工具使用之间插入了一个推理步骤。该步骤生成一个“意图框架”（IntentFrame），包含对隐含需求的结构化估计以及一个用于控制探测预算和工具选择的标量“差距评分”（gap score）。

Result: 在包含100个查询的隐含意图基准测试中，AURA 提升了对隐含需求的覆盖率（提升幅度为 0.07，p < 10^-6）；在事实查询任务中，AURA 在减少 82% 探测次数的同时，在隐私敏感场景下实现了零违规，且未通过记忆答案来投机取巧。

Conclusion: AURA 通过引入“意图框架”有效提升了智能体识别并满足用户隐含需求的能力，在保障效率和隐私的前提下，实现了从简单的字面回答到更具主动性和智能性的交互升级。

Abstract: A situated query like "where is Lin Wei?" often encodes more than its literal content: the user may also want to know whether Lin Wei is free, in a good mood, or worth interrupting now. Standard tool-use agents answer the literal question and stop. AURA inserts an inference step between scene perception and tool use that produces an IntentFrame: a structured estimate of the implicit need with a scalar gap score that controls per-query probe budget and tool selection. On a 100-query four-scene implicit-intent benchmark, AURA improves implicit-need coverage over ReAct-style probing (Delta = +0.07, p < 10^-6); three of four scenes are individually significant, the gain reproduces on a second backbone, and a prompt ablation attributes the lift to gap calibration rather than answer memorisation. On factual lookup the controller trades raw accuracy for 82% fewer probes and zero forbidden-tool violations on a privacy-sensitive slice; scope conditions are detailed in Limitations. Code, simulator, and benchmark are released at https://github.com/innovation64/AURA.

</details>


### [6] [Predictable Scaling Laws of Optimal Hyperparameters for LLM Continued Pre-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05610)
*Yongwei Zhou,Juncheng Diao,Junlin Shang,Peiguang Li,Rongxiang Weng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于缩放定律的自动化框架，通过量化计算预算与超参数的关系，显著降低了大模型持续预训练中的超参数搜索成本（最高减少90%），同时保持了优异的训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型持续预训练的超参数配置长期依赖启发式经验或昂贵的网格搜索，导致训练不稳定且成本过高。研究旨在寻找一种基于Scaling Laws的量化方法，以高效预测持续预训练的最优超参数。

Method: 提出了一套两阶段超参数预测框架：1. 经验定律发现阶段：通过小规模代理模型建立计算预算与最优超参数之间的函数映射；2. 状态感知预测阶段：根据初始检查点的验证损失估算其“等效预训练计算量”，结合目标计算预算预测出最优超参数。

Result: 该方法在多种架构上验证有效，能够减少高达90%的超参数搜索开销，且模型性能与传统方法持平甚至更优，证明了该框架具有良好的普适性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种基于缩放定律（Scaling Laws）的预测框架，实现了大模型持续预训练过程中超参数的自动化、精准化配置，不仅大幅降低了计算成本，还为持续预训练提供了通用的理论指导。

Abstract: The efficacy of continued pre-training for Large Language Models (LLMs) hinges upon hyperparameter configurations, such as learning rate and batch size. However, current practices often rely on heuristics or grid searches, leading to training instability and excessive costs. In this work, we first empirically discover that optimal hyperparameters follow stable and predictable scaling laws throughout the continued pre-training process. Leveraging these insights, we propose a novel framework to establish quantitative relationships between compute budget and optimal hyperparameters for a given checkpoint. Our approach has two stages: (1) \textit{Empirical Law Discovery}, where we train small-scale proxy models to derive functions mapping compute budget to optimal hyperparameters via standard loss-compute scaling laws; and (2) \textit{State-Aware Hyperparameter Prediction}, where we evaluate an initial checkpoint's validation loss and use the inverse scaling law to estimate its \textit{equivalent pre-training compute} -- the compute needed to achieve the same loss from scratch. Combining this with the planned compute budget, we predict optimal hyperparameters for the target run. Empirical results demonstrate that our method reduces the hyperparameter search overhead by up to 90\% while achieving comparable or superior performance relative to baselines. This model-agnostic framework generalizes across architectures, providing a principled and efficient methodology for diverse continued pre-training scenarios starting from any given point.

</details>


### [7] [Bootstrapping Semantic Layer from Execution for Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05634)
*Youngwon Lee,Jaejin Kim,Seung-won Hwang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GATE 是一种通过执行反馈引导数据库接地（grounding）的文本到 SQL 框架，它通过实时验证假设并积累执行记录，有效解决了领域知识缺失带来的歧义问题，显著提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实中的文本到 SQL 任务往往存在说明不充分的问题，即用户的短语与数据库实际存储的值之间缺乏明确的关联（接地）。现有的预定义语义层方法在专家领域中通常不完整且难以维护，导致 SQL 生成时存在多个不确定的接地假设。

Method: 引入了 GATE（Grounding After Test from Execution）框架。该方法在存在多种接地假设时，通过保持假设开放并利用执行反馈进行观察，筛选出唯一支持的假设，将其作为记忆条目存储，并允许后续任务步骤重用这些已验证的接地信息。

Result: 在真实世界和受控基准测试中，GATE 始终优于强基线模型，证明了该方法在处理未指定接地信息时的有效性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: GATE 证明了执行反馈不仅可以作为文本到 SQL 任务中的验证手段，还可以作为引导机制构建可重用的执行基础内存，从而有效解决复杂数据库领域中接地（grounding）信息缺失的问题。

Abstract: Real-world text-to-SQL is often under-specified until user phrases are grounded in how the database stores values. Prior work attempts to address this by requiring a semantic layer to specify groundings in advance, but such specifications are often incomplete, especially in expert domains where domain-specific conventions are under-documented. As this leaves multiple grounding hypotheses open for the same SQL part, we introduce GATE (Grouding After Test from Execution), which bootstraps missing groundings from execution feedback. GATE keeps grounding hypotheses open while executing the already grounded parts to obtain observations. Then, only the hypothesis supported by that observation is grounded and stored as a memory entry, recording what was tested and how the open part should be written in SQL. These entries accumulate into execution-grounded memory, allowing later steps to reuse supported groundings. Across real-world and controlled benchmarks, GATE consistently improves over strong baselines, demonstrating that execution can serve not only as validation but also as a bootstrapping mechanism for reusable memory in text-to-SQL.

</details>


### [8] [QueryAgent-R1: Bridging Query Generation and Product Retrieval for E-Commerce Query Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05671)
*Dike Sun,Zheng Zou,Jingtong Zang,Qi Sun,Huaipeng Zhaoand Tao Luo,Xiaoyi Zeng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 QueryAgent-R1 框架，通过将查询生成与实时检索反馈挂钩并引入强化学习一致性奖励，解决了电商搜索中查询相关性与下游转化率不匹配的问题，有效提升了点击率与转化率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的电商查询推荐方法主要关注查询层面的相关性，忽略了推荐查询所检索到的产品是否符合用户的最终转化需求，导致了查询点击率（CTR）高但转化率（CVR）低的“错位”问题。

Method: 1. 提出了一个内存增强的代理框架 QueryAgent-R1；2. 引入了“检索链优化（chain-of-retrieval）”，将查询生成与实时库存检索关联，实现基于检索产品的查询验证与修正；3. 在代理强化学习过程中设计了“一致性奖励（consistency reward）”，同时优化查询相关性与下游转化率；4. 构建了内存抽象模块以进行高效的用户画像建模。

Result: 在离线数据集上，QueryAgent-R1 表现优于主流基准模型；在工业生产环境的大规模 A/B 测试中，该方法实现了查询点击率（CTR）提升 2.9%，引导转化率（CVR）提升 3.1%。

Conclusion: QueryAgent-R1 证明了将检索环节纳入代理决策过程，并利用强化学习优化下游转化目标，是提升电商搜索推荐效果的有效途径。该研究提出的基于产品反馈的查询生成和一致性奖励机制，成功弥补了查询相关性与最终转化率之间的差距。

Abstract: Query recommendation in e-commerce search aims to proactively suggest queries that match users' potential interests. However, existing methods mainly optimize query-level relevance, while neglecting whether the retrieved products align with users' downstream preferences. This mismatch often leads to high query click through rates (CTR) but low product conversion rates (CVR). To bridge this gap, we propose QueryAgent-R1, a memory-augmented agentic framework that improves end-to-end alignment via chain-of-retrieval optimization. Our QueryAgent-R1 grounds query generation in real inventory retrieval, allowing the agent to validate and refine queries based on retrieved products. We also design a consistency reward in the agentic reinforcement learning (RL) process to jointly optimize query relevance and downstream engagement. In addition, we construct a memory abstraction module for efficient user profiling. To support offline evaluation, we construct two datasets based on both proprietary industrial data and public datasets, on which QueryAgent-R1 consistently outperforms strong baselines. Moreover, on a large scale production platform, QueryAgent-R1 improves Query CTR by 2.9% and guided CVR by 3.1% in online A/B tests.

</details>


### [9] [Interpreting Style Representations via Style-Eliciting Prompts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05716)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有利用大语言模型解释文本风格表示的方法存在模型偏见、幻觉问题，且缺乏明确的优化目标和实际应用价值，难以对潜在的风格表示进行准确且可操作的解释。

Method: 提出了一种基于风格诱导提示的框架：首先构建了包含26个类别、1010个独特风格特征的数据集，利用大模型生成相应特征的文本；随后训练一个解码器，使其能够从风格表示中重构出对应的风格描述提示词；最后通过风格恢复、风格仿写及控制输出等多项任务验证其有效性。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在恢复原始风格提示、基于重构提示生成一致风格文本以及引导大模型匹配人类写作风格等方面，均显著优于传统的直接提示基准方法。

Abstract: Style representation learning is a powerful tool for authorship analysis and modeling writing style, yet the latent nature of learned representations makes them difficult to interpret. However, such descriptions are often prone to the LLM's biases and hallucinations, and they lack an explicit objective and practical utility. In this work, we propose a novel framework for interpreting style representations through style-eliciting prompts: natural language instructions designed to steer LLMs to generate text that reflects specific stylistic attributes. We curate 1,010 distinct style features spanning 26 stylistic categories and construct a dataset by prompting an LLM to generate text conditioned on these features. Using this data, we train a decoder to generate a style prompt from the style representation of the generated text. We evaluate our approach on three tasks: (1) recovering original style prompts from generated text, (2) generating text in the same style using the recovered prompts, and (3) steering LLM outputs to match the style of human-written texts. Experiments demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms strong baselines that directly prompt LLMs with target text, achieving superior performance in both style description and style imitation. These results highlight that style-eliciting prompts can provide a practical and interpretable interface to stylistic information encoded in style representations.

### [10] [Can LLMs Be Constrained to the Past? Improving Knowledge Cutoff through Recall-Based Prompting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05804)
*Michiro Asai,Ailiang Lin,Yu Kishimoto,Takao Obi,Satoshi Kosugi,Kotaro Funakoshi,Manabu Okumura*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了解决大型语言模型在遵循知识截止日期时的不足，本文提出了两种提示策略（SR与QR），通过引导模型回顾截止日期前的约束和相关知识，显著提升了模型在面对复杂因果及反事实问题时的合规性与准确度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的知识截止提示方法主要依赖直接回答，在处理非显式查询但与截止日期后知识存在因果关联的问题时，往往难以严格遵守时间限制。为了解决这一局限性，研究者旨在探索更有效的引导方式。

Method: 作者提出了两种基于回溯的提示策略：1. 自我回溯（Self-Recall, SR）：要求模型重述其知识截止限制；2. 问题回溯（Question-Recall, QR）：要求模型提取并回顾在截止日期前有效的相关信息。此外，作者构建了多截止点历史事件基准（MHEB）用于全面评估模型在不同时间设定下的性能。

Result: 实验表明，SR和QR策略在三个现有基准测试上均优于直接回答及常规思维链（CoT）基线，在反事实问题上表现尤为出色。MHEB测试结果进一步证实，结合使用SR和QR能始终达到最佳性能，并揭示了模型性能随截止距离变化的趋势。

Conclusion: 通过实施提示约束（Self-Recall）和基于问题的回溯（Question-Recall）策略，可以有效引导大型语言模型遵循特定的知识截止日期，特别是在处理具有因果关联或反事实问题时，这种方法显著提升了模型的稳健性和准确性。

Abstract: Prompted knowledge cutoff instructs a large language model (LLM) to act as if information beyond a specified cutoff date were unavailable. However, prior work mainly relies on direct-answer generation, which struggles when post-cutoff knowledge is not explicitly queried but is only causally related to the question. To address this limitation, we propose two recall-based prompting strategies: Self-Recall (SR), which asks the model to restate its cutoff constraint, and Question-Recall (QR), which requires the model to recall question-relevant information valid under the cutoff. Across three existing benchmarks, our methods outperform both direct-answer prompting and conventional step-by-step reasoning baselines, with particularly strong improvements on counterfactual questions. To investigate robustness across different cutoff settings, we further construct the Multi-cutoff Historical Event Benchmark (MHEB), which evaluates the same question under multiple cutoff years. Results show that knowledge cutoff performance varies with cutoff distance, while combining SR and QR consistently yields the best performance.

### [11] [ProSPy: A Profiling-Driven SQL-Python Agentic Framework for Enterprise Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05836)
*Zhaorui Yang,Huawei Zheng,Sen Yang,Yuhui Zhang,Haoxuan Li,Zhizhen Yu,Xuan Yi,Chen Hou,Defeng Xie,Chao Hu,Minfeng Zhu,Dazhen Deng,Haozhe Feng,Danqing Huang,Yingcai Wu,Peng Chen,Wei Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ProSPy 是一个创新的 SQL-Python 代理框架，通过自动分析数据、精简数据库模式以及混合使用 SQL 和 Python，有效解决了企业级 Text-to-SQL 任务中数据复杂、元数据缺失及分析困难的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Text-to-SQL 系统在面对企业级数据库时表现不佳，主要原因是现实数据库存在架构庞大且异构、元数据不全、方言差异大以及复杂分析需求难以通过单一 SQL 查询解决等难题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ProSPy 的“分析驱动型 SQL-Python 代理框架”，主要包含四个阶段：1. 自动分析（Profiling）以提取细粒度数据证据；2. 基于任务相关性对大规模模式（Schema）进行剪枝；3. 通过方言无关的 SQL 接口获取中间视图；4. 利用 Python 执行灵活的下游数据分析。

Result: 在 Spider 2.0-Lite 和 Spider 2.0-Snow 基准测试中，ProSPy 表现优于现有强基准模型。在使用 Claude-4.5-Opus 模型时，无需多数投票即可分别达到 60.15% 和 60.51% 的执行准确率。同时，实验证明了该框架在处理不同 SQL 方言时的鲁棒性，并在模式召回率与精确度之间取得了良好的平衡。

Conclusion: ProSPy 通过结合 SQL 处理大规模数据的效率与 Python 进行复杂分析的灵活性，成功应对了企业级 Text-to-SQL 的挑战，不仅降低了对元数据的依赖，还增强了跨 SQL 方言的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large language models have substantially advanced Text-to-SQL systems, yet applying them to enterprise-scale databases remains challenging. Real-world databases often contain large and heterogeneous schemas, incomplete metadata, dialect-specific SQL syntax, and complex analytical questions that are difficult to solve with a single SQL query. To address these challenges, we propose ProSPy, a Profiling-driven SQL--Python agentic framework for enterprise-scale Text-to-SQL. ProSPy structures the reasoning process into four stages: it first extracts fine-grained data evidence through automatic profiling, progressively prunes large schemas into task-relevant contexts, fetches intermediate views through a dialect-agnostic SQL interface, and finally performs flexible downstream analysis with Python. This design combines the efficiency of SQL over large databases with the flexibility of Python-based analysis, while reducing reliance on unreliable metadata and improving robustness across SQL dialects. Experiments on Spider 2.0-Lite and Spider 2.0-Snow show that ProSPy consistently outperforms strong baselines with both open-source and proprietary models, achieving execution accuracies of 60.15% and 60.51% with Claude-4.5-Opus, without majority voting. Further analysis shows that ProSPy is robust to SQL dialect variations and achieves a favorable trade-off between schema recall and precision.

### [12] [Mechanistic Insights into Functional Sparsity in Multimodal LLMs via CoRe Heads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05843)
*Ruoxi Sun,Quantong Qiu,Juntao Li,Zecheng Tang,Yihang Lou,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了多模态大模型（MLLM）内部存在“功能稀疏性”，发现了一类关键的“上下文感知检索（CoRe）”注意力头。这些 CoRe 头专门负责高效提取视觉特征，仅需保留极少数此类头部即可维持模型性能，从而为模型推理加速和架构优化提供了理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多模态大模型（MLLM）在复杂视觉语言任务中表现卓越，但其在复杂噪声环境中提取查询相关视觉特征的内部机制仍不透明。该研究旨在探究 MLLM 的可解释性，特别是揭示其跨模态检索过程中的内部结构性属性。

Method: 1. 引入“检索注意力质量（RAM）”指标，用以量化 token 级别的跨模态信息检索能力。
2. 识别出一组专门负责上下文感知检索的注意力头，命名为 CoRe（Context-aware Retrieval）heads。
3. 通过因果干预实验（消融实验）验证 CoRe 头在多模态推理中的必要性。
4. 进行模型加速实验，验证在保留关键 CoRe 头的前提下实现推理加速的可行性。

Result: 1. 发现 MLLM 内部存在明确的功能分工：CoRe 头作为专门的视觉信息提取器，而其他大部分注意力头则负责更广泛的上下文信息分布。
2. 实验证明仅消融前 5% 的 CoRe 头会导致多模态推理性能大幅下降，而消融非关键头影响微乎其微。
3. 验证了利用 CoRe 头的局部稀疏性可以在保证模型性能的前提下显著加速推理过程。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了多模态大模型（MLLM）内部存在“功能稀疏性”这一结构性原则。通过识别并验证 CoRe 注意力头在跨模态检索中的关键作用，研究不仅提升了对 MLLM 内部机制的理解，还为高效的模型架构设计与推理优化提供了理论依据和实践路径。

Abstract: While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) demonstrate remarkable proficiency on complex vision-language tasks, the mechanisms by which they extract query-relevant visual features from complex, noisy contexts remain opaque. In this paper, we present an in-depth interpretability study that uncovers a profound structural property within MLLMs: functional sparsity in cross-modal retrieval. Leveraging a token-level metric termed Retrieval Attention Mass (RAM), we identify and characterize a highly specialized subset of attention heads, referred to as Context-aware Retrieval (CoRe) heads. Across diverse visual domains and model scales, we observe a clear functional division: CoRe heads act as dedicated information extractors, while most other heads distribute attention over broader contextual regions. Causal interventions further demonstrate the necessity of these specialized heads. Ablating only the top 5% of CoRe heads causes significant degradation in multimodal reasoning performance, whereas ablating lower-ranked heads has minimal effect. Moreover, acceleration experiments validate the utility of CoRe heads, showing that leveraging this localized sparsity significantly accelerates inference while maintaining robust task performance. Our findings reveal a structural principle of functional sparsity within MLLMs, refining the current understanding of mechanistic interpretability and laying a theoretical foundation that can inspire future architecture design and model optimization.

Existing approaches primarily improve CS-ASR performance through synthetic CS speech generation or pair-specific fine-tuning on limited bilingual datasets. Nevertheless, these approaches face an inherent scalability limitation, as support for CS must be developed separately for language pairs whose number grows combinatorially with the number of supported languages. In this work, we investigate whether CS capabilities learned from a limited set of seen language pairs can generalize to unseen language pairs through model merging and domain generalization methods. ### [14] [Forgive or forget: Understanding the context of hate in audio retrieval systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05857)

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于情感控制中介的事后因果去偏框架，通过Forgive（重排序/过滤）和Forget（反事实提示）两种手段，在不牺牲文本转音频系统检索准确性的前提下，有效地抑制了有害音频内容的检索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了一种带有情感控制中介的事后因果去偏（post hoc causal debiasing）框架。具体包含两种变体：1. Forgive：通过对数几率调整（logit adjustment）对有毒音频进行重排序和过滤；2. Forget：通过生成反事实的有毒提示词来减轻有害检索的影响。该方法是模型无关的，可集成到现有检索流水线中。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在显著降低检索内容毒性的同时，对检索准确率的影响极小，实现了系统安全性和可靠性的双重提升。

Conclusion: 本文提出的事后因果去偏框架能够有效解决文本转音频系统中的有害检索问题，在保持语义相关性和检索准确性的前提下，显著提升了系统的安全性。该方法具备模型无关性，具有较强的通用性和实际应用价值。

Abstract: Handling toxic retrieval in text-to-audio systems is challenging due to contextual dependencies. Existing strategies (e.g., rephrasing, summarization) risk altering intent or omitting details. We propose a post hoc causal debiasing framework with a sentiment-controlled mediator to preserve semantic relevance while suppressing harmful speech. Our approach is model-agnostic and integrates seamlessly with existing retrieval pipelines. We introduce two variants: Forgive, which re-ranks and filters toxic audio via logit adjustment, and Forget, which generates counterfactual toxic prompts to mitigate harmful retrievals. Experiments show consistent toxicity reduction with minimal loss in retrieval accuracy, improving both safety and reliability.

### [15] [ReverseEOL: Improving Training-free Text Embeddings via Text Reversal in Decoder-only LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05858)
*Ailiang Lin,Zhuoyun Li,Yusong Wang,Keyu Mao,Kotaro Funakoshi,Manabu Okumura*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出 ReverseEOL 方法，通过结合正向和反向的 LLM 嵌入，解决了因果注意力机制导致的上下文信息缺失问题，显著提升了无训练文本嵌入的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解码器架构（decoder-only）的大语言模型具有因果注意力机制（causal attention），导致模型在生成文本嵌入时无法利用未来的上下文信息，从而产生有偏差的表示。研究旨在无需重新训练模型的前提下，通过补充信息来增强冻结 LLM 的表示能力。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ReverseEOL 的方法，通过将输入文本反转后输入到冻结的 LLM 中，获取反向嵌入（reversed embedding），并将其与正向嵌入（forward embedding）相结合。通过引入明确的单词限制（Explicit One-word Limitation）来优化这一过程，从而获得更全面、无偏的上下文表示。

Result: 在 STS 和 MTEB 基准测试中，ReverseEOL 显著提升了多种架构和规模的 LLM 作为无训练文本嵌入器的性能，验证了该方法的有效性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: ReverseEOL 是一种简单且通用的方法，通过结合正向和反向的 LLM 嵌入，有效地弥补了因因果注意力机制导致的上下文信息缺失，显著提升了训练即用型（training-free）文本嵌入的质量。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have opened new avenues for generating training-free text embeddings. However, the causal attention in decoder-only LLMs prevents earlier tokens from attending to future context, leading to biased contextualized representations. In this work, we propose Reverse prompting with Explicit One-word Limitation (ReverseEOL), a simple yet effective method for enhancing the representational capability of frozen LLMs. ReverseEOL augments the standard forward embedding with an additional reversed embedding derived from the reversed input text. Since reversing the input exposes each token to context inaccessible in the original order, the resulting reversed embedding effectively provides complementary information to the original one. As a result, combining the forward and reversed embeddings yields a richer final representation. Comprehensive experiments on STS and MTEB benchmarks demonstrate that ReverseEOL significantly improves the performance of existing training-free baselines across a broad range of LLMs with diverse architectures and scales. Extensive ablations and analyses further confirm the necessity of our reversal mechanism.

</details>


### [16] [TARPO: Token-Wise Latent-Explicit Reasoning via Action-Routing Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05859)
*Liting Zhang,Shiwan Zhao,Xuyang Zhao,Zichen Xu,Jianye Wang,Qicheng Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TARPO 是一种通过强化学习自适应切换离散生成与连续潜空间推理的新框架，解决了连续推理在探索策略上的限制，并在各类基准测试中实现了性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的潜空间推理虽然具有表达力，但因其连续表示的确定性导致在强化学习中的策略探索受限；而离散思维链虽常用，但在表达深度推理方面存在局限。作者旨在寻找一种既能保留离散采样随机性，又能利用连续推理表达能力的方法，从而增强模型的推理效能。

Method: 提出了 TARPO 框架，其核心在于引入了一个轻量级的“动作头路由”（action head router）。该路由根据当前的隐藏状态，在每个推理步骤动态决定是采用离散的 Token 生成还是连续的潜空间推理。模型采用纯强化学习方法进行端到端优化，并利用共享的组相关优势信号（group-relative advantage signal）来同步更新 LLM 主干网络和路由策略。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5（1.5B 至 7B）和 Llama-3.1-8B 模型上的实验结果表明，TARPO 在多个推理基准测试中均优于现有的显式和潜空间推理强化学习基线。分析显示，模型能够自主学习到有效的 token 级切换行为，且训练过程保持稳定。

Conclusion: TARPO 通过引入一种基于强化学习的自适应机制，成功地结合了离散思维链和连续潜空间推理的优势，证明了在大型语言模型中实现灵活的推理策略不仅可行，而且能够显著提升在复杂推理任务上的性能表现。

Abstract: Latent reasoning has emerged as a promising alternative to discrete Chain-of-Thought (CoT) in large language models (LLMs), enabling more expressive reasoning by operating over continuous representations. However, the inherently deterministic nature of continuous representations limits policy exploration in reinforcement learning (RL). To address this, we propose TARPO (Token-Wise Latent-Explicit Reasoning via Action-Routing Policy Optimization), a pure RL framework that adaptively switches between discrete token generation and continuous latent reasoning at each step. TARPO introduces a lightweight action head router that observes the current hidden state and samples a routing decision from a binary mode-selection space, preserving the stochasticity of discrete token sampling from the vocabulary. The LLM backbone and router are jointly optimized end-to-end with a shared group-relative advantage signal. Extensive experiments across Qwen2.5 (from 1.5B to 7B) and Llama-3.1-8B backbones demonstrate that TARPO consistently outperforms existing explicit and latent reasoning RL baselines across diverse benchmarks. Further analysis shows that TARPO learns adaptive token-wise switching behaviors while maintaining stable training dynamics. Our code is available at https://github.com/NKU-LITI/TARPO-master.

</details>


### [17] [Analysis of the Neglect-Zero Effect in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05864)
*Jin Tanaka,Daiki Matsuoka,Ryoma Kumon,Hitomi Yanaka*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文通过结构启动实验评估了大型语言模型是否像人类一样存在“零忽略效应”（忽视空集相关的逻辑真值），研究发现大型语言模型并不具备这种人类特有的认知偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨大型语言模型在语言处理过程中是否具备类似于人类的认知偏好。具体聚焦于“零忽略效应”（人类倾向于忽略使命题因空集而为空真的零模型），旨在揭示AI模型与人类在逻辑推理认知过程中的相似性与差异。

Method: 研究采用了基于“结构启动”（structural priming）的范式。研究者通过精心设计的“启动句”（prime）强制模型考虑零模型，并观察这种处理方式是否会影响后续“目标句”（target）的处理，从而评估模型是否存在与人类相似的认知偏差。

Result: 实验结果显示，受测的大型语言模型在面对涉及零模型的推理时，并没有表现出人类那种忽略零模型的倾向。这意味着模型对于逻辑结构的解析可能并不依赖于人类的认知启发式策略。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理包含“零模型”（zero-models）的逻辑推理任务时，并不表现出人类常见的“零忽略效应”（neglect-zero effect）。这暗示了大型语言模型与人类的语言认知处理机制存在本质差异。

Abstract: We investigate the extent to which the language processing of LLMs resembles human cognitive processes, focusing on a human cognitive bias called the $\textit{neglect-zero effect}$. This effect refers to the human tendency to ignore $\textit{zero-models}$, which are configurations that render a proposition vacuously true by virtue of an empty set. We focus on two types of inferences driven by the neglect-zero effect, and examine how LLMs process these inferences by comparing their behavior with that in an inference that does not involve the neglect-zero effect. For this purpose, we employ a paradigm based on $\textit{structural priming}$, where recent exposure to a preceding sentence (the $\textit{prime}$) facilitates the processing of a subsequent sentence (the $\textit{target}$) due to their structural similarity. We prepare primes to force LLMs to consider the zero-model, and analyze whether they also consider it in the target. The results suggest that the neglect-zero effect may not occur in the LLMs analyzed in this study. Our code is available at https://github.com/ynklab/neglect_zero

</details>


### [18] [Staying with the Uncertainty: Uncertainty-Scaffolding Strategies for Artificial Moral Advisors in LLM-to-LLM Simulated Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05890)
*Salvatore Greco,Hainiu Xu,Jacopo Domenicucci,Yulan He,Sylvie Delacroix*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了LLM作为“人工道德顾问”时应如何处理道德困境中的不确定性。研究发现，相比于劝说或盲目顺从，采用“不确定性应对策略”虽未必能大幅改变用户的道德立场，但能显著提升对话参与的质量与深度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用作人工道德顾问（AMA），学术界亟需探讨其对话模式。传统的AI往往倾向于快速给出确定的结论或顺从用户，但在处理复杂的道德困境时，这种方式可能并不理想。本研究旨在探讨AMA如何通过“与不确定性共处”来优化对话模式，从而提供更具深度的道德引导。

Method: 作者提出了三种不确定性应对模式（视角倍增、张力保持、过程反思），并将其与三种对照组模式（基线、劝说、阿谀奉承）进行对比。通过用户模拟代理与采用不同策略的AMA进行道德困境对话，并利用对话前后的问卷进行评估。此外，研究还对比了两种角色提示方式（陈述式与叙事式）的效果。

Result: 1. 不存在单一的统治模型：开放模型通过不同角色间的差异表现出模糊性，而闭合模型通过角色内部的对冲表现出模糊性；2. 角色设定影响：陈述式角色能更好捕捉初始立场的多样性，而叙事式角色能带来更真实的信念修正；3. 策略差异：所有六种AMA策略均能产生可区分的对话模式；4. 核心价值：不确定性策略的主要作用不在于改变用户的立场，而在于维持更高质量的对话参与度。

Conclusion: 研究表明，针对道德困境，LLM作为道德顾问（AMA）应通过提供“不确定性”策略来提升互动质量。研究指出不存在单一的完美模型，模型应根据其特性（开放或闭合）采用不同的策略，且叙事性提示词在促进信念修正方面表现更佳。未来设计道德AI系统时，应将“保持不确定性”作为评估对话质量的核心维度，而非仅仅关注用户的立场改变。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly deployed as Artificial Moral Advisors (AMA) in a variety of contexts: what kind of conversational patterns should they display? In this paper, we study how AMA can help their interlocutors "stay with the uncertainty". We propose three modes of uncertainty (Perspective-Multiplying, Tension-Preserving, Process-Reflecting) and compare them against three control conditions (Baseline, Persuasive, Sycophantic). A user-agent LLM engages in a dialogue on an ethical dilemma with an AMA following a specific uncertainty strategy, and completes pre- and post-conversation questionnaires. We further examine the effect of two persona prompt formats (Declarative and Narrative). We found that (1) no single model dominates as a simulated user agent, with open models aligning with human ambiguity through between-persona divergence and closed models through within-persona hedging; (2) declarative personas better capture initial stance diversity while narrative personas show more realistic belief revision; (3) all six AMA strategies produce distinguishable conversational patterns; and (4) uncertainty strategies differ not in how much stance revision they produce, but in the quality of engagement they sustain.

</details>


### [19] [EMBER: Efficient Memory via Budgeted Evidence Retention for Long-Horizon Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05894)
*Yilong Li,Suman Banerjee,Tong Che*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对长序列AI代理在处理海量历史时的效率瓶颈，本文提出了EMBER策略。它通过一种学习型机制，在处理信息时自动挑选并压缩关键证据存储为“胶囊”，在固定内存预算下显著提升了模型在面对长序列查询时的检索准确率和响应能力，避免了代价高昂的原始数据重读。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长周期代理虽然能处理海量历史，但由于受限的上下文窗口和高昂的检索成本，在面对海量数据时，如果预先保留的记忆遗漏了关键信息，系统不得不回溯庞大的原始数据，导致效率低下且开销巨大。因此，研究如何在已知查询之前，在固定预算内优化证据的保留策略至关重要。

Method: 提出了EMBER（Evidence-backed Memory via Budgeted Execution and Retention），一种学习型证据保留策略。该方法在数据摄入时将原始历史转换为“证据胶囊”（存储原文字段、检索键和元数据），并通过查询后的反馈机制训练“写入器”，使其能在固定token预算下，自动识别并保留对未来回复最关键的证据。

Result: 在LongMemEval-RR基准测试中，EMBER-14B在8192个token的保留预算下达到0.3017的F1分数，显著优于最强的非EMBER基线模型（0.1765）。在不同预算水平下，EMBER均在F1分数、保留召回率（Retain-Recall）和阅读召回率（Read-Recall）上表现出显著优势。

Conclusion: EMBER证明了在长序列处理任务中，通过学习型策略在有限预算下智能保留关键证据，比在查询时重读整个原始历史记录更能有效提升模型性能。这为构建高效的长时记忆代理提供了一种新的范式。

Abstract: Long-horizon agents can archive large histories, but future answers still incur retrieval, rereading, and context costs. When retained memory misses answer-relevant evidence, the system must return to larger portions of the raw history. We study budgeted evidence survival: before the query is known, which source evidence should be retained so that it remains recoverable and usable under a fixed retained source-evidence token budget? We instantiate this setting as Budgeted Pre-Query Retention, where memory is written during ingestion and later read without access to the full raw stream. We introduce EMBER, a learned retention policy that constructs a compact, source-backed evidence state. EMBER stores evidence capsules: verbatim source excerpts paired with retrieval keys and update metadata, preserving both grounding and read-time access. Post-query outcome feedback trains the writer to preserve evidence across the ingestion-retrieval-answer chain. On LongMemEval-RR, our LongMemEval-derived retained-evidence protocol, EMBER-14B reaches 0.3017 F1 at the 8192-token retained-evidence comparison point, compared with 0.1765 for the strongest non-EMBER budgeted baseline. Across retained source-evidence budgets, EMBER improves F1, Retain-Recall, and Read-Recall, indicating that long-horizon memory depends on retaining evidence within the budget rather than rereading larger histories.

</details>


### [20] [To Be Multimodal or Not to Be: Query-Adaptive Audio-Visual Person Retrieval via Active Modality Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05931)
*Erfan Loweimi,Mengjie Qian,Kate Knill,Guanfeng Wu,Chi-Ho Chan,Abbas Haider,Muhammad Awan,Josef Kittler,Hui Wang,Mark Gales*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对视频检索中模态缺失带来的噪声问题，本文提出了一种查询自适应框架，通过检测模态间的分数一致性来动态选择融合策略，显著提升了大规模广播视频档案的检索精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实世界的视频档案中，目标人物往往存在“听见声音但不见人影”或“看见人影但听不见声音”的情况。现有的固定多模态融合方法在某模态缺失时会引入噪声，导致检索精度低于最优的单模态系统，因此需要一种能自动识别模态有效性的检索机制。

Method: 提出了一种查询自适应框架，利用跨模态分数一致性（Cross-modal Score Consistency）来检测模态活跃度。通过比较不同模态的检索结果一致性，判断当前模态是否缺失，并据此决定是否使用多模态融合，从而规避模态缺失带来的噪声干扰。

Result: 该方法在模态检测任务中达到了89%的准确率。在BBC Rewind数据集上，该自适应系统实现了94.2%的P@1，显著优于仅语音检索（82.9%）、仅人脸检索（93.4%）及固定融合方法（90.0%），并填补了64%的真实模态标签Oracle系统与现有系统之间的差距。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了在视频检索中，动态调整多模态融合策略（而非盲目融合）对于应对“模态缺失”噪声至关重要，查询自适应框架是提升现实世界视频档案检索性能的有效方案。

Abstract: When retrieving a person from a video archive by voice and face, should the system be multimodal or not? In real-world broadcast archives, unlike curated benchmarks, a target may be heard but unseen, seen but unheard, or both. Fusing scores from an absent modality injects noise, degrading precision below the best unimodal system. We propose a query-adaptive framework that detects active modalities via cross-modal score consistency: when both modalities are active, files retrieved by one also score highly on the other; this agreement breaks down when a modality is absent. Classifiers driven by these cross-modal features achieve 89% detection accuracy. On the BBC Rewind corpus (with over 12,000 broadcast videos) the adaptive system attains 94.2% P@1, outperforming speaker-only (82.9%), face-only (93.4%), and fixed fusion (90.0%), recovering 64% of the gap to an oracle with ground-truth modality labels (96.6%).

</details>


### [21] [Measuring the sensitivity of LLM-based structured extraction to prompt, model, and schema choices in clinical discharge summaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05970)
*Martin Murin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种无需人工标注的审计方法，发现临床大模型在信息抽取中的不一致性主要源于对“缺失”的判定差异，且模型选择对多分类任务的影响远大于提示词设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在临床自由文本结构化抽取中的应用日益广泛，但目前缺乏对其输出敏感性的系统评估。现有研究多关注固定基准测试上的准确率，却忽视了上游配置选择（如提示词措辞、模型规模）如何影响提取结果的复现性与稳定性。

Method: 在不使用人工标注金标准的前提下，通过控制变量法对比不同提示词和模型规模对临床文本结构化提取的影响。研究使用MIMIC-IV v3.1出院总结，固定提取任务（17个临床文档标志和47个入院原因标签），通过Cohen's kappa衡量跨提示词的一致性，并进行双重模型比较以隔离模型选择和架构的影响。

Result: 在三向标志提取中，不同模型表现出类似的一致性水平（kappa 0.68-0.69），且将三向标签简化为二元标签可显著减少分歧；在多分类任务中，改变模型会导致约半数样本的分类标签发生变动，而改变提示词仅影响约1/8的样本，且大模型在减少“残留/其他”类别的占比方面表现更优。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一种无需人工标注的评估框架，用于量化临床大语言模型在信息抽取任务中的不确定性。结论表明，临床数据提取的差异主要源于模型对“缺失与沉默”的定义区分，且在复杂分类任务中，模型架构的选择比提示词设计对结果的影响更为显著。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly used for structured extraction from clinical free-text notes, but the sensitivity of their output to upstream configuration choices is less understood than their accuracy on fixed benchmarks. This work measures that sensitivity without human-annotated ground truth, by holding the extraction task fixed and varying one choice at a time. The fixed schema comprises 17 clinical documentation flags on a three-way yes/no/not_documented value set and a 47-tag vocabulary for the primary admission reason. Three prompt variants expressing this schema were each run at two model sizes on MIMIC-IV v3.1 discharge summaries. Cross-prompt agreement was measured by Cohen's kappa on ICD-stratified subsets. A paired same-note comparison isolated the effect of model choice, and a post-hoc collapse of the three-way flags to binary tested the schema's contribution to disagreement. On the three-way flags, the two models reach the same pooled cross-prompt agreement (median kappa 0.69 and 0.68); the larger model raises agreement on some fields and lowers it on others, a redistribution rather than the absence of an effect. Collapsing the schema to binary dissolves most of the cross-prompt disagreement, locating it on the absence-versus-silence distinction rather than on whether the finding is present. On the multi-class admission categorization, changing the model reassigns the dominant tag on close to half of all notes while changing the prompt phrasing reassigns it on roughly one in eight, and the larger model places far less mass on residual catch-all categories (44% to 26%). These patterns indicate a schema-imposed source of disagreement concentrated on the absence-versus-silence axis and a dominance of model over prompt phrasing on multi-class categorization, identified by a reusable methodology for auditing extraction reproducibility on a population-scale deployment.

### [22] [Beyond Alignment: Value Diversity as a Collective Property in Multicultural Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05985)
*Shaoyang Xu,Jingshen Zhang,Long P. Hoang,Jinyuan Li,Wenxuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出“价值多样性”作为评价多智能体系统的新指标，揭示了当前大模型系统普遍存在同质化倾向，且社会交互会进一步加剧这种多样性丧失，从而影响决策的公平性与多元性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文化评估主要侧重于单一智能体与特定文化的“价值对齐”，忽略了多智能体系统作为一个整体是否能够维持其所代表的文化多元性。作者旨在通过引入系统级的评估维度，揭示当前多元文化多智能体系统在保持文化多样性方面的不足。

Method: 研究提出了“价值多样性”这一系统级评估指标，通过衡量不同文化背景智能体在共享价值调查（基于世界价值观调查 WVS）中响应的差异性来量化。研究团队评估了19种文化和18个主流模型底座，对比了不同系统配置（如混合模型底座系统），并进一步通过参与式预算决策案例，分析了社会交互过程对系统多样性的影响。

Result: 1. 价值多样性与价值对齐并不相关，两者捕捉的是系统不同的属性；2. 当前多智能体系统的价值多样性远低于人类社会；3. 即使采用混合模型底座，也无法完全填补多样性鸿沟；4. 社会交互通过推动达成共识，进一步削弱了系统多样性，导致集体决策范围的缩小。

Conclusion: 本研究明确了“价值多样性”作为多元文化多智能体系统核心评价指标的重要性。研究结果揭示，当前基于大语言模型的多智能体系统存在显著的同质化倾向，单纯依赖单一模型架构无法实现真正的文化多样性，且社会交互进一步加剧了这一同质化过程，损害了集体决策的广泛性。

Abstract: Multicultural multi-agent systems are increasingly deployed in globally diverse settings, where different agents are grounded in different cultural backgrounds. Existing cultural evaluation focuses on value alignment: how closely a single agent matches a target culture. Yet alignment is a per-agent property and cannot reveal whether a system, taken as a whole, preserves the cultural plurality it is meant to represent. We propose value diversity as a system-level evaluation axis for multicultural agent systems, defined through the dissimilarity between culturally conditioned agents' responses on a shared value survey. Using the World Values Survey, we evaluate 19 cultures and 18 backbone models across a wide range of system configurations. We find that diversity is largely uncorrelated with alignment, indicating that the two capture complementary system properties, and that current multicultural agent systems fall substantially below human societies in value diversity. Mixed-backbone systems narrow this gap but do not close it, and the gap persists across culture compositions and agent scales. Social interaction further erodes diversity by driving agents toward consensus, and a participatory budgeting case study shows that this homogenization narrows the breadth of collective decision-making. Together, our results establish value diversity as a distinct evaluation axis for multicultural multi-agent systems and reveal a persistent homogenization tendency in current LLM-based societies. Our code and data are publicly available at https://github.com/iNLP-Lab/MultiAgent-Diversity.

</details>


### [23] [The Generator-Eraser Paradox: Community Guidelines for Responsible LLM-Assisted Dialect Resource Creation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06004)
*Wajdi Zaghouani*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了利用大语言模型（LLM）进行方言资源建设的“生成者-抹除者悖论”，提出了12条社区设计指南，并通过阿拉伯语方言案例，旨在指导研究者在利用AI提高效率的同时，有效保护语言多样性和社区主权。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）虽然能极大地加速方言资源的开发，但也带来了严重的风险，如通过偏向强势语言品种、统一正字法和形成反馈循环，导致方言的“抹除”和语言多样性的流失。特别是在面临双层语言现象或资源匮乏的语言社区中，这些风险尤为突出。因此，需要一套机制来规范LLM在方言工作中的应用，确保技术进步不以牺牲语言多样性和文化主权为代价。

Method: 1. 理论建模：结合变异社会语言学与语料库语言学，正式提出了“生成者-抹除者悖论”理论框架；2. 指南制定：推导出12条社区导向的实践原则，将其转化为可实施的设计要求；3. 案例分析：以阿拉伯语方言为例，进行深度分析与比较，验证该框架在解决双层语言现象、拼写变异及社区治理等挑战中的适用性。

Result: 提出了一个涵盖理论、实践指南和案例研究的综合框架。该框架揭示了LLM对方言工作的双重影响，并为资源构建者提供了具体的实施准则（如尊重变异性、确保社区参与等），旨在推动在保持语言真实性和多样性的前提下，安全、有效地利用AI技术开展方言数字化工作。

Conclusion: 本文构建了一个旨在平衡LLM技术潜力与语言多样性保护的理论与实践框架。通过“生成者-抹除者悖论”这一视角，强调了在利用大模型进行方言资源建设时，必须将社区主权、语言变体保护和文化真实性置于技术效率之上，从而为全球范围内的语言资源开发提供了负责任的指导方针。

Abstract: Dialect resources occupy a unique position at the intersection of scientific description, cultural preservation, and computational infrastructure. Large language models offer powerful capabilities for accelerating dialect resource development through retrieval-grounded drafting, corpus navigation, metadata enrichment, and annotation workflow support. However, the same systems pose substantial risks: they can contribute to dialect erasure by privileging prestige varieties, homogenizing orthography, and enabling synthetic feedback loops that reduce linguistic diversity over time. These risks are particularly acute for language varieties characterized by diglossia, limited written standardization, or marginalized speaker communities. This paper makes three contributions. First, we integrate insights from variationist sociolinguistics and corpus linguistics to formalize the generator-eraser paradox as a theoretical framework for understanding the dual nature of LLM-assisted dialect work. Second, we derive 12 community guidelines that operationalize this framework into implementable design requirements for dialect resource creation and documentation. Third, we provide an in-depth case study of Arabic dialects, including a structured comparison of widely used resources, to demonstrate how these guidelines address language-specific challenges including diglossia, orthographic variability, and community governance. The contribution is conceptual and operational rather than experimental, with the goal of enabling dialect communities and resource builders across languages to adopt LLMs without sacrificing authenticity, variation, or sovereignty.

</details>


### [24] [Contextualized Prompting For Stance Detection On Social Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06022)
*Tilman Beck,Shakib Yazdani,Simon Kruschinski,Marcus Maurer,Iryna Gurevych*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了向大型语言模型（LLM）输入上下文信息以辅助社交媒体立场检测的效果，发现只有特定类型的上下文（如LLM生成的目标描述）能提升性能，而盲目引入用户元数据或历史推文往往会因引入噪声而导致模型表现下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交媒体文本具有短小、噪声大及语境依赖性强的特点，现有的LLM零样本立场检测往往缺乏必要的上下文支持，导致模型难以准确解读具有歧义的观点，因此需要研究如何通过有效融合上下文信息来提升LLM的立场检测能力。

Method: 该研究系统性地评估了将三种类型的上下文信息融入零样本（zero-shot）提示词对大型语言模型（LLM）立场检测的影响：1. 现实世界特征（如用户简介）；2. 衍生特征（如政党归属）；3. LLM生成特征（如目标描述）。研究涵盖了四个基准数据集，并引入了一个新的高质量德语推特立场检测数据集，通过对比实验评估了不同上下文组合对模型性能的差异。

Result: 实验发现，并非所有上下文都有益：LLM生成的“目标描述”能稳定提升准确率；而用户元数据的影响不稳定，甚至可能产生负面效果；特别是将同一用户的其他推文作为上下文（在有监督学习中通常有效），在零样本环境下反而因引入噪声而损害了性能。定性分析显示，LLM在区分任务相关信息与无关干扰信息方面存在局限性。

Conclusion: 在社交媒体立场检测任务中，上下文信息的融入并非总是有效的，甚至可能因引入噪声而损害模型性能。研究强调了LLM在筛选任务相关信息能力上的不足，提示未来在构建零样本提示词时，应更审慎地选择上下文，重点利用LLM生成的精准目标描述。

Abstract: Stance detection on social media is challenging due to short, noisy, and context-dependent language. While large language models (LLMs) show zero-shot generalization, they are typically prompted without contextual information, which limits their ability to interpret ambiguous posts. In this work, we systematically investigate the impact of incorporating real-world (e.g., user biographies), derived (e.g., political party), and LLM-generated (e.g., target descriptions) contextual features into zero-shot prompting for stance detection on Twitter. Our evaluation spans four benchmark datasets, including a new high-quality German Twitter stance dataset. Across multiple LLMs, we find that integrating contextual information improves performance, but only under specific conditions. LLM-generated target descriptions consistently enhance accuracy, while other user metadata has mixed or even detrimental effects. Notably, we show that the inclusion of other tweets by the same user, often beneficial in supervised learning, can impair performance due to input noise. Our qualitative analysis reveals that LLMs struggle to distinguish task-specific useful information from irrelevant context. Our findings highlight both the promise and challenges of prompting with context information in noisy real-world settings. We publish code and data at this \href{https://github.com/tilmanbeck/stance-context-twitter}{page}.

### [25] [EGTR-Review: Efficient Evidence-Grounded Scientific Peer Review Generation via Multi-Agent Teacher Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06025)
*Xinpeng Qiu,Wang Yihu,Zhifeng Liu,Xiaochen Wang,Jimin Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型的评审生成方法存在评论空泛、缺乏证据支持、不可追溯以及复杂多智能体系统推理成本过高等问题。

Method: 提出了 EGTR-Review 框架：1. 构建包含论文分解、关键要素提取、外部证据检索、验证推理与评审合成的多智能体教师系统；2. 采用任务前缀驱动的多任务学习，将教师的推理路径与最终评审结果蒸馏至轻量级学生模型；3. 使用证据加权目标函数（Evidence-weighted objective）来优化模型，减少噪声数据的干扰。

Result: 在公开评审数据集上的实验结果表明，EGTR-Review的学生模型在自动评价指标、LLM-as-Judge评价及人工评价中均优于现有的提示工程、微调及结构化/智能体基线模型，并显著降低了推理成本。

Conclusion: EGTR-Review 通过多智能体教师蒸馏，成功在保持高效推理的同时，提升了同行评审生成的实证性与可追溯性，为解决大模型评审生成的质量与效率平衡问题提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Scientific peer review generation has attracted increasing attention for reducing reviewing burdens and providing timely feedback. However, existing Large Language Model (LLM)-based methods often produce generic comments with insufficient evidence support and weak source traceability, while complex multi-agent systems incur high inference costs. To address these challenges, we propose EGTR-Review, an Evidence-Grounded and Traceable Review Generation framework via Multi-Agent Teacher Distillation. EGTR-Review first constructs a multi-agent teacher that performs structure-aware paper decomposition, key-element extraction, external scholarly evidence retrieval, evidence-state labeling, verification reasoning, and review synthesis. It then distills both intermediate reasoning trajectories and final review comments into a lightweight student model through task-prefix-driven multi-task learning. An evidence-weighted objective further reduces the influence of weak, missing, or non-verifiable supervision. Experiments on public peer-review datasets show that EGTR-Review (Student) outperforms strong prompt-based, fine-tuned, and structured/agentic baselines across automatic metrics, LLM-as-Judge evaluation, and human evaluation, while maintaining strong factual grounding and source traceability with substantially lower token consumption and inference time. Our code, prompts, configurations, and sample data are available on GitHub.

### [26] [NAVIRA: Decoupled Stochastic Remasking for Masked Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06031)
*Andrey Fomenko,Maksim Kryzhanovskiy,Svetlana Glazyrina,Roman Ischenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: NAVIRA提出了一种改进掩码扩散语言模型推理的解码策略，通过将“评估质量”与“重生成”步骤解耦并引入随机重掩码，有效解决了生成过程中的上下文污染问题，实现了流畅度与多样性的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的掩码扩散语言模型在并行生成过程中存在“上下文污染”问题：同一步骤生成的令牌基于边缘分布预测，早期局部依赖错误会累积并干扰后续生成。虽然PRISM试图通过评分机制解决，但其检测与生成步骤耦合，导致错误令牌仍参与后续推理。因此，需要一种能够更有效清理上下文并优化推理路径的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为NAVIRA的推理时间解码策略。其核心创新在于：1. 解耦机制：将令牌质量评估（检测）与令牌重生成过程分为两个独立的网络前向传播步骤，避免错误令牌污染上下文；2. 随机调度：引入温度控制的随机重掩码策略，平衡流畅度与多样性，避免重复修正相同位置。

Result: 在170M参数的掩码扩散模型上的实验表明：与传统解码策略相比，NAVIRA的解耦机制显著提升了生成文本的流畅度；通过引入随机调度，模型在保持文本熵（多样性）的同时，在LLM-judge评估中获得了更高的分数，证明了该方法在较大推理预算下更具优势。

Conclusion: NAVIRA证明了在掩码扩散语言模型中，推理时的重掩码策略（而非仅仅是模型学习到的质量分数）对于提升生成质量至关重要。通过解耦检测与生成过程，并引入随机性调度，可以有效解决上下文污染问题，从而在保持多样性的同时显著提升生成文本的流畅度。

Abstract: Masked diffusion language models generate text by iteratively unmasking many tokens in parallel, but this speed comes with a correction problem: tokens generated in the same step are predicted from marginal distributions, and early local dependency errors can later contaminate the context. PRISM addresses this by learning token-level quality scores and remasking unreliable tokens, but its inference rule is coupled: the same forward pass both detects low-quality tokens and computes logits for their replacements, so the erroneous tokens still condition regeneration. We propose NAVIRA, an inference-time decoding policy that separates these two operations and samples remasking positions stochastically. A first forward pass scores tokens; selected tokens are masked; a second forward pass regenerates from the cleaned context. Temperature-controlled remasking reduces repeated correction of the same positions and balances fluency against diversity. In controlled experiments with a 170M masked diffusion language model, decoupling improves fluency, while scheduled stochastic remasking preserves entropy and achieves stronger LLM-judge scores under larger forward-pass budgets. These results show that remasking policy, not only the learned quality signal, is central to reliable masked-diffusion text generation.

</details>

Abstract: We study English-to-Prakrit machine translation in a low-resource setting where the target language is unsupported by IndicTrans2. Using a 1,474-pair Maharashtri Prakrit parallel corpus and evaluation on a 20-sample Ardhamagadhi test set, we report corpus BLEU improvements over an untuned baseline. The results indicate that script-compatible language routing can enable feasible transfer to unsupported classical languages, while highlighting limitations due to data scarcity and dialect mismatch. Our code and trained models are released to the public for further exploration https://github.com/D3v1s0m/indictrans2-prakrit-mt.

### [28] [IA-RAG: Interval-Algebra-Driven Temporal Reasoning for Dynamic Knowledge Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06044)
*Xiaoman Wang,Yaoze Zhang,Wenzhuo Fan,Hongwei Zhang,Ding Wang,Guohang Yan,Song Mao,Botian Shi,Yunshi Lan,Pinlong Cai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: IA-RAG是一种层次化时间检索增强生成框架，通过将知识建模为时间区间并结合区间代数进行推理和检索，突破了传统RAG难以处理复杂时间结构和关系推理的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的RAG及Graph RAG框架通常将知识视为静态，或仅使用粗粒度的时间戳，难以捕捉和推理现实中复杂的时间结构（如持续、重叠、包含等），导致在处理时间敏感的问答任务时表现受限。

Method: 提出了IA-RAG框架：1. 将事实表示为区间事件单元（IEU）；2. 构建层次化的“主题森林”（Thematic Forest），利用Allen区间代数管理时间依赖；3. 引入子图时间收紧（Sub-graph Time Tightening）机制，处理模糊或不完整的时间边界；4. 实现基于区间代数引导的隐式时间语义检索。

Result: 在TimeQA、TempReason和ComplexTR等多个时间问答基准测试中，IA-RAG表现优异，特别是在需要组合式时间推理的任务中，相比现有方法具有显著的性能提升。

Conclusion: IA-RAG通过将知识建模为时间区间并利用Allen区间代数进行推理，有效解决了RAG在处理复杂时间结构（如持续时间、重叠和包含关系）时的局限性，为处理时间敏感的问答任务提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has shown strong effectiveness in grounding Large Language Models (LLMs) with external knowledge. However, existing RAG and Graph RAG frameworks largely treat knowledge as static or associate time with coarse-grained timestamps or metadata, failing to capture rich temporal structures such as duration, overlap, and containment. We propose IA-RAG, a hierarchical temporal RAG framework that models knowledge as time intervals and performs retrieval under formal temporal constraints. IA-RAG represents facts as Interval Event Units (IEUs) and organizes them into a hierarchical Thematic Forest, where temporal dependencies are governed by Allen's Interval Algebra. To handle incomplete or uncertain temporal boundaries, IA-RAG further introduces a Sub-graph Time Tightening mechanism that refines fuzzy intervals through logical constraints within connected event subgraphs. In addition, IA-RAG supports implicit temporal semantic retrieval through interval-algebra-guided traversal. Experiments on multiple temporal question answering benchmarks, including TimeQA, TempReason, and ComplexTR, demonstrate that IA-RAG achieves strong temporal retrieval and reasoning performance, particularly on complex compositional temporal reasoning tasks. Our code is released at https://github.com/xiaoAugenstern/LogicalRAG_TemporalQA.

### [29] [Automatic Labelling of Speech Translation Errors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06047)
*Dominik Macháček,Maike Züfle,Ondrej Klejch*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了语音翻译错误标注（STEL）框架，旨在解决ST系统缺乏质量评估标准的问题。研究发现现有模型在识别错误方面的能力尚不及人类，但多模态方法与纯文本分析在错误分类上具有互补价值。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语音翻译（ST）系统缺乏统一的错误评估与置信度量化标准，翻译错误会严重损害系统可信度并带来负面后果，因此亟需建立一套标准的评估方法体系。

Result: 1. 现有模型（XCOMET及Qwen2.5-Omni）在STEL任务中的精度约为人类的一半；2. 验证了直接处理语音信号对执行STEL任务至关重要；3. 发现纯文本模型与多模态/语音处理系统在区分“翻译错误”与“语音处理错误”方面表现出明显的互补性。

Abstract: Errors in speech translations reduce trustworthiness of Speech Translation (ST) systems and can have serious consequences. Yet currently there is no established methodology for evaluating confidence and quality estimation of speech translations. To initiate progress in this direction, we propose Speech Translation Error Labelling (STEL). We create an annotation protocol, a small authentic end-to-end evaluation dataset, and we analyse how existing text-only and speech-processing systems perform the STEL task. Our results show that text-only XCOMET and multimodal LLM Qwen2.5-Omni are able to perform the STEL task in roughly half the precision of humans. We also find that direct speech processing is necessary for the STEL task, and that the current text-only and speech-processing systems are complementary in labelling translation-only vs. speech-processing errors in ST.

### [30] [Multi-task Learning is Not Enough: Representational Entanglement in Dual-output Second Language Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06065)
*Seung Hwan Cho,Young-Min Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了第二语言语音识别中多任务学习的局限性，发现其在提升意义理解的同时可能损害表面转录，根本原因在于编码器层面的表征纠缠，并为此类系统的优化提出了改进方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然多任务学习通常被认为是提升第二语言语音识别性能的有效途径，但研究发现该方法在不同语言（韩语与英语）上的表现并不一致，有时甚至会导致表面转录质量的下降。因此，作者旨在探究这种性能退化的根本原因。

Method: 研究人员通过对比韩语和英语在L2语音识别中的表现，分析了多任务学习（MTL）对意义理解和表面转录的影响。通过测量莱文斯坦编辑距离来量化表面与意义的差异，并深入分析了编码器层面的表征纠缠以及解码器的任务适配机制。

Result: 实验表明，多任务学习能显著改善意义识别，但会损害表面转录效果，且这种损害程度与表面与意义之间的分歧程度相关。分析发现，英语任务在编码器中产生了高度纠缠的表征，限制了解码器的灵活性，而韩语则保持了较好的任务独立性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了在第二语言（L2）语音识别的多任务学习中，编码器层面的任务纠缠是导致表面转录性能下降的关键因素。未来的研究应致力于通过解耦编码器表征来优化多任务学习框架，以平衡意义理解与表面转录的精度。

Abstract: Second-language (L2) speech recognition often requires transcriptions of pronunciations and intended meanings. Multi-task learning (MTL) is a natural approach because it assumes that shared representations benefit both outputs. However, this paper shows that this assumption does not hold across Korean and English. MTL improves meaning but degrades surface transcription, especially in English, where the degradation scales with surface-meaning divergence measured by Levenshtein edit distance.Encoder analysis links these patterns to encoder-level entanglement, with Korean preserving distinct task representations while English produces nearly identical ones. Cross-task decoder analysis shows that the meaning dual-output decoder adapts with a unique representation, while the surface dual-output decoder remains constrained by the encoder. These findings motivate the design of MTL frameworks that mitigate encoder-level entanglement to reduce surface degradation in dual-output L2 automatic speech recognition.

### [31] [LatentSkill: From In-Context Textual Skills to In-Weight Latent Skills for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06087)
*Aofan Yu,Chenyu Zhou,Tianyi Xu,Zihan Guo,Rong Shan,Zhihui Fu,Jun Wang,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang,Jianghao Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LatentSkill通过超网络将文本技能转化为LoRA权重，有效解决了大语言模型智能体在使用文本技能时面临的上下文过载和隐私暴露问题，在显著降低计算开销的同时提升了任务执行性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型智能体系统中，将可重用的任务过程编码为文本技能是一种常见做法。然而，这种方式存在两个主要问题：一是频繁将技能注入提示词会消耗大量上下文资源（context overhead），二是直接以明文形式暴露技能内容存在安全隐患。因此，研究者旨在探索一种能够将技能知识有效存储在权重空间的方法，以解决上下文压力并增强模块化特性。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为LatentSkill的框架。该框架利用一个预训练的超网络（hypernetwork），将文本形式的任务技能直接转化为即插即用的LoRA适配器。通过这种方式，技能知识被存储在权重空间而非上下文空间中，从而在执行任务时无需在提示词中注入大量文本，同时保持了技能的模块化加载、缩放和组合特性。

Result: 在ALFWorld和Search-QA基准测试中，LatentSkill表现优于传统的上下文技能基线。在ALFWorld中，该方法在已知和未知任务集上的成功率分别提高了21.4和13.4个百分点，同时减少了64.1%的预填充（prefill）token；在Search-QA中，精确匹配率提高了3.0个百分点，技能token开销降低了72.2%。此外，生成的LoRA权重展现出结构化的语义几何特性，支持通过缩放系数进行精确控制及参数空间算术组合。

Conclusion: LatentSkill证明了通过将文本技能转化为权重空间的LoRA适配器，可以在提升智能体任务性能的同时，显著降低提示词的上下文开销。这种方法不仅增强了技能的模块化和组合能力，还提高了知识的安全性，是扩展大语言模型智能体能力的高效范式。

Abstract: Agent systems increasingly use textual skills to encode reusable task procedures, but injecting these skills into the prompt at every step incurs substantial context overhead and exposes skill content as plaintext. We present LatentSkill, a framework that converts textual skills into plug-and-play LoRA adapters through a pretrained hypernetwork. LatentSkill stores skill knowledge in weight space rather than context space, removing per-step skill tokens while preserving modular loading, scaling, and composition. On ALFWorld and Search-QA, LatentSkill outperforms the corresponding in-context skill baseline while using substantially fewer prefill tokens: it improves ALFWorld success by 21.4 and 13.4 points on the seen and unseen splits with 64.1% fewer prefill tokens, and improves Search-QA exact match by 3.0 points with 72.2% lower skill-token overhead. Further analysis shows that generated skill LoRAs form a structured semantic geometry, can be precisely controlled via the LoRA scaling coefficient, and can be composed through parameter-space arithmetic when skill components are aligned. These findings suggest that weight-space skills provide an efficient, modular, and less exposed substrate for extending LLM agents.

</details>

*Michal Tichý,Jindřich Libovický*

TL;DR: 研究者推出了CHALIS数据集，专门用于测试语言识别系统在亲缘语言辨别及正字法噪声（如俚语、转写）处理上的能力，揭示了当前主流系统在这些复杂场景下的局限性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了包含亲缘语言（如捷克语/斯洛伐克语、西班牙语/加泰罗尼亚语等）及正字法噪声（包括跨脚本转写、去变音符号、同形异义词攻击和网络俚语）的CHALIS数据集，并利用该基准对四种主流语言识别系统进行了评估。

Result: 实验证明所有被测系统在处理亲缘语言（尤其是低资源语言对）和转写文本时性能大幅下降，验证了CHALIS数据集作为挑战性测试基准的有效性。

Conclusion: 现有的主流语言识别系统在处理亲缘语言和复杂噪声文本时表现不佳，该研究提出的CHALIS数据集为评估和提升语言识别系统的鲁棒性提供了重要基准。

Abstract: We present CHALIS (Challenging Language Identification Samples), a new benchmark dataset explicitly designed to address difficult cases in language identification: cousin languages and orthographic noise. Our dataset has two parts: First, we collected sentences shared across mutually intelligible language pairs (Czech/Slovak, Spanish/Catalan, Portuguese/Galician, Danish/Norwegian). The second part tests for orthography noise: we transliterate text across multiple scripts, remove diacritics, simulate homoglyph attacks, and use Internet slang. We evaluate four widely used language identification systems on CHALIS and demonstrate that all struggle substantially in these scenarios, especially on lower-resource languages within cousin pairs and on transliterated input. The resource is publicly available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/michal-tichy/CHALIS.

### [33] [Ouvia: A User-centered Framework for Measuring Usability of Speech Translation in Real-World Communication Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06177)
*Giuseppe Attanasio,Beatrice Savoldi,Daniel Chechelnitsky,Matteo Negri,Marine Carpuat,Maarten Sap,André F. T. Martins*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了Ouvia评估框架，通过真实场景下的交互测试揭示了现代语音翻译技术在用户可用性上的局限性和公平性问题，并验证了基于QA的评估方法优于传统质量指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语音翻译评估主要依赖脱离语境的测试基准和整体质量指标，忽略了终端用户的实际沟通需求和不同群体间的用户体验差异。

Method: 提出了“Ouvia”评估框架，通过自定义网络应用和多阶段研究设计，模拟真实世界中的一对一沟通场景。研究涵盖了医疗和日常情境，涉及4个语音翻译系统、3种英语方言和2种性别，收集了超过1,750次人机交互数据，并将基于问答（QA）的评估与传统评估指标进行了比较。

Result: 研究发现，现代语音翻译系统的实际可用性有限，仅约一半的交互被用户评价为“可用”，且不同人口统计学群体之间存在显著的可用性差距。此外，基于QA的评估指标比标准自动评估指标（如BLEU）更能准确预测真实场景下的可用性。

Conclusion: 传统的整体式质量评估指标无法充分反映语音翻译在真实场景中的可用性。研究强调，必须建立以用户为中心、基于真实沟通情境的评估框架，并重点关注不同人口统计学群体之间的技术公平性。

Abstract: Speech translation (ST) is increasingly adopted in user applications, yet its evaluation largely focuses on decontextualized testbeds and holistic quality, rather than end users' communication needs. We introduce Ouvia, an evaluation framework for measuring user-perceived usability of speech translation outputs in real-world settings. Ouvia focuses on one-to-one communication: an English speaker needs to convey a request to a Portuguese speaker, and the message is automatically translated. Through a custom web app and multi-phase study design, we collect more than 1,750 such interactions in healthcare and everyday situations, mediated by four ST systems, involving speakers from three English dialects and two genders. We find that modern ST serves people only to a limited extent -- only around half of interactions are rated as usable -- with significant gaps in reported usability across demographic groups. Moreover, among quality metrics, we find that QA-based evaluation is a substantially stronger predictor of real-world usability than standard approaches. Together, these findings stress the importance of situated, user-centered evaluation frameworks that go beyond holistic quality scores and attend to who the technology serves -- and how well.

Abstract: Question answering (QA) systems have achieved notable progress with the advent of large language models (LLMs). Existing approaches often struggle with contextual understanding, answer consistency, and generalization across diverse domains. The motivation behind this research lies in addressing the limitations of current QA systems, particularly their tendency to produce irrelevant or imprecise responses despite having access to the correct context. Our methodology involves fine-tuning a pre-trained LLM on a benchmark QA dataset to improve its contextual comprehension and answer extraction capabilities. Specifically, we utilize the Stanford Question Answering Dataset (SQuAD1.1), which provides high-quality context-question-answer triplets for supervised training and evaluation. Experimental results show that the fine-tuned Roberta-base model achieves the highest performance, attaining a ROUGE-L score of 86.84%, a BLEU score of 28.24%, and a BERTScore of 95.38%. These results indicate strong accuracy and answer relevance, demonstrating the effectiveness of the proposed approach for context-based question answering tasks. Furthermore, the findings confirm that targeted fine-tuning substantially improves the reliability and precision of QA systems.

Abstract: Institutional documents contain substantial amounts of operational and analytical information embedded within figures and tables. In this work, we introduce a benchmark dataset and evaluation framework for \textit{data snapshot extraction}, the task of identifying and localizing semantically meaningful visual artifacts within institutional documents. The benchmark spans humanitarian reports, World Bank policy research working papers, and project appraisal documents, and includes annotations for figures and tables that contain reusable analytical information. Using this dataset, we benchmarked multiple open-source layout detection models and evaluated both detection performance and spatial extraction quality. Our results show that current models struggle to generalize to operational institutional documents despite strong performance on conventional academic benchmarks. Common failure modes include confusion between analytical and non-analytical content, fragmentation of composite analytical artifacts, and incomplete extraction of contextual information required for interpretation. These findings highlight a persistent gap between generic document layout analysis and operationally useful data snapshot extraction. We release the source PDFs, annotation dataset, metadata, and source code to support future research in operational document intelligence. ### [36] [From Self to Other: Evaluating Demographic Perspective-Taking in LLM Hate Speech Annotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06266)
*Paloma Piot,Javier Parapar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究评估了利用大模型（LLM）模拟不同人群对仇恨言论感知的有效性，发现简单的人格化提示无法完全复刻人类的社会判断分歧，但通过特定的“替代提示”策略，Llama 3.1 在模拟人类感知差异方面表现出了一定的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仇恨言论检测具有高度的主观性，不同背景的人对同一内容的感知存在差异。由于大规模收集多样化群体的标注数据成本高昂且困难，研究旨在探讨利用“人格化”（Persona-conditioned）大模型模拟不同群体视角的可行性，以及这些模型是否能够真实反映人类的认知分歧。

Method: 研究通过评估三种人类社会判断维度来考察大模型（LLM）模拟不同人口群体观点的能力：(1) 群体间分歧（inter-group disagreement）；(2) 群体内敏感度（in-group sensitivity）；(3) 替代预测（vicarious prediction，即预测其他群体的反应）。研究对比了不同模型在这些维度上的表现，并探讨了身份提示（persona prompting）与替代提示对模型输出的影响。

Result: 研究发现，没有单一模型能够稳定地覆盖上述所有三个维度。模型表现高度依赖于特定模型架构，仅凭简单的身份提示无法可靠地产生符合人类认知的多样化观点。不过，使用 Llama 3.1 配合“替代提示”（vicarious prompting）策略，在多数人口统计维度上展现出最高的一致性，是目前模拟人类意见分歧模式的最有效配置。

Conclusion: 目前的模型无法仅通过简单的身份提示（persona prompting）稳定地模拟人类在仇恨言论感知上的多样性与社会偏见。虽然 Llama 3.1 在“替代预测”（vicarious prompting）配置下表现最佳，最接近人类的意见分歧模式，但研究强调了在利用大模型进行自动化标注时，需要对模型配置进行谨慎的选择和验证，不能简单地依赖身份标签。

Abstract: Hate speech detection is inherently subjective: people from different demographic groups perceive the same content very differently. Collecting enough annotations from multiple demographic groups is costly and difficult to scale. Persona-conditioned Large Language Models (models prompted to adopt a specific demographic identity) have been proposed as a way to simulate diverse perspectives at scale. But do they actually reflect how different groups disagree? We evaluate three aspects of human social judgement: (i) whether personas from different groups disagree in human-like ways (inter-group disagreement), (ii) whether they become more sensitive when content targets their own identity (in-group sensitivity), and (iii) whether they can accurately predict how another group would react (vicarious prediction). Our results show that no model consistently captures all three dimensions, and performance is highly model-dependent and does not emerge reliably from minimal identity prompts alone. However, vicarious prompting with Llama 3.1 yields the highest cross-group agreement in most demographic axes and provides the closest overall approximation to human disagreement patterns, indicating that this configuration may provide a more reliable setting for automatic annotation aligned with human judgements.

### [37] [FOXGLOVE: Understanding Goal-Oriented and Anchored Writing Feedback from Experts and LLMs on Argumentative Essays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06271)
*Yijun Liu,Yifan Song,John Gallagher,Sarah Sterman,Tal August*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究发布了FOXGLOVE数据集，系统对比了专家导师与大语言模型在写作反馈上的差异，发现模型反馈质量虽高但存在长度偏差，且在交互策略上与人类导师有所不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然大语言模型（LLM）被广泛用于提供写作反馈，但目前缺乏关于模型与人类专家在写作修订核心维度（如目标导向、锚定具体句子、优先级排序）上的系统性对比分析。为了弥补这一空白，本研究旨在通过实证研究探究两者的异同。

Method: 构建了FOXGLOVE数据集，包含696条人类导师反馈与1644条由四个前沿大模型生成的反馈。研究者通过专家评分评估了反馈的质量，并从目标导向、锚定位置、反馈优先级以及语言复杂度等多个维度，对人类反馈与模型反馈进行了系统性的量化对比分析。

Result: 研究发现：1. 导师和模型在反馈的目标分布和论文位置分布上高度相似；2. 双方在具体的锚定句子选择上存在差异；3. 模型生成的反馈通常比导师更复杂，且较少使用提问式引导；4. 在专家评分中，模型反馈在多数质量维度上得分更高，但这种优势主要是由于模型反馈的篇幅更长。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，尽管大语言模型在反馈质量评价上表现优异，但这种优势很大程度上源于反馈长度。通过FOXGLOVE数据集，研究揭示了AI与人类导师在反馈策略上的异同，为未来优化AI辅助写作教育提供了数据基础。

Abstract: While large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate writing feedback, there remains no systematic comparison of LLM and expert feedback on the dimensions that writing research identifies as central to revision: goal-orientation, anchoring to specific sentences, and prioritization. We introduce FOXGLOVE, a dataset of 696 feedback comments written by trained writing instructors on 69 twelfth-grade argumentative essays, paired with 1,644 comments generated from four frontier LLMs under a shared protocol, totaling 2,340 comments. We provide expert quality ratings on a subset of both instructor and LLM comments. We find that instructors and LLMs distribute feedback similarly across goals and essay positions, yet instructors and models diverge on the specific sentences on which to provide feedback. Additionally, we find that models tend to write more complex feedback and use fewer questions than instructors. LLM feedback also receives higher ratings on most dimensions of quality, as rated by instructors, but much of this advantage appears to be attributable to lengthier comments. FOXGLOVE enables systematic comparison of where human and LLM feedback align, diverge, and differ.
