### [77] [Harnessing Structural Context for Entity Alignment Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06109)
*Xingyu Chen,Yuanning Cui,Zequn Sun,Wei Hu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ContextEA 是一个增强的实体对齐基础模型框架，通过引入跨图交互编码和多层次结构校准解码，有效解决了现有模型结构信息利用不足的问题，显著提升了模型在未见知识图谱上的迁移对齐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的实体对齐（EA）基础模型在处理不同知识图谱对时，存在两个主要缺陷：一是编码阶段跨图交互较弱，二是最终的候选排序过度依赖粗糙的相似度，未能充分利用结构上下文信息。

Method: 本文提出了 ContextEA，一个增强的编码器-解码器框架：
1. 编码器端：引入跨图交互编码器（Cross-KG Interaction Encoder），通过锚点桥梁（Anchor Bridges）统一两个知识图谱，并进行早期的关系感知跨图传播。
2. 解码器端：引入结构校准解码器（Structural Calibration Decoder），利用实体级、邻域级、关系级和锚点感知的结构证据对对齐分数进行校准。

Result: 在 OpenEA、SRPRS 和 DBP 三个基准组的 29 个数据集上的实验表明，ContextEA 在所有指标上均超越了强基准模型。特别是在未进行微调的情况下，预训练的 ContextEA 即已超越了经过微调的基准模型，展示了其强大的迁移能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 ContextEA 框架通过显式地利用结构上下文，显著提升了实体对齐基础模型的迁移能力。实验结果验证了在编码器阶段增强跨图交互，并在解码器阶段引入多层次结构校准对于提升对齐性能的有效性，为构建更通用的实体对齐基础模型提供了重要方向。

Abstract: Entity alignment (EA) aims to identify equivalent entities across heterogeneous knowledge graphs (KGs) and is a key component of knowledge fusion and cross-KG reasoning. The recent EA foundation model demonstrates that alignment knowledge, once pretrained, can be directly applied to diverse previously unseen KG pairs. However, it still underuses structural context in two places: cross-KG interaction is weak during encoding, and final candidate ranking still relies too heavily on coarse similarity. We address these limitations with ContextEA, an enhanced encoder-decoder framework for transferable EA. On the encoder side, we introduce a cross-KG interaction encoder that unifies the two KGs with anchor bridges and performs earlier relation-aware cross-graph propagation. On the decoder side, we introduce a structural calibration decoder that calibrates alignment scores with entity-level, neighborhood-level, relation-level, and anchor-aware structural evidence. This design strengthens both structural context construction and structural context exploitation while remaining lightweight. Experiments on 29 EA datasets in OpenEA, SRPRS, and DBP show consistent gains over strong transferable baselines. Notably, the pretrained ContextEA already surpasses the finetuned baselines on all three benchmark groups, demonstrating substantially stronger transfer to unseen KGs. These results suggest that explicitly harnessing structural context is an effective direction for improving EA foundation models.

</details>


### [78] [Dense Contexts Are Hard Contexts: Lexical Density Limits Effective Context in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06203)
*Giovanni Dettori,Matteo Boffa,Danilo Giordano,Idilio Drago,Marco Mellia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出大语言模型处理长文本的能力不仅受长度和位置影响，还深受“词汇密度”制约。研究证明，在相同长度下，高密度信息会导致模型检索能力大幅衰减，揭示了词汇密度是评估模型长文本处理效能的关键未被关注指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前学术界普遍认为输入长度和关键信息位置是导致大语言模型（LLM）长文本性能下降的主要原因。本文旨在探讨“词汇密度”（即上下文中引入独特信息的频率）这一被长期忽视的因素，是否也是限制模型有效上下文窗口的关键变量。

Method: 作者利用三种“大海捞针”（find-the-needle）风格的基准测试，在保持输入总长度（约12k token）和目标信息位置不变的前提下，系统地增加上下文中无关干扰信息的密度。通过对比不同密度水平下9B至685B参数规模模型的检索表现，并对任务类型进行控制变量分析，量化了词汇密度对性能的具体影响。

Result: 研究发现词汇密度与模型性能呈强负相关：在处理高密度文本时，模型检索性能出现急剧崩溃，即便在总长度一致的情况下，从稀疏上下文到密集上下文，检索得分可从近乎完美降至60%以下。通过降低密度，模型性能可得到有效恢复，证实了有效上下文容量本质上是词汇密度的函数。

Conclusion: 词汇密度是决定大模型长文本处理能力的第三个核心关键维度。现有的评估往往忽视了信息密度对模型性能的制约，未来在构建长文本任务及优化模型架构时，必须将词汇密度作为一个独立且重要的变量进行考量，以提升模型在处理信息密集型真实任务时的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Input length and the position of relevant information are widely cited as the primary causes of degraded LLM long-context performance. Here, we study lexical density -- the rate at which a context introduces distinct information -- as a third, largely overlooked factor that systematically reduces the effective context window of LLMs. We quantify the impact of lexical density on open-weight LLMs (9B-685B) using three "find-the-needle" style benchmarks with identical length (~12k tokens) and controlled needle position, but increasing density of information. We observe a sharp performance collapse in higher-density benchmarks: models that are near-perfect in sparse contexts drop below 60% retrieval score on denser ones. To rule out task-type confounds, we vary and control the density within each benchmark while keeping all other properties unchanged. Reducing density generally restores performance, especially in the high-density regimes where degradation appears. These results show that effective context capacity is a function of lexical density, with direct implications for real-world LLM systems operating on compact, information-rich inputs.

</details>

### [79] [The Evaluation Blind Spot: A Stereological Theory of Benchmark Coverage for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05169)
*Jason Z Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过立体学理论揭示了LLM基准测试体系中存在严重的结构性盲点和高额冗余，证明了现有排行榜上的模型排名极不稳定，并提出了一套基于子模优化的高效基准测试评估策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前LLM基准测试体系缺乏严谨的理论支撑，导致评估结果存在较大的结构性不确定性和冗余；作者旨在定量分析基准测试的覆盖能力，揭示评分背后的能力空间盲点，并提供更优的评估选择策略。

Method: 利用立体学（Stereological）理论建模基准测试覆盖率，引入有效维度（d_eff）分析，结合卡方投影模型进行模拟；采用子模贪婪算法（Nemhauser 1-1/e保证）筛选基准测试子集；基于最优恢复理论，在数学上解决了Gardner 1.5问题。

Result: 发现LLM排行榜的有效维度极低（d_eff在2.86至4.80之间）；结构性盲点比现有排名差距大两个数量级；评估体系极其不稳定（模型排名在不同测试集下极易发生反转）；提出了一个仅需4个基准测试即可构成的核心评估集，并验证了其跨时期的稳健性。

Conclusion: 现有大语言模型（LLM）基准测试存在结构性盲点，其规模远超统计噪声；通过子模贪婪算法可识别出核心基准集，实现高效的性能覆盖与评估冗余度管理。该研究揭示了基准测试维度的局限性，并为优化评估体系提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We give a stereological theory of LLM benchmark coverage. For any suite with effective dimensionality d_eff, the visible Hausdorff distance between two convex capability profiles consistent with the same scores is bounded by epsilon + C R m^(-1/(d_eff-1)), with matching Lipschitz lower bound. Empirically, three independent leaderboards (Open LLM v2, an extended 12-benchmark suite, LiveBench) all have d_eff in [2.86, 4.80] on their competitive frontier; the structural blind spot exceeds the observed runner-up score gap by two orders of magnitude and dominates statistical noise by 52-127x. Under a chi-squared projection model, the isotropic prior is the optimistic case; across six hidden-capability priors and four ambient dimensions the simulated half-split swap rate of the top two models stays in [0.38, 0.49], and a 500-trial random visible/held-out split shows that 92% of trials swap the top-1 ranking with on average 2.83 of 5 top-5 models changing. A submodular greedy algorithm with the Nemhauser (1 - 1/e) guarantee finds a stable core of 4 benchmarks; 7 of 12 suffice for 90% coverage, and the trained subset transfers across temporal quarters with 93-97% retention. A counterfactual validation across 12 internal benchmarks and 27 Chatbot Arena categories confirms that the eigenstructure predicts which evaluations are irreplaceable (rho = -0.69, p = 0.013 for removal disruption) and which external evaluations bring new information (rho = +0.38). As a second, independent theoretical contribution, we resolve Gardner's Problem 1.5 (1995) for C^2 support functions, establishing the minimax rate Theta(R/(kappa m^(2/(D-1)))) in general dimension via optimal recovery theory on S^(D-1).

</details>


### [80] [State commitment learning: training language models to distinguish computation from memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05201)
*Fei Ding,Yongkang Zhang,Runhao Liu,Yuhao Liao,Zijian Zeng,Huiming Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决大模型推理过程中的思维干扰问题，该论文提出了“状态承诺学习”，通过一种新的强化学习方法（CERL）强制模型区分必要结论与临时草稿，显著提升了模型推理的稳定性和可控性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的推理语言模型无法区分用于计算的临时标记（思维过程）与构成持久状态的标记（最终结论），导致后续的推理过程容易受到之前失败尝试、无效思路或私有草稿的影响，从而降低了输出的稳健性。

Method: 提出了一种名为“状态承诺学习（State Commitment Learning）”的训练目标；定义了“持久状态充分性（Persistent-state Sufficiency）”这一反事实准则；开发了“反事实擦除强化学习（CERL）”算法，通过对比保留思维路径与擦除思维路径后的推理结果，仅在擦除路径仍能得到正确结果时给予奖励。

Result: 在数学、长链逻辑、科学问答和多轮工具使用等多个任务中，CERL显著降低了答案对隐式思维过程的依赖，且在不牺牲准确率的前提下，表现优于仅关注正确率的强化学习方法（Correctness-only RL）和长答案监督微调（SFT）基线。

Conclusion: 该研究证明通过明确区分“持久状态”与“临时计算”，可以有效提升推理模型生成的稳健性，减少推理过程对错误思维路径的依赖，从而在保持高精度的同时提高了模型输出的可靠性。

Abstract: Reasoning language models do not distinguish tokens used for computation from tokens that constitute persistent state: once generated, all hidden thoughts remain in context and influence future predictions. As a result, downstream reasoning may depend on failed attempts, dead ends, and private scratch work that should not be safely relied on later. We recast this phenomenon as a new training objective, state commitment learning: training models to explicitly distinguish information that should be committed as persistent state from temporary computation that can be discarded. We define a counterfactual criterion, persistent-state sufficiency, which makes it trainable and measurable whether an answer remains usable after hidden thoughts are erased. We then propose Counterfactual Erasure RL (CERL), which evaluates, under the same prefix, both a path that keeps hidden thoughts and a path that erases them, and gives reward only when the erasure path remains correct. We also introduce the Erasure Dependence Protocol and show across mathematics, long-chain logic, scientific QA, and multi-turn tool-use evaluation that CERL substantially reduces answer dependence on hidden thoughts without sacrificing accuracy, consistently outperforming correctness-only RL and long-answer SFT baselines.

</details>


### [81] [Trust, but Don't Verify: Epistemic Blind Spots in LLM Source Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05403)
*Rohan N. Pradhan,Steve Goley*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了语言模型在综合信息时存在严重认知偏差：模型容易被“专业的语气”欺骗，导致其无法分辨统计数据的真伪，即便模型本身具备辨别能力，但在实际应用中却更倾向于信任风格化的表述而非客观逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究大型语言模型在作为“认识论代理”综合多源信息时，是真正具备评估证据质量的能力，还是仅仅根据表层展示（surface presentation）进行简单聚合，从而理解模型为何在面对虚假统计数据时失效。

Method: 研究人员采用了多种评估手段，包括：1. 比较模型在孤立情境下与多源合成情境下识别伪造统计数据的能力；2. 跨五个模型（Claude, Qwen, OLMo）及三个专业领域的行为测试；3. 利用因果追踪（causal tracing）、线性探针（linear probes）和组件级归因分析（component-level attribution）等机制分析方法，揭示模型内部对方法论风格与数据有效性的编码差异。

Result: 研究发现模型虽具备识别虚假统计数据的能力，但在多源合成时会忽略数据的逻辑有效性，转而受“方法论语域（methodology-register）”控制。即无论统计数据是否合理，模型仅关注文本是否表现出专业风格。即便通过提示工程（如清单核查）进行干预，模型也只会表现出无差别的怀疑，而非选择性的精准识别。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型存在“认识论对齐”问题：模型在多源信息合成过程中，会错误地将文本风格（即“看起来像专业分析”）误认为证据的真实性，而忽视了统计数据的客观有效性。这种缺陷源于模型在训练和对齐过程中强化了基于风格的捷径，而非真正的逻辑或数值验证能力。

Abstract: Language models increasingly act as epistemic proxies, synthesizing evidence from multiple sources to inform decisions. Whether they evaluate the quality of that evidence, or merely aggregate it based on surface presentation, remains poorly understood. We show that models possess the capability to detect fabricated statistics (correct identification rates of 0.76-1.00 for methodology in isolation) but do not recruit this capability during multi-source synthesis, producing similar numeric estimates whether the statistics are fabricated or valid. Specifically, source influence is governed by a methodology-register gate that responds to the distributional register of analytical text but not to numeric validity: for example, statistically impossible confidence intervals receive the same weight as valid ones. The behavioral dissociation replicates across five models from three families (Claude, Qwen, OLMo) and three professional domains. Mechanistic analyses, including causal tracing, linear probes, and component-level attribution, converge on the same account: the model encodes and causally uses a methodology-register representation that transfers across domains (probe AUC 0.83-0.92), while numeric-validity signals, decodable in isolation, are suppressed to chance during multi-source synthesis. Prompting-based mitigations, even an oracle checklist naming the exact statistical checks, produce blanket skepticism rather than selective discernment, and the post-training pipelines we examine reinforce the stylistic shortcut without building numeric verification. Unlike sycophancy, which tracks user preference, this failure tracks whether a source presents as analytically credible, not whether its claims are internally consistent. We term this epistemic alignment: like preference and safety alignment, the question is not capability but deployment.

</details>


### [82] [CausalPOI: Spatio-Temporal Graph-Based Causal Modeling for Cold-Start POI Check-in Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05413)
*Zhaoqi Zhang,Miao Xie,Yi Li,Linyou Cai,Siqiang Luo,Gao Cong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对新设兴趣点（POI）预测难的问题，本研究提出 CausalPOI 框架，通过时空功能交互图与因果推断技术，实现了对城市动态行为更准确、可解释的预测与分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 POI 时空预测方法多基于邻近度与相关性，缺乏对 POI 间功能依赖的建模，且无法评估城市干预措施的因果效应。此外，缺乏针对新设立 POI（冷启动）的预测机制，限制了其在城市规划与商业决策中的应用。

Method: 提出了一种基于时空图的因果表示学习框架 CausalPOI。该方法构建了“时空功能交互图”以捕获 POI 间的语义与空间依赖，并通过构建结构对齐的“处理组”与“对照组”图来模拟事实与反事实场景，从而解耦并估计 POI 的因果演化规律。

Result: 在 SafeGraph 真实数据集上的实验表明，CausalPOI 在时空预测、语义交互建模及因果效应估计任务中均显著优于现有的先进基线模型。

Conclusion: CausalPOI 通过结合时空功能交互图与因果表示学习，成功解决了新设兴趣点（POI）的冷启动预测难题，不仅提升了预测准确性，还增强了模型在城市干预分析中的可解释性与决策支持能力。

Abstract: As urban environments continue to evolve rapidly, accurately modeling the dynamic behaviour of Points of Interest is essential for supporting data-driven urban planning and commercial decision-making. While recent advancements in spatio-temporal graph learning have improved POI forecasting, most methods rely on proximity-based graphs and correlation-driven modeling, which overlook the functional dependencies between POIs and fail to capture the causal effects of urban interventions. In this paper, we introduce a novel research problem -- cold-start POI check-in forecasting, which aims to predict the future check-in pattern of a newly introduced POI, by modeling its temporal evolution and functional interactions with nearby POIs in a structured urban spatial context. To address these challenges, we propose CausalPOI, a spatio-temporal graph-based causal representation learning framework. CausalPOI leverages Spatio-Temporal Functional Interaction Graph to model semantic and spatial relationships between POIs, and constructs structurally aligned treatment and control graphs to simulate factual and counterfactual scenarios. Extensive experiments on real-world SafeGraph datasets demonstrate that CausalPOI significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across the board, validating its effectiveness in spatio-temporal forecasting, semantic interaction modeling, and causal effect estimation, providing a more interpretable and actionable foundation for urban intervention analysis. Source code is available at Github.

</details>


### [83] [Towards Unified and Data-Efficient Prognostics and Health Management with Tabular Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05481)
*Raffael Theiler,Lev Telyatnikov,Leandro Von Krannichfeldt,Olga Fink*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将表格基础模型应用于工业PHM（故障预测与健康管理），通过将时间序列转化为表格数据，利用上下文学习解决了工业数据碎片化和标注稀疏的挑战，在多项预测与诊断任务中展现了优于传统序列模型的高效性和通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业PHM领域的数据往往存在碎片化、观测不完整及标注缺失的问题，限制了监督学习的应用。现有的大多数时间序列基础模型主要针对常规、长序列的预测任务，无法很好地适应复杂的工业PHM场景，因此需要一种更通用的数据驱动解决方案。

Method: 提出了一种利用“上下文学习”（in-context learning）将工业时间序列应用于表格基础模型（Tabular Foundation Models）的框架。该方法通过将原始的单元级（unit-level）信号转化为表格行数据，并利用PFN（Prior-Data Fitted Networks）架构处理预测与诊断任务，验证了在低数据环境下的性能表现。

Result: 实验表明，表格基础模型在多项预测与诊断任务中取得了最佳的平均排名；在数据稀缺的情况下极具竞争力；证明了通过适当的上下文构建，表格表示法能够保留时间序列的时序特征，且优于现有的Transformer基线模型和梯度提升树。

Conclusion: 表格基础模型为异构工业PHM问题提供了一种通用、实用且高效的接口，能够有效地处理碎片化、部分观测及标注稀疏的工业数据，在多种预测与诊断任务中表现优于传统序列模型。

Abstract: Data-driven Prognostics and Health Management (PHM) uses time-varying condition-monitoring data to diagnose system states and estimate remaining useful life in engineered assets. These tasks are central to maintenance planning, but industrial PHM data are often fragmented, partially observed, and poorly labeled, which hinders supervised learning. Foundation models offer a route toward reusable predictive systems, yet most time-series foundation models are designed for forecasting and assume long, coherent, regularly sampled sequences. To address this gap, we propose a framework for applying Tabular Foundation Models to industrial time series using in-context learning, and we evaluate them on a variety of PHM tasks. By converting raw unit-level signals into tabular rows, we show that these models perform well across multiple tasks - including prognostics, and diagnostics - and are highly data efficient. We compare them directly with sequence models, transformer baselines, and gradient-boosted trees under a common evaluation protocol. The results indicate that tabular foundation models achieve the best average ranks across prognostic and diagnostic tasks. Our findings further show that PFN-based models are competitive in low-data regimes, that temporal context can be preserved in the tabular representation, and that performance depends on representative context construction under subsampling. These results demonstrate that tabular foundation models provide a practical and general interface for heterogeneous PHM problems.

</details>


### [84] [What Objects Enable, Not What They Are: Functional Latent Spaces for Affordance Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05533)
*Rohan Siva,Neel P. Bhatt,Yunhao Yang,Seoyoung Lee,Nishant Gadde,Christian Ellis,Alvaro Velasquez,Zhangyang Wang,Ufuk Topcu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: A4D 通过将机器人视觉感知从“看外观”转向“察功能”（可供性），实现了更高效、更具泛化能力的机器人规划，能够快速适应未见过的物体交互并显著提升推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器人规划系统过于依赖基于外观的表征，导致模型无法捕捉任务相关的功能性（如“可移动性”），从而限制了机器人在处理新对象和新交互时的泛化能力。

Method: 提出了一种名为 A4D 的框架，核心是将视觉观测映射到一个基于“可供性”（Affordance，如“可移动”）组织的共享潜在空间。该方法通过计算视觉观测与可供性的距离来推断对象的功能，并包含一个可供性发现机制，通过量化推断的不确定性，在现有可供性不足时自动扩展潜在空间以适应新场景。

Result: 在多项规划任务中，A4D 在现有可供性推断上达到 94% 的准确率，较现有最优方法提升超 15 个百分点；在面对新可供性时，准确率从 70% 提升至 90% 以上，同时所需训练数据量减少 90%，且推断速度提升了 100 倍。

Conclusion: A4D 通过引入以功能性（可供性）为导向的潜在空间，成功解决了传统基于外观的机器人规划系统在处理新型交互时的泛化能力瓶颈。该方法证明了将视觉观察映射至功能性空间是实现高效、自适应机器人规划的有效途径。

Abstract: Existing robot planning systems rely on appearance-based reasoning, where visual observations are encoded into latent spaces organized around object appearances (e.g., recognizing a "cart" based on how it looks). However, planning requires reasoning about task-relevant functionalities of objects (e.g., whether an object is "movable"), which appearance-based latent spaces do not capture. As a result, existing approaches struggle to generalize to novel robot-object interactions. We address this limited generalizability through affordance reasoning, enabling planning based on task-relevant object functionalities instead of appearance alone. We introduce A4D, which maps visual observations into a shared latent space structured around affordances (e.g., "movable"). By projecting visual observations into this functional latent space and measuring their proximity to affordances, A4D infers functionalities relevant to the observed object. Furthermore, we introduce an affordance discovery mechanism that expands the latent space to handle unseen scenarios where existing affordances are insufficient. A4D uses proximity in the functional latent space to quantify uncertainty in affordance inference and selectively triggers affordance discovery. We evaluate A4D across several planning tasks involving diverse and unseen affordances. A4D achieves 94% inference accuracy on existing affordances outperforming state-of-the-art approaches by over 15% points, improves new-affordance inference accuracy from 70% to over 90% with fewer than 10% of the original training data, and enables 100x faster inference. Code, videos, and data available at: https://A4Dance-reasoning.github.io.

</details>


### [85] [Autoregressive Diffusion World Models for Off-Policy Evaluation of LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05558)
*Kaixuan Liu,Guojun Xiong,Weinan Zhang,Shengpu Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ADWM 是一种无需在线交互的离线评估框架，通过自回归扩散世界模型模拟智能体与环境的交互，有效解决了 LLM 智能体评估成本高、风险大以及传统 OPE 方法处理离散动作效果不佳的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多轮交互环境中评估大语言模型（LLM）智能体需要实时交互，这不仅成本高昂，而且由于不确定性可能带来风险。现有的离线策略评估（OPE）方法难以处理 LLM 智能体中离散的文本动作以及因自回归模型导致的累积误差问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ADWM（自回归扩散世界模型）的评估框架。该方法通过学习潜在扩散世界模型来模拟环境对智能体策略的响应。核心机制是将每个状态转移建模为独立的去噪过程，并由待评估的 LLM 智能体通过策略条件分数函数引导扩散生成，从而实现环境与智能体的因果交互式演进。

Result: 实验结果表明，ADWM 在多种多轮智能体任务中均能实现准确的价值估计，并具有良好的评估可靠性，证明了其作为离线评估框架的实际应用价值。

Conclusion: ADWM 提供了一种高效且可靠的离线评估 LLM 智能体的方法。通过结合扩散模型与自回归推理的优势，该框架无需在线交互即可准确评估智能体在复杂环境中的性能，为 LLM 智能体的迭代开发提供了有效的评估工具。

Abstract: Evaluating large language model (LLM) agents in multi-turn interactive environments is expensive and risky, as it requires online environment interaction. We propose ADWM (Autoregressive Diffusion World Model), an evaluation framework that estimates the performance of a new LLM agent policy purely from pre-collected trajectories. The core idea is to learn a latent diffusion world model that simulates how the environment responds to the evaluation policy, without ever executing it in the real environment. Existing diffusion-based OPE methods guide full trajectories in a single pass by jointly diffusing states and actions, an assumption that breaks down for LLM agents whose actions are discrete text that must be sampled from the policy after observing the environment. Unlike autoregressive world models that suffer from compounding errors, ADWM models each transition as an independent denoising process, enabling reliable step-by-step rollouts where the world model and agent alternate in causal order. Crucially, the LLM agent under evaluation directly guides the diffusion generation at each step via a policy-conditioned score function, ensuring that simulated trajectories accurately reflect its decision-making patterns. Empirically, ADWM achieves accurate value estimates and evaluation reliability across diverse multi-turn agent tasks, demonstrating its promise as a practical framework for offline LLM agent evaluation.

*Evan Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过控制实验构建了一个发育模型，揭示了从单纯的世界预测器向具备自我意识的智能体转化的四个严格顺序条件，并提出了“代理增益”这一核心指标来衡量这一过程。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究确定了系统产生自我意识的四个必要条件：1. 形成稳定吸引子的持久状态；2. 连接输出与输入的因果动作循环；3. 将隐性知识显性化的本体感受反馈；4. 感知学习先于动作学习的异步唤醒机制。实验表明，前向采样动作选择策略能有效产生代理增益，而梯度优化方法则失效。同时，研究证伪了12个关于自我意识发育的假设，指出单纯的预测编码无法产生自我。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了自我意识并非源于单一的算法，而是一个需要满足严格顺序的四个阶段的发育过程。通过引入“代理增益（agency gain）”指标，验证了自我预测在复杂和混沌环境中的优势。研究强调，单纯的预测编码不足以产生自我表征，必须通过特定的因果循环和异步学习机制才能实现。

Abstract: How does a system that merely predicts the world come to distinguish its own causal influence from everything else? We trace this transition in a minimal 192-dimensional GRU through 40 controlled experiments arranged as a developmental sequence, adding components one at a time and tracking whether the system can distinguish self-caused from world-caused changes.
  The developmental path reveals four conditions that must be satisfied in strict order: (1) persistent state forming stable attractors, (2) a causal action loop linking output to input, (3) proprioceptive feedback that makes implicit causal knowledge explicit, and (4) asynchronous awakening - perceptual learning must consolidate before action learning begins. We propose agency gain (A = Err_world - Err_self), the predictive advantage of knowing one's own action, as a metric to track this process. The self-aware predictor consistently outperforms the self-blind predictor across periodic (sinusoidal) and chaotic (Lorenz) environments, and the metric survives ablation of all auxiliary components. Only forward-sampled action selection produces meaningful agency gain; two gradient-based alternatives degenerate.
  Equally significant are 12 falsified hypotheses mapping where development stalls: predictive coding alone does not produce self-represent

### [87] [StableRCA: Robust Graph-Agnostic Mechanism-Level Root Cause Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05636)
*Xiaoyu Lin,Nicholas Tagliapietra,Kehan Li,Lavdim Halilaj,Juergen Luettin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: StableRCA 是一种新型的局部根因分析框架，它通过估计局部马尔可夫边界及检测条件分布偏移来定位系统异常，无需全局因果图，在多种复杂应用场景下均具备高鲁棒性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的根因分析（RCA）方法存在局限性：基于图的方法依赖于准确的因果图，而无图的统计方法则难以区分结构性原因或对系统假设要求过高。因此，需要一种能够避开全局图发现且鲁棒性强的 RCA 方法。

Method: 提出 StableRCA 框架，该方法避免了全局因果图的发现，转而通过估计局部马尔可夫边界（Markov boundaries）并检测其内部的条件分布偏移来定位根因。

Result: 实验证明，StableRCA 对图的错误指定具有稳健性，在多干预目标下表现有效，且在大规模系统和不同应用领域中均展现出可靠的性能。其干预目标的识别概率随着样本量的增加呈指数级收敛。

Conclusion: StableRCA 通过利用独立因果机制原则，在无需全局因果图的情况下，实现了对复杂系统中干预目标的有效定位，具有较强的稳健性、可扩展性和领域通用性。

Abstract: Root-Cause Analysis (RCA) seeks to identify the variables responsible for abnormal system behavior in complex domains such as manufacturing, cloud computing, and healthcare. Existing approaches face a critical bottleneck: graph-based causal methods can identify intervention targets but typically require a known or accurately estimated causal graph, while graph-free statistical methods either localize marginal anomalies rather than structural causes, or rely on restrictive assumptions about graph structure or functional form. We propose StableRCA, a local mechanism-level RCA framework that avoids global graph discovery by estimating local Markov boundaries and detecting conditional distribution shifts within them. Leveraging the Independent Causal Mechanism principle, we show that intervention targets can be identified with probability converging exponentially in sample size under faithful Markov boundary recovery and non-degenerate mechanism shifts. Experiments on synthetic benchmarks and five real-world datasets demonstrate that StableRCA is robust to graph misspecification, effective under multiple intervention targets, scalable to large systems, and reliable across diverse application domains. Code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/StableRCA-E362

Unlike existing benchmarks, it supports static and time-varying treatments, as well as both single-policy and multi-policy intervention settings, enabling evaluation of causal inference methods across a broad range of causal inference scenarios. Leveraging a calibrated agent-based model grounded in real-world demographic, mobility, epidemiological, and policy data, we generate realistic counterfactual trajectories across more than 150 U.S. counties. Using this benchmark, we evaluate widely used and state-of-the-art causal inference methods, revealing substantial performance differences and highlighting the challenges of realistic time-series causal reasoning.

### [89] [Zero-Copy Semantic Contagion: An In-Memory Streaming Architecture for Evolving Attention Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05733)
*Kabir Murjani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于动态注意力图的金融预测系统，通过高性能流式架构捕捉新闻驱动的跨公司联动效应，显著优于传统单资产预测模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的单资产（Per-ticker）金融时间序列预测模型无法感知公司间的联动与信息传导效应（例如：台积电的供应链中断无法在苹果的单资产模型中即时体现），导致模型在处理突发新闻对跨资产影响时存在严重的盲区与滞后。

Method: 研究提出了一种结合高性能Rust-Python的流式计算架构，具体包括：1. 基于Rust的零拷贝高速新闻解析与目标资产扫描引擎；2. 基于多变量神经霍克斯过程（Neural Hawkes Process）的预测模型，利用带有节点级连续时间LSTM状态和双线性潜投影来模拟资产间的定向激发；3. 采用自适应剪枝策略限制动态邻域更新的计算开销。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了跨公司图拓扑结构对于捕捉金融时间序列中的联动效应至关重要。通过结合高性能流式处理架构与多变量神经霍克斯过程，该系统不仅解决了单资产模型无法捕捉行业联动溢出效应的局限，还实现了亚毫秒级的数据吞吐与毫秒级的预测延迟，验证了在金融高频场景下动态图注意力机制的有效性。

Abstract: Per-ticker forecasting models dominate financial time-series work yet remain blind to cross-company propagation: a foundry disruption in Taiwan does not register in a single-asset model until Apple's own price has already moved. To address this limitation, we introduce a heterogeneous Rust-Python streaming architecture that maps cross-company attention as a continuous-time graph driven directly from text. We show that on the ingestion side, a zero-copy Rust edge parses news records in $\sim$100 ns and scans the target equity universe in $\sim$1.2 $μ$s. On the inference end, a multivariate Neural Hawkes Process featuring per-node continuous-time LSTM states and a bilinear latent projection propagates directed excitation, while an adaptive pruning rule bounds the computational cost of dynamic neighborhood updates. Combining these stages, we demonstrate an end-to-end processing latency of $\sim$13 ms per incoming news record on a single commodity CPU. Evaluated on a one-month temporal holdout of the FNSPID corpus (638 articles across 47 tickers), the system delivers a $1.70\times$ precision lift over random at the 90th-percentile next-day return threshold, and $3.36\times$ over a same-sector baseline. Crucially, removing the graph topology collapses precision to zero, confirming that the dynamic attention network is the sole driver of cross-company signal in this architecture.

### [90] [Beyond Soft Masks: Hard-Perturbation Mixup Explainer for Robust GNN Explainability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05756)
*Jialiang Yin,Zheng Zhao,Linsey Pang,Bo Dong,Bin Shi,Jiaxing Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HPME 是一种新型 GNN 解释框架，通过将解释过程离散化并利用结构级替换策略，有效克服了传统软掩码方法带来的冗余信息泄露和分布外问题，显著提升了解释的准确性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图神经网络（GNN）解释方法多采用软掩码，无法彻底消除标签无关信息，导致冗余结构影响预测并加剧分布外（OOD）问题，从而降低了解释的保真度。

Method: 提出了硬扰动混合解释框架（HPME），基于广义图信息瓶颈理论，利用图池化（Graph Pooling）提取离散解释子图并压缩标签无关信息，同时引入结构级替换混合策略来生成分布内解释，以缓解分布偏移。

Result: 在多个合成及真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，HPME 在生成稳健且具可解释性的解释方面优于现有的先进方法。

Conclusion: HPME 通过离散化子图提取和结构级替换策略，有效解决了现有解释方法在处理标签无关信息和分布外（OOD）问题上的不足，在鲁棒性和可解释性方面达到了业界领先水平。

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) have demonstrated remarkable performance across a range of applications involving graph-structured data, particularly in high-stakes domains. However, the opaque nature of their decision-making processes limits their trustworthiness and broader adoption. Existing post-hoc explanation methods aim to improve explainability by identifying subgraphs that influence GNN predictions and adopt mixup strategies to alleviate the out-of-distribution (OOD) issue caused by using subgraphs for prediction. Yet, these approaches typically rely on soft masks, which are inherently unable to fully eliminate label-irrelevant information, allowing redundant structures to leak into the mixup process and hindering the resolution of the OOD problem, thereby degrading explanation fidelity. In this work, we propose HPME, a Hard-Perturbation Mixup Explanation framework grounded in a generalized Graph Information Bottleneck, which leverages graph pooling to extract discrete explanatory subgraphs and to yield an information-capacity bound to thoroughly compress label-irrelevant components. Furthermore, we introduce a novel mixup strategy built upon structure-level replacement, generating in-distribution explanations to effectively mitigate the distribution shift. Extensive experiments on diverse tasks demonstrate that HPME achieves state-of-the-art performance in generating robust and interpretable explanations across both synthetic and real-world datasets.

In blind evaluation on 53 previously unseen production transcripts, it achieves 100% JSON structural validity, 83.0% human-validated overall accuracy, and 100% accuracy on the most critical classification field. The proposed approach formalizes a hybrid neural-symbolic decomposition and introduces targeted hard-negative augmentation to improve performance on critical decision boundaries. Running on a single NVIDIA A100 GPU, inference completes in approximately 2 seconds, which is 2-5x faster than frontier-model APIs. The system costs only $0.013 per evaluation compared with $0.025-$0.055 for proprietary alternatives, resulting in 46-76% cost savings. These results demonstrate that domain-adapted small language models, when combined with deterministic post-processing, can match frontier-model accuracy for structured compliance evaluation while substantially reducing operational cost, latency, and privacy risk.

### [92] [Causal Longitudinal Prior-Fitted Networks for Counterfactual Outcome Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05797)
*Amirhossein Zare,Amirhessam Zare,Herlock Rahimi,Reza Salarikia,Mohammad Kashkooli*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的纵向因果评估方法通常需要针对每个特定的队列或模拟器进行独立训练，在面对时间变化的混杂因素、患者动态异质性以及特定领域数据匮乏时，训练成本高且灵活性不足。因此，需要一种能够泛化且无需频繁重新训练的通用因果预测框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CausalLongPFN 的先验拟合上下文预测器。该模型通过在合成的临时结构因果模型（Temporal SCMs）上进行大规模预训练，捕捉治疗-混杂因子反馈、潜在异质性及非线性状态演化等特征。在测试阶段，模型被固定，通过对支持轨迹和查询历史进行上下文学习（In-context learning），无需梯度更新即可直接输出未来治疗序列下的结果预测。

Result: 在癌症、HIV和华法林等具有反事实标签的基准测试中，CausalLongPFN 的表现与经过特定领域训练的基线模型相当；在 MIMIC-III 重症监护数据集的事实预测任务中也表现出色，验证了合成因果预训练的有效性。

Conclusion: CausalLongPFN证明了在大规模合成因果先验上进行预训练，可以有效地构建一种无需微调的通用纵向因果预测模型。该方法在处理多步骤治疗序列和复杂因果动态时表现出竞争力，为在计算成本高昂或数据受限的场景下提供了一种高效的替代方案。

Abstract: Longitudinal treatment decisions require predicting potential outcomes under future treatment sequences in the presence of time-varying confounding, heterogeneous patient dynamics, and limited domain-specific data. Existing longitudinal causal estimators typically train a new model for each cohort or simulator. We introduce Causal Longitudinal Prior-Fitted Networks (CausalLongPFN), a prior-fitted in-context predictor for longitudinal causal prediction. The model is pretrained entirely on synthetic episodes sampled from a broad prior over temporal structural causal models, exposing it to treatment-confounder feedback, latent heterogeneity, nonlinear state evolution, delayed effects, and cumulative treatment responses. At test time, CausalLongPFN is frozen: it conditions on support trajectories, a query history, and a proposed future treatment sequence, and returns a predictive distribution over future outcomes without gradient updates or propensity-model fitting. Multi-step predictions are obtained by recursively applying the one-step predictor under the specified treatment sequence. We evaluate on branchable cancer, HIV, and warfarin benchmarks with ground-truth counterfactual labels, and on factual-only rolling-origin prediction in MIMIC-III ICU trajectories. CausalLongPFN is competitive with domain-trained longitudinal baselines on counterfactual benchmarks and performs strongly on factual MIMIC-III prediction, suggesting that broad synthetic causal pretraining can provide a useful frozen alternative when repeated domain-specific training is costly or impractical.

</details>


### [93] [Robust and sparse support vector machine via hybrid truncated loss for supervised classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05814)
*Yuliang Yang,Chen Chen,Yuxiang Liu,Huiru Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Lht的混合截断损失函数，通过结合高效的优化算法，构建了单视图及多视图支持向量机模型，显著提升了分类性能、稀疏性及对噪声的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的支持向量机（SVM）模型存在缺陷：凸损失函数（如铰链损失）对异常值敏感，而有界非凸损失函数计算成本高昂。作者旨在开发一种既能保持稀疏性（减少支持向量数量）又具有鲁棒性（对噪声不敏感）且计算高效的损失函数及对应模型。

Method: 1. 提出了一种兼具稀疏性和有界性的混合截断损失函数（Lht）；
2. 引入P-驻点概念，推导出一阶最优性必要和充分条件；
3. 设计了基于工作集策略的交替方向乘子法（ADMM）以降低计算成本；
4. 将模型扩展至多视图场景（MvLht-SVM），结合视图权重和结构信息，利用一致性和互补性原则进行优化。

Result: 实验表明，Lht-SVM在单视图分类中比对比方法具有更高的准确率、更少的支持向量和更强的抗噪能力；MvLht-SVM在多视图学习任务中，在准确率、精确率、召回率和F1值指标上均超越了六种主流对比方法。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一种新型混合截断损失函数（Lht），有效平衡了稀疏性与鲁棒性。通过P-驻点理论和基于工作集策略的交替方向乘子法（ADMM），实现了高效的全局收敛求解。该模型在单视图和多视图分类任务中均表现优于现有主流方法，特别是在噪声鲁棒性和稀疏性方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: The support vector machine (SVM) is a widely used classifier, but choosing an appropriate loss function remains difficult. Convex losses such as the hinge loss and least-squares loss are sensitive to outliers, while bounded non-convex losses often lead to high computational cost. To address this, we propose a hybrid truncated loss function ($L_{\mathrm{ht}}$) that is both sparse and bounded, and build the $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM model for single-view classification. We introduce the P-stationary point and use it to establish the first-order necessary and sufficient optimality conditions. Based on these conditions, we design an alternating direction method of multipliers with a working-set strategy that reduces computational cost and achieves global convergence. We further extend $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM to multi-view learning by adding structural information and view weights, resulting in Mv$L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM, which follows both the consensus and complementarity principles. Experiments on synthetic, real-world, and image datasets show that $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM achieves higher accuracy with fewer support vectors and better noise robustness than five single-view methods, while Mv$L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM outperforms six multi-view methods in accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score.

### [94] [Consistency Training Along the Transformer Stack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05817)
*Sukrati Gautam,Neil Shah,Arav Dhoot,Bryan Maruyama,Caroline Wei,Rohan Kapoor,Robert Sidey,Prakhar Gupta,Zi Cheng Huang,David Demitri Africa*

TL;DR: 本文扩展了一致性训练方法，通过引入MLP和注意力一致性目标，成功防御了多种新型的大模型安全威胁，证明了该框架在统一不同安全防御机制方面的有效性与泛化潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索一致性训练在减少大模型错位（misalignment）方面的潜力，试图将其应用范围从已有的谄媚（sycophancy）和越狱（jailbreak）场景扩展到更广泛的失效模式，并探究其背后的机制及泛化性能。

Result: 实验证明，一致性训练在上述四种新的安全威胁中均能显著降低模型的错位程度。研究还发现，针对某种失效模式的训练能够提升对其他模式的鲁棒性（即跨威胁泛化），并确定了不同一致性训练方法在机制上的异同。

Conclusion: 一致性训练不仅是一种有效的对齐方法，而且是一个灵活且可扩展的框架，能够整合针对多种模型失效模式的防御策略。研究揭示了不同一致性目标（ACT、MLPCT、AttCT）背后存在共享的残差流机制，且其防御效果具有跨威胁的泛化能力。

Abstract: Consistency training encourages models to behave similarly across different contexts, and has shown promise for reducing misalignment. We broaden the scope of consistency training in two ways. First, we introduce two new internal consistency targets: MLP Consistency Training (MLPCT), which matches post-activation MLP states, and Attention Consistency Training (AttCT), which matches per-head attention distributions. Second, we apply consistency training to four additional safety threats: persona in-context learning attacks, adversarial frustration, prefill attacks, and conditional misalignment. Across several models and threat settings, we find that consistency training reduces misalignment well beyond the sycophancy and jailbreak settings studied in prior work. We also find cases of cross-threat generalization, where training against one failure mode improves robustness to another, and identify a shared residual-stream mechanism underlying ACT, MLPCT, and AttCT, while distinguishing BCT as mechanistically distinct. Our results suggest that consistency training is a flexible and extensible framework for alignment, capable of unifying defenses against a broader class of model pathologies.

### [95] [Deciphering Two Training Clocks in Grokking via Deep Linear Network Theory with Conditional ReLU Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05863)
*Hu Tan,Kuo Gai,Shihua Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“双训练时钟”理论，解释了深度学习中Grokking现象的动力学过程：模型通过较快的时间尺度完成数据拟合，随后通过较慢的时间尺度进行表示简化，从而实现从记忆到泛化的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在通过数学分析揭示“Grokking”现象（即神经网络在训练误差趋近于零后，随着训练时间的推移，测试误差依然会持续下降的现象），解释模型拟合数据与学习简单潜在规律为何发生在不同的时间尺度上。

Method: 1. 形式化建模：提出了“双训练时钟”的概念，区分分类损失衰减与表示简化；2. 深度线性网络分析：在具有权值衰减的条件下，利用Schatten型惩罚和Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz尾部条件证明了结构能量在多项式时间尺度上收敛；3. ReLU MLP推广：通过链式法则估算和分段线性假设，论证了分类头与嵌入块在有效梯度上的差异，解释了模型为何先拟合后简化；4. 实验验证：以模运算为基准任务验证上述理论。

Result: 证明了在深度线性网络中，分类任务的拟合发生在对数时间尺度，而权值衰减引起的表示简化发生在多项式时间尺度；在ReLU MLP中，由于梯度动力学的差异，分类头优先拟合，后续阶段则进行更深层的表示简化。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了深度学习中“Grokking”现象的本质原因，即模型训练过程中存在两个不同的时间尺度：较快的分类损失下降（拟合阶段）和较慢的表示简化（泛化阶段）。通过将训练动力学分解为这两个阶段，作者为理解神经网络为何在过拟合后仍能通过持续训练获得泛化能力提供了坚实的数学框架。

Abstract: Grokking suggests that fitting the training data and learning a simple underlying rule may occur on different time scales. We formalize this phenomenon by separating the fast decay of the classification loss from the slower simplification of the learned representation, and we call the resulting pair of stopping times two training clocks. For deep linear networks, we show that a post-margin gap-growth or one-step tail-contraction condition reduces the cross-entropy loss to level epsilon on a logarithmic time scale. In contrast, when layerwise weight decay is present, the induced regularization on the end-to-end map can be expressed as a Schatten-type penalty; under a sharp late-time Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz tail, this structural energy closes on a polynomial time scale. The two clocks, therefore, separate fitting from representation simplification. We then explain how the same mechanism can appear in ReLU MLPs. In regions where the activation patterns on the training set remain fixed, the network reduces to a linear model in the active coordinates. In a two-layer ReLU embedding model, chain-rule estimates further show that the classifier head can receive larger effective gradients than the embedding block under controlled downstream norms. This supports a two-stage mechanism in which the classifier fits first, while the representation continues to simplify later. We use modular addition as the main experimental setting. The deep linear theory provides the rigorous core of the analysis. But the ReLU results are formulated as conditional reductions that account for empirical behavior without claiming a global proof for nonlinear training dynamics.

</details>


### [96] [Dead Directions: Geometric Singular Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05957)
*Tejas Pradeep Shirodkar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入“死方向”概念，成功将奇异学习理论与信息几何在神经网络领域融合，提供了一种在原始参数空间中无需复杂消解即可分析模型奇异几何结构的新方法，并据此提出了能够高效优化深层网络的DDCAdam算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有奇异学习理论（通常需参数消解）与信息几何（通常假设非退化性）在处理过参数化模型时存在脱节。过参数化模型在训练中经常出现参数空间奇异性，使得传统非退化假设失效，因此需要一种无需复杂消解且能在原始参数空间工作的理论框架来描述这些奇异结构。

Method: 1. 引入“死方向”（dead direction）作为连接奇异学习理论与信息几何的核心基元。
2. 证明了在原始参数坐标下，通过Fisher曲率在趋近奇异点时的衰减率，即可提取KL散度阶数。
3. 建立选择规则，将该衰减率转化为真实对数正则阈值（RLCT）。
4. 在深层网络中利用K-FAC分解，将Fisher块写为激活与梯度侧速率的乘积。
5. 构建了与规范群（gauge group）等变的DDCAdam优化器，确保梯度流在几何上的有效性。

Result: 1. 实现了在原始参数坐标下直接量化奇异性，无需复杂的数学消解过程。
2. 为深度神经网络架构提供了闭式预测模型。
3. 开发了DDCAdam算法，通过保持梯度流的群等变性，改善了模型在奇异区域的优化表现。
4. 提供了一种从单一检查点（checkpoint）的前向和后向传递中，直接读取Watanabe三元组（RLCT λ，多重性 m，奇异波动 ν）的实用方法。

Conclusion: 本研究成功架起奇异学习理论与信息几何之间的桥梁，证明了可以通过神经网络训练轨迹的动力学行为（如Fisher曲率衰减率）直接提取Watanabe的三元组（λ, m, ν），无需依赖复杂的奇异点消解（Hironaka resolution）或后验采样。此外，提出的DDCAdam优化器能够利用这些几何特性，在现代深度学习架构中实现更稳定的优化。

Abstract: Singular learning theory and information geometry have studied the same parameter spaces in mostly separate vocabularies: the former computes Bayesian invariants in resolved coordinates, the latter works in original coordinates under a non-degeneracy assumption that overparameterised models routinely violate. We bridge them through one primitive, the dead direction: a unit vector along which the Fisher metric degenerates, equivalently a tangent to the analytic singular set with a definite KL order, set by how fast the KL divergence vanishes. The two readings name the same vector; our central move shows its KL order is recoverable as the decay rate of the directional Fisher curvature approaching the singularity, in original parameter coordinates and without a Hironaka resolution. A selection rule on smooth fibres translates this rate into Watanabe's single-direction contribution to the real log canonical threshold, and we extend the recovery to multi-component crossings, multiplicity $m$, the singular fluctuation $ν$ (universal in the KL order for 1D directions), prior-RLCT shifts, and tempered posteriors. We then lift this rate to a deep network: a multi-layer K-FAC factorisation writes each Fisher block as a product of activation- and gradient-side rates with a duality between them, instantiated at modern-network primitives (residual streams, layer normalisation, attention). A quotient theorem carries the rate to the gauge quotient $Θ/G$ under gradient flow on a $G$-invariant metric; SGD qualifies, standard Adam does not, and we construct a $G$-equivariant Adam-family preconditioner (DDCAdam) that does. The bridge yields a parameter-coordinate handle on singular geometry, closed-form per-architecture predictions, and a trajectory-rate readout of Watanabe's triple $(λ, m, ν)$ from one checkpoint's forward and backward passes, without posterior sampling.

</details>

Abstract: Causal graphs provide a high-level language for making mechanisms transparent. Recent work uses Large Language Models (LLMs) to recover causal graphs of external-world processes. Instead, in this paper, we use causal graphs to model LLM inference itself, providing stakeholders with a transparent view of how the model perceives and organizes high-level concepts to produce a prediction. We propose a four-phase method for constructing such graphs. Given a target LLM and a set of textual examples, our method discovers class-discriminative, human-interpretable concepts and maps each input to LLM-perceived concept states. We then introduce an MCMC-inspired counterfactual augmentation procedure that expands the sparse observational data through chains of counterfactuals. This enables stable causal discovery with $σ$-CG, yielding informative, interpretable graphs. We apply our method to three LLMs across disease diagnosis, sentiment analysis, and LLM-as-a-judge classification tasks. We evaluate the learned graphs for predictive fidelity and structural stability, and the MCMC-inspired augmentation for convergence and downstream utility. Our results show that the discovered causal graphs capture meaningful dependencies consistent with LLMs' reasoning. Together, this paper provides a foundation for concept-level explainability of LLMs.

### [98] [HoT-SSM:Higher-order Temporal Knowledge Graph Reasoning with State Space Models for Health Care](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05994)

Abstract: Medical knowledge graphs (MKGs) infused with clinical knowledge have been increasingly used to model electronic health records (EHRs) to support interpretable predictions in healthcare domain. In addition, most representation learning methods that leverage MKGs either collapse temporal information across visits or lack an explicit mechanism for modeling long-range temporal dependencies, which is critical for clinical tasks such as mortality prediction. To mitigate these limitations, we propose HoT-SSM, a parameter efficient and higher-order temporal graph reasoning with state space models. For each visit, HoT-SSM constructs hypergraphs by grouping semantically related clinical concepts into hyperedges using domain knowledge, thereby preserving visit-level clinical context. Further, to model the temporal dynamics while learning the representations, we introduce a novel dynamic hypergraph-based state space model that explicitly captures patients latent state evolution over time while preserving long-range information. The learned representations are used for downstream clinical prediction and reasoning. Experiments on MIMIC-III and MIMIC-IV datasets shows significant performance improvement over the current state-of-the-art models, demonstrating the effectiveness of jointly modeling higher-order clinical interactions and long-range temporal dependencies.

*Zhangyao Song,Ziqiong Li,Xiangfei Qiu,Chao Zha,Yinfei Xu,Tao Guo*

TL;DR: AOSNET 是一种新型长期时间序列预测框架，通过引入希尔伯特变换将周期预测转变为“自适应振荡状态对齐”，从而克服了传统固定模板方法难以处理非平稳时间动态（如相位漂移、频率变化）的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的周期性预测方法通常依赖于固定的周期定义、全局谱分量或固定的可学习模板。然而，现实世界的时间序列往往具有非平稳性（如振幅调制、相位漂移和局部频率变化），导致固定模板无法准确捕捉复杂的动态变化。为了解决这一问题，研究者旨在开发一种能自适应处理非平稳振荡的时间序列预测方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 AOSNET 的希尔伯特导向预测框架。该方法将周期性预测重构为自适应振荡状态对齐问题：首先从观测序列和可学习的全局振荡先验中提取解析信号描述符，然后通过一个描述符条件门控机制，动态地对齐局部状态，实现对观测值的选择性保留和对失配区域的平滑修正。

Result: 在八个基准测试中，AOSNET 实现了最先进或极具竞争力的预测精度，且推理速度快。合成实验进一步验证了随着非平稳性的增强，该方法在处理振幅调制、相位漂移和局部频率变化方面的优势愈发显著。

Conclusion: AOSNET 证明了在处理具有非平稳性（如振幅调制、相位漂移和频率变化）的长期时间序列时，从“固定模板匹配”转向“自适应振荡状态对齐”是有效的。该框架证明了通过希尔伯特变换提取解析信号并结合可学习的振荡先验，能显著提升预测的灵活性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting benefits from inductive biases that expose recurring temporal structure. Existing periodic forecasting methods typically model recurrence through predefined periods, global spectral components, or fixed learnable templates. However, real-world temporal dynamics are rarely rigidly periodic: oscillatory behavior often evolves through amplitude modulation, phase drift, and local frequency variation. Under these conditions, fixed-template periodic modeling can become fundamentally mismatched to the underlying temporal states. We propose AOSNET, a Hilbert-guided forecasting framework that reformulates periodic forecasting from fixed template matching to adaptive oscillatory-state alignment. AOSNET extracts analytic-signal descriptors from both the observed sequence and a learnable global oscillatory prior, then adaptively aligns local states through a descriptor-conditioned gate that selectively preserves reliable observations while softly correcting mismatched regions. The learned prior serves not as a rigid repeated template but as a flexible oscillatory reference interpreted through local state dynamics. Experiments on eight benchmarks demonstrate state-of-the-art or highly competitive accuracy with fast inference speed. Controlled synthetic studies isolating amplitude modulation, phase drift, and local frequency variation confirm that the advantage of oscillatory-state alignment consistently increases as non-stationarity intensifies.

</details>


### [100] [Catastrophic Forgetting as Accessibility Collapse: A Three-Level Framework for Knowledge Persistence in Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06032)
*Ayushman Trivedi,Bhavika Melwani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 灾难性遗忘本质上是一种“访问失败”而非“知识擦除”；即便模型表现完全失效，深层网络中仍保留了大量可恢复的任务信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为灾难性遗忘是旧知识在持续学习过程中被不可逆地擦除。本文旨在挑战这一观点，探讨遗忘是否是由于模型丧失了对已保存信息访问路径的控制，而非信息本身的物理破坏。

Method: 作者构建了一个包含知识存储、表示和可访问性的三层分析框架，并在CIFAR-100序列任务上使用ResNet-18模型进行实验。具体方法包括：线性探测（Linear Probing）、表征几何分析、分类器重置恢复实验、逐层可恢复性评估以及投影能量与主角分析，以量化模型在遗忘前后的信息保存情况。

Result: 实验显示，即使在模型表现完全坍塌（任务准确率从54.8%降至0%）的情况下，线性探测仍能保留约76%的任务信息。仅通过重训练最后一层分类器，模型即可恢复75.7%的原始性能，且早期和中间层保留了高度可恢复的特征，这些知识以分布式的形式嵌入在高维表征中。

Conclusion: 灾难性遗忘并非旧知识的彻底销毁，而是知识“可访问性”的丧失。神经网络在功能性遗忘发生后，其内部表示层中仍保留了大量可恢复的任务知识。这一发现挑战了传统观点，并为开发新型持续学习策略提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Catastrophic forgetting is commonly interpreted as the irreversible erasure of previously acquired knowledge during sequential learning. In this work, we investigate an alternative perspective: that forgetting may arise not from complete destruction of task representations but from a loss of accessibility to preserved information. We introduce a three-level framework separating knowledge storage, representation, and accessibility, and evaluate each component through a series of continual-learning experiments on sequential CIFAR-100 classification using ResNet-18. Our analysis combines checkpoint persistence, linear probing, representation geometry, classifier-reset recovery, and layer-wise recoverability experiments. We observe complete behavioral forgetting of earlier tasks, with task accuracy collapsing from 54.8% to 0%, while linear probe performance retains approximately 76% of the original representational information. Furthermore, retraining only the final classifier restores 75.7% of the original task performance without modifying the backbone network. Layer-wise analysis reveals that early and intermediate layers preserve highly recoverable task information despite severe degradation at later stages. Projection-energy and principal-angle analyses indicate that retained knowledge persists as distributed high-dimensional representations rather than through preservation of a small dominant subspace. These findings suggest that catastrophic forgetting is better characterized as an accessibility failure than complete representational erasure, and that substantial task-relevant information remains embedded within neural representations even after functional forgetting has occurred.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分块线性注意力机制中的矩阵求逆过程在NPU上存在严重的并行化瓶颈，传统的基于前向代入的方法硬件利用率低且计算效率受限，难以支撑长上下文建模的需求。

Method: 提出了基于截断诺依曼级数（Neumann-series）展开的算法，结合结构化掩码和并行残差校正技术消除序列依赖；同时针对低比特量化（INT）场景，通过抑制矩阵幂运算带来的动态范围扩张，并根据分块大小动态调整近似阶数和残差步骤。

Conclusion: 该研究成功提出了一种基于矩阵乘法（MatMul）的线性注意力机制逆矩阵计算算法，通过降低序列依赖性显著提升了长上下文模型在NPU上的运行效率，且保持了极高的推理精度，为大语言模型的部署提供了高效且硬件友好的解决方案。

Abstract: Matrix inversion in chunk-wise parallel linear attention is a major bottleneck for long-context modeling, particularly on NPUs, where forward-substitution-based methods exhibit limited parallelism and poor hardware utilization. We propose a fast, Matrix Multiplication (MatMul)-based algorithm tailored for strictly lower-triangular matrices arising in chunk-wise linear attention. Motivated by the rapid growth of Neumann-series terms and the diagonal concentration of the inverse matrix, we employ a truncated Neumann expansion with structural masking and parallel residual correction to eliminate sequential dependencies. We further extend our method to low-bits INT by mitigating the dynamic range expansion arising from repeated matrix power operations, and adapt the approximation order and residual step to the chunk size to minimize computational cost while preserving the model's accuracy. Experiments on Qwen3.5-family models demonstrate up to 5$\times$ kernel-level speedup and a 20% reduction in decode-layer overhead, while preserving accuracy under both floating-point and low-precision inference. Our method offers an efficient and hardware-friendly solution for scalable linear attention.

*Mohammad Mahdi Salmani-Zarchi,Zahra Rahimi,Heshaam Faili,Mohammad Javad Dousti*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 MDP-GRPO 框架，包含四项核心改进：(1) 多温度采样以增加奖励离散度；(2) 双锚优势函数以解决同质组内的梯度消失和平均归一化盲区；(3) 基于前景理论的奖励塑形以限制更新并惩罚违规；(4) 非对称 KL 正则化。

Conclusion: MDP-GRPO 通过解决 z-score 分组归一化在离散、低离散度奖励下的缺陷，有效提升了多约束指令遵循任务中的策略优化稳定性和性能，且不会损害模型的基础能力。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards is ideal for multi-constraint instruction following, yet standard group-relative policy optimization (GRPO) becomes unstable under discrete, low-dispersion rewards, where within-group reward distributions are frequently homogeneous. We identify and formalize three pathologies of z-score group normalization in this regime: low-variance amplification, mean-centering blindness, and zero-variance collapse. To address them, we propose MDP-GRPO, which stabilizes learning through (1) multi-temperature sampling to increase reward dispersion, (2) dual-anchor advantages to restore gradients in homogeneous groups and stop mean-centering blindness, (3) prospect-theoretic shaping to bound updates and penalize violations based on Kahneman and Tversky's theory, and (4) asymmetric KL regularization. Evaluated on FollowBench, IFEval, and a curated multi-constraint dataset, MDP-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO, improving strict constraint satisfaction by up to 5.0% on Llama-3.2-3B. Our method also enables stable convergence with small group sizes while preserving general capabilities on MMLU and ARC.

Result: 实验结果表明，所提出的 L2O 基线能显著降低梯度方差，MaxPO 在性能上超越了传统的非中心化优势估计方法，并证明了该方法在基于组的强化学习（Group-based RL）中的集成优势。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入“留二法”（Leave-Two-Out）基线，成功解决了现有推理时间目标优化中优势估计偏差的问题，提出的 MaxPO 方法不仅在数学上更严谨，且在实际应用中有效降低了梯度方差，为大语言模型的后训练提供了更高效的优化手段。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards is widely used for post-training reasoning models, but sparse outcome rewards make exploration difficult. A complementary approach is to optimize inference-time objectives such as pass@K and max@K directly, yet existing policy-gradient estimators for these objectives use different signals, baselines, and normalizations, making their relationships unclear. We study this issue through baseline design and advantage centering. Starting from the advantage estimator of a leading method in the field, we show that it is policy-gradient unbiased but yields a non-centered advantage. We then introduce a Leave-Two-Out baseline that preserves policy-gradient unbiasedness while making realized batch advantages exactly centered. The resulting method, MaxPO, has an efficient quadratic-time implementation and integrates naturally into group-based RL for LLM post-training. We further derive the canonical finite-batch advantage for max@K, providing a unified view of existing advantage estimators. ### [104] [OrderGrad: Optimizing Beyond the Mean with Order-Statistic Policy Gradient Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06096)
*Paavo Parmas,Yongmin Kim,Kohsei Matsutani,Shota Takashiro,Soichiro Nishimori,Takeshi Kojima,Yusuke Iwasawa,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OrderGrad 是一种新的梯度估计框架，通过简单的奖励重加权，使策略梯度方法能够直接优化回报的顺序统计量（如 CVaR、中位数、Top-m 等），从而实现风险敏感、稳健及探索性的强化学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的策略梯度方法主要优化期望回报（均值），但在许多现实应用中，用户更关注回报的分布特性，例如尾部风险（风险规避）、对异常值的稳健性或最佳探索（Best-of-K）。现有方法在处理这些特定顺序统计目标时往往缺乏统一且高效的实现手段。

Method: 作者提出了 OrderGrad，这是一类用于顺序统计目标（order-statistic objectives）的似然比和重参数化梯度估计器。该方法通过将有限样本的 L-统计量（即排序奖励的加权平均）转化为简单的奖励变换，使得现有的策略梯度算法无需复杂改动即可直接优化 VaR、CVaR、截尾均值、中位数及 Top-m 等目标。

Result: 实验表明，OrderGrad 能够为顺序统计目标提供无偏的梯度估计。在包括大模型数学推理训练在内的多个任务中，相比于单纯优化均值，OrderGrad 能够有效优化风险敏感型和探索型目标，显著提升了模型在特定部署目标下的性能。

Conclusion: OrderGrad 提供了一种通用、即插即用的框架，能够通过简单的奖励变换，将传统的策略梯度方法扩展至优化各种顺序统计量目标（如风险规避、稳健性或最佳探索）。该方法在处理均值优化不匹配的任务（如大模型数学推理）中展现了显著优势，并为强化学习中的复杂分布目标优化提供了统一的理论基础。

Abstract: Policy-gradient methods usually optimize expected return, but many real world applications care about distributional properties of returns: tail risk, outlier robustness, or best-of-K discovery. We introduce OrderGrad, a family of likelihood-ratio and reparameterization gradient estimators for order-statistic objectives. OrderGrad optimizes finite-sample L-statistics, i.e., weighted averages of sorted rewards or costs, recovering objectives such as VaR, CVaR, trimmed means, medians, and top-m/best-of-K criteria by changing only the rank weights. For any fixed sample size and rank-weight vector, OrderGrad provides an unbiased gradient estimator for the corresponding order-statistic objective. The method is implemented as a simple reward transformation that can then be used in an otherwise standard policy-gradient or reparameterized update. We study the resulting estimator's variance behavior and evaluate it on tasks where mean optimization is mismatched to the deployment objective, including LLM math post-training and other tasks. OrderGrad provides a unified, plug-and-play route to risk-averse, robust, and exploratory learning.
  Code: https://github.com/paavo5/ordergrad

### [105] [Adaptive state-action abstractions via rate-distortion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06123)

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在强化学习中动态调整抽象粒度的新原则：当学习误差与抽象引起的误差相当时，即对模型进行细化。通过结合性能证书与率失真理论，该方法实现了高效的状态-动作空间压缩，并在实验中取得了显著的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习方法缺乏一套通用的原则，以实现在学习过程中动态调整任务抽象的粒度（即从粗糙模型逐步细化到复杂模型），无法像婴儿学习行走那样高效地平衡探索复杂度与学习精度。

Method: 提出了一种通过性能证书（Performance Certificate）将值函数误差分解为贝尔曼残差（学习误差）和双模拟度量（抽象误差）的方法；利用基于率失真理论（Rate-Distortion Theory）构建的软状态-动作抽象，通过动态调整状态和动作空间的解析度来实现粒度切换。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于学习误差与抽象误差平衡的动态抽象细化原则，为强化学习中多粒度任务的学习提供了理论依据，并证明了在显著压缩状态和动作信息的情况下仍能保持近乎最优的性能。

Abstract: When learning to walk, infants seem to address a coarse version of the problem first - stay upright, reach the caregiver - and refine it only when further practice at that resolution stops paying off. Reinforcement learning offers multiple techniques for building simple versions of complex tasks, but lacks general principles for how to dynamically adjust the granularity of these abstractions during learning. This paper proposes one such principle: refine the abstraction as soon as the learning error within it becomes comparable to the error induced by the abstraction itself. Here, we investigate one way of formalising this principle via a performance certificate that decomposes value error into two terms: a learning error bound captured by a Bellman residual, and an abstraction error bound given by a bisimulation metric. The resulting switching strategy is implemented by soft state-action abstractions built from rate-distortion principles, whose resolution along state and action axes can be continuously adjusted. We validate this construction in a range of tabular settings, showing that near-optimal performance can be achieved under substantial lossy compression of state and action information.

### [106] [Tight list replicability bounds via a novel sphere covering theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06148)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 列表可复制性（list replicability）是机器学习领域形式化复现性的重要框架。研究旨在量化解决该问题所需的列表大小与算法准确度参数及假设空间复杂性度量之间的内在关系。

Method: 1. 理论推导：利用Borsuk-Ulam定理证明了一个新的拓扑球覆盖定理；2. 算法设计：基于上述定理为VC类和特定几何约束下的半空间类设计了列表可复制算法，并给出了相应的理论边界。

Result: 1. 证明了若$d$维球被若干开集覆盖且每个开集均位于某个开半球内，则其中必有$d+1$个集合拥有公共交集；2. 获得了VC类学习中列表大小与准确度关系的尖锐边界；3. 针对大间隔半空间问题，给出了随间隔大小变化的特定列表大小界限（即维数相关结论）。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入拓扑学的球覆盖定理，成功建立了列表可复制性与学习理论中复杂性度量之间的紧密联系，为理解和实现高效的可复制学习提供了重要的理论基础。

Abstract: In recent years, list replicability has emerged as a framework for formalizing reproducibility in learning theory. A central question is how the required list size relates to the accuracy parameter and natural complexity measures of the hypothesis class.
  To achieve sharp bounds on list replicability, we prove a novel topological sphere covering theorem, derived from the Borsuk-Ulam theorem. Specifically, if the $d$-sphere is covered by open sets, each of which lies in an open hemisphere, then $d+1$ of these sets must have a common intersection. Using this result, we obtain a sharp bound on the relationship between list size and accuracy for VC classes. We also show that for large-margin half-spaces, provided the margin is not too large, the optimal list size equals the ambient dimension. However, when the margin is taken to be very large, we devise a replicable algorithm achieving the minimal list size of $\lceil d/2 \rceil + 1$.

*Rebecca Potts,Aiden Durrant,Rick Hackney,Georgios Leontidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对燃气轮机机组排放预测中标签数据稀缺的问题，提出了一种结合多头循环网络与不确定性量化的信任感知框架，实现了高可靠性的氮氧化物（NOx）排放预测与分布外检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于机器学习的预测性排放监测系统（PEMS）在燃气轮机机组中应用广泛，但面临严重的数据瓶颈：只有少数机组拥有排放标签。如何利用有限的带标签数据，在缺乏标签的大规模工业机组中实现准确且可靠的氮氧化物（NOx）排放预测，是当前工业界的迫切需求。

Method: 提出了一种综合性的概率预测框架，核心组件包括：1. 多头循环预测模型；2. 学习型置信度估计；3. 基于集成学习的不确定性量化；4. 辅助特征预测；5. 特征空间距离分析；6. 运行范围诊断。通过这些组件生成可解释的“信任得分”来评估未标记机组的预测可靠性。

Result: 实验表明该框架有效，通过置信度过滤，预测平均绝对误差（MAE）从全覆盖时的0.202降低至最高置信度10%时的0.070。此外，该框架对未标记及分布外（OOD）样本表现出预期的不确定性增加，证明了其在面对数据分布偏移时具有良好的鲁棒性和诊断能力。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种具备可信度感知能力的概率框架，能够有效缓解燃气轮机机组间排放预测的泛化难题。通过量化预测不确定性，该框架不仅提升了预测准确度，还为工业部署提供了透明、可解释的可靠性指标，显著增强了部署过程中的决策支持能力。

Abstract: Machine learning-based predictive emissions monitoring systems offer a practical alternative to direct emissions measurement, but their deployment across gas turbine fleets is challenging when emissions labels are available for only a small subset of assets. In this work, a trust-aware probabilistic framework is proposed for fleet-level gas turbine NOx prediction under limited labelled supervision. The framework combines a multi-head recurrent prediction model with learned confidence estimation, ensemble-based uncertainty quantification, auxiliary feature prediction, feature-space distance analysis, and operating-range diagnostics. These signals are calibrated on labelled data to produce interpretable per-sample trust scores, providing indicators of prediction reliability on unlabelled turbines, supporting the identification of predictions that should be treated with greater caution during fleet-level deployment. Confidence-based filtering reduces MAE from 0.202 at full coverage to 0.070 for the highest-confidence 10\% of predictions, demonstrating that confidence estimates are meaningfully related to prediction error. Unlabelled and out-of-distribution samples exhibit increased uncertainty and reduced confidence, indicating that the framework responds appropriately to distributional shift. The results show that the proposed trust framework provides actionable reliability information for emissions prediction on unlabelled turbines, supporting more transparent and trustworthy deployment of PEMS across industrial fleets.

### [108] [On the training of physics-informed neural operators for solving parametric partial differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06164)
*Nanxi Chen,Chuanjie Cui,Airong Chen,Sifan Wang,Rujin Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统性地分析并优化了物理信息神经算子（PINO）的训练流程，证明了CViT架构的优越性，并将PINN的优化策略应用于PINO，实现了在多种偏微分方程任务中高效、鲁棒的求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然PINO结合了神经算子的泛化能力和物理约束的数据效率，但其训练过程相比于数据驱动的神经算子或物理信息神经网络（PINN）而言，缺乏高效、鲁棒的训练范式和系统性的理解。

Method: 本文评估了三种算子骨干网络（DeepONet、FNO、CViT）在五种参数化偏微分方程系统下的表现。重点分析了架构设计、优化器选择、损失平衡和配点采样策略，并将PINN中缓解梯度冲突和因果违规的算法迁移至PINO训练中，系统对比了物理驱动与数据驱动在不同数据量下的效果。

Result: 研究发现：(1) CViT在所选基准测试中表现最强且最稳定；(2) PINN训练中的常见优化病理（如梯度冲突、因果违规）同样存在于PINO中；(3) 针对PINN开发的缓解算法在PINO中同样有效；(4) 精心设计的物理驱动训练流程在不同数据规模下均具有很强的竞争力。

Conclusion: 本文系统性地揭示了物理信息神经算子（PINO）训练中的优化挑战，通过优化架构、损失平衡和采样策略，证明了经过精心设计的物理驱动训练流程在鲁棒性和性能上可以与纯数据驱动方法相媲美甚至超越，为高效物理驱动算子学习提供了实操指南。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural operators (PINOs) aim to learn solution operators for partial differential equations by using the governing physics as supervision, rather than relying solely on paired input-output simulation data. By incorporating physical constraints into the training objective, PINOs combine the cross-instance generalization of neural operators with the data efficiency of physics-informed learning. Despite this promise, how to train PINOs efficiently and robustly remains less well-understood than the training of either data-driven neural operators or physics-informed neural networks (PINNs). To bridge this gap, we examine key components of the PINO training pipeline, including architecture design, optimizer choice, loss balancing, and collocation-point sampling strategy. We study three representative operator backbones, Deep Operator Network (DeepONet), Fourier Neural Operator (FNO), and Continuous Vision Transformer (CViT), across five diverse parametric PDE systems. Our results show that CViT provides consistently strong and stable performance across the considered benchmarks. Beyond architecture, we find that several optimization pathologies previously identified in PINN training naturally arise in PINOs, including gradient conflicts and causal violation. We also find that mitigation algorithms developed for PINNs remain effective in the PINO setting. We further compare physics-informed and data-driven training under different data regimes, revealing that a carefully designed physics-informed training pipeline can match, and in some cases, outperform purely data-driven neural operators. Taken together, these findings provide a systematic empirical understanding of the optimization challenges in PINO training and inform a practical pipeline for efficient and robust physics-informed operator learning. Code and data are available at https://github.com/NanxiiChen/PI-CViT.

</details>

To address these limitations, we developed an unsupervised machine learning framework based on dynamic graph representation learning to capture temporal relationships within and across patients from longitudinal clinical measurements. Using the learned representations, we applied K-means++ clustering to identify well-separated groups. We then iteratively increased the number of clusters (k), using stability analysis to assess robustness and reveal additional meaningful clusters beyond the initial optimal solution. ### [112] [Non-Negative Matrix Factorization for Event Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06205)
*Raphaël Romero*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对连续时间事件数据在处理过程中因分桶预处理导致细节丢失的问题，本文提出了 EventNMF。该模型通过直接在事件时间上建模，利用非负 B 样条函数实现可解释的分解，在保持计算效率的同时提升了对细粒度时间模式的捕捉能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非负矩阵分解（NMF）方法在处理连续时间事件数据时，通常需要对数据进行分桶（binning）或平滑预处理，这会导致实体间的异质性和细粒度时间特征的丢失。因此，作者旨在开发一种无需预处理、能直接在连续时间域上操作的分解模型。

Method: 提出了一种名为 EventNMF 的模型，直接作用于事件时间戳，而非对数据进行分桶或平滑处理。该方法将每个实体的事件建模为泊松过程，并利用非负 B 样条基函数对强度函数进行分解，从而学习出跨实体的共享时间模板，同时提供了一种简单高效的估计算法。

Result: 实验结果表明，EventNMF 不仅在数学上严谨，且易于实现、计算高效。通过合成数据和真实世界应用验证，该模型在捕捉事件演化模式方面优于传统的离散化方法，且成功涵盖了分桶计数方法作为其特殊情况（零次样条）。

Conclusion: EventNMF 提供了一种无需离散化即可对连续时间事件数据进行非负矩阵分解的稳健框架，通过利用 B 样条基函数，有效保留了细粒度的时间特征，证明了该方法在处理多领域连续时间事件数据时的优越性。

Abstract: Continuous-time event data, in which entities emit instantaneous events over time, arises naturally across many domains such as neuroscience, seismology, and social networks. Non-negative matrix factorization (NMF) is a natural tool to uncover interpretable structure in such data, but it has so far only been applied after binning or smoothing the entity-level counting measures. This preprocessing step comes with the risk of erasing entity-level heterogeneities and fine-grained temporal features. In this paper, we introduce EventNMF, a continuous-time non-negative factorization model that operates directly on event times: each entity's events are modeled as a Poisson process whose intensity factorizes through a non-negative B-spline basis, and a simple estimation procedure recovers interpretable temporal templates shared across entities. The resulting method is mathematically principled, easy to implement, and computationally efficient. We further show that standard binned-count approaches arise as the special case of degree-zero splines, explore bias-variance tradeoffs and compare against existing methods on a synthetic latent factor model, and demonstrate the effectiveness of EventNMF on several real-world applications.

### [114] [Tracing the Oracle: Improving Diffusion Timestep Scheduling for 3D CT Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06236)
*Yujia Wu,Zhaoqiang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 3D CT 重建中扩散模型推理效率低与采样误差大的问题，本文提出 TrO 框架，利用动态规划优化时间步调度，在极少采样步数下实现了高精度的重建结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练扩散模型在解决 3D CT 反问题时表现出色，但推理过程计算开销巨大。现有的均匀时间步调度方案无法捕捉扩散模型反向随机微分方程的非均匀演化特性，从而导致严重的截断误差。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Tracing the Oracle (TrO) 的即插即用框架。该方法首先通过对少量样本进行密集采样以构建“参考预言（oracle）”，随后利用动态规划算法在全局范围内最小化少步近似与预言之间的累积误差，从而得出最优的时间步调度策略，将采样步数精准分配至对截断误差最敏感的演化阶段。

Result: 在 AAPM 数据集上的 3D CT 重建任务中，TrO 框架配合现有的 DDS 方法，与启发式调度方案相比，在极其受限的采样步数（≤10步）下，显著提升了重建保真度和计算效率。

Conclusion: TrO 框架通过动态规划实现了最优的时间步调度，解决了扩散模型在 3D CT 重建任务中因步数限制导致的截断误差问题，在保证计算效率的同时显著提升了重建质量。

Abstract: Pretrained diffusion models demonstrate impressive potential in solving highly ill-posed 3D computed tomography (CT) inverse problems, while the inference process suffers from significant computational overhead. Furthermore, existing uniform timestep schedules fail to capture the non-uniform evolution of the reverse conditional diffusion stochastic differential equation, thereby introducing substantial truncation errors. To overcome this limitation, we propose Tracing the Oracle (TrO), a plug-and-play framework for improved timestep scheduling. Specifically, we treat densely sampled numerical integration trajectories on a few samples as the reference oracle. The optimized schedule is extracted by leveraging dynamic programming to globally minimize the cumulative error between the few-step approximation and the oracle. This mechanism precisely allocates the limited sampling steps to critical evolution stages that are highly susceptible to truncation errors. Our extensive experiments on the AAPM dataset across multiple 3D CT reconstruction tasks demonstrate that, when combined with the state-of-the-art 3D CT reconstruction method DDS, our optimized timesteps significantly improve reconstruction fidelity and computational efficiency compared to existing heuristic schedules, especially under a strict budget of no more than 10 sampling steps.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）的生成过程缺乏明确的统计物理描述。本文旨在通过统计场论的方法探究LLM生成文本时的集体统计结构，并理解解码策略（如温度调节）与相变现象之间的联系。

Method: 将LLM的Token嵌入视为一维链上的连续自旋变量，定义了基于双点关联函数的磁化率和基于系综平均嵌入场的序参量。通过调节softmax温度（T），分析磁化率峰值、序参量变化及语义方向坍缩，并利用最近邻（TwoNN）方法估算内在维度进行交叉验证。

Result: 研究发现模型在特征温度 $T_c$ 附近表现出尖锐的磁化率峰值和序参量剧烈变化，且在 $T_c$ 以下发生向单一语义方向的坍缩。内在维度分析证实了 $T_c$ 附近的系统状态转变。这些现象在不同规模的模型（Qwen3: 0.6B--32B）中具有稳健性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统计场论框架来分析LLM的文本生成过程，揭示了LLM在解码过程中存在类似于相变的临界现象。这一发现为定量评估大模型的生成统计特性及解码策略提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We propose a statistical-field framework for text generated by large language models (LLMs), treating token embeddings as continuous spin variables on a one-dimensional chain. Defining a susceptibility from the connected two-point correlator and an order parameter from the ensemble-averaged embedding field, we vary the \texttt{softmax} temperature $T$ and observe a sharp susceptibility peak near a characteristic $T_c$ with power-law-like scaling, a concurrent rapid change in the order parameter, and a collapse onto a single semantic direction below $T_c$. The intrinsic dimension estimated by the two nearest neighbor (TwoNN) method independently corroborates these findings, reaching a minimum near $T_c$. Results are robust across model scales (Qwen3: 0.6B--32B) and prompt categories. While the phenomenology closely resembles a continuous phase transition, the non-equilibrium nature of autoregressive generation warrants further investigation. Our framework provides quantitative tools for probing the collective statistical structure of LLM outputs and suggests connections between decoding strategies and critical phenomena.

### [116] [Your GFlowNet Secretly Learns an Optimal Transport Plan](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06272)

TL;DR: 本文建立了非循环GFlowNets与最优传输（OT）理论的数学联系，证明了最小流GFlowNet可用于求解图上的最优传输问题，并提供了一种基于神经网络的可扩展求解方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的最优传输（OT）求解算法在处理大规模图结构时往往面临计算复杂度的挑战。作者旨在利用GFlowNets这种通过随机轨迹采样结构化对象的框架，为解决图上的最优传输问题提供一种新的、可扩展的参数化学习范式。

Method: 研究者建立并论证了非循环GFlowNets与最优传输（OT）问题之间的数学等价性。具体而言，通过固定初始流分布，将GFlowNet的优化目标转化为基于图上最短路径代价的Kantorovich OT问题，并利用神经网络对边流进行参数化以在大规模图上进行求解。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法求解的结果与精确的OT求解器高度一致。通过将GFlowNet策略视为最优传输计划，研究证明了该框架能够有效地学习并恢复高质量的传输耦合，且具备处理大规模图数据的潜力。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将非循环GFlowNets与最优传输（OT）理论联系起来，证明了最小流GFlowNet的优化目标等价于图上的Kantorovich OT问题。这一发现为在大规模图结构上求解OT问题提供了一种高效的深度学习方法，扩展了GFlowNets的应用边界。

Abstract: Generative Flow Networks (GFlowNets) are a framework for sampling structured objects via stochastic trajectories in a directed graph. In this work, we establish a theoretical connection between non-acyclic GFlowNets and optimal transport (OT). We show that fixing the initial flow distribution in a minimum-flow GFlowNet reduces its objective to a Kantorovich OT problem with graph-induced shortest path costs. At the optimum, the learned GFlowNet policy therefore encodes an optimal transport plan from the source distribution to the target distribution: we show that sampling trajectories from the minimum-flow GFlowNet recovers the corresponding optimal coupling. Our formulation enables applying the GFlowNet learning framework to OT problems on large graphs via edge flows and neural parameterization. Experiments confirm agreement with exact OT solvers and demonstrate that GFlowNets can learn high-quality transport plans.

### [117] [PAC-Bayesian Adversarially Robust Generalization for Message Passing Graph Neural Networks: A Sensitivity Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06293)
*Ziling Liang,Xinping Yi,Qingsong Wen,Shi Jin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个针对图神经网络（MPGNNs）的改进型PAC-Bayesian泛化分析框架，通过利用雅可比矩阵的低秩性质和各向异性高斯后验，成功推导出了更紧致的鲁棒泛化界，解决了现有方法过于依赖网络宽度的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对图神经网络（GNN）鲁棒泛化的PAC-Bayesian分析通常采用各向同性高斯后验分布，并在全参数空间控制扰动，导致其泛化界过于依赖隐藏层宽度且不够紧致。作者旨在通过捕获异构参数敏感性来改进这一理论框架，以获得更紧致的鲁棒泛化界。

Method: 本文将敏感度感知PAC-Bayesian框架扩展至MPGNNs。首先通过推导输出对权重参数的雅可比矩阵来量化不同参数块的敏感度；其次，利用分类任务中雅可比矩阵的秩约束（秩最多为K），构造了雅可比对齐的敏感度矩阵；最后，采用优化协方差的各向异性高斯后验分布来紧致化KL散度项。

Result: 实验和理论分析表明，该方法将泛化界中的主要维度因子从隐藏层宽度降低为类别数K，显著提升了泛化界的紧致性，能够更准确地反映模型在对抗环境下的鲁棒性，并为设计更鲁棒的MPGNN模型提供了理论指导。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种针对消息传递图神经网络（MPGNNs）的敏感度感知PAC-Bayesian分析框架。通过利用雅可比矩阵的秩约束，并使用各向异性高斯后验分布，本文有效地降低了泛化界对隐藏层宽度的依赖，使其与类别数相关，从而为理解和提升GNN的鲁棒性提供了更紧密的理论保障。

Abstract: Whilst the vulnerability of graph neural networks (GNNs) to adversarial attacks poses a critical threat to graph representation learning, the understanding of the robust generalization behavior remains a fundamental challenge in the adversarial setting. Recently, PAC-Bayesian margin-based generalization analysis substantially advances this line of research by providing a flexible and data-dependent analytical framework. However, existing robust analyses often rely on isotropic Gaussian posteriors and control weight perturbations in the full parameter space, which limits the ability to capture heterogeneous parameter sensitivity yet hinges on hidden-width-dependent complexity terms, resulting in not-tight-enough generalization bounds. In this paper, we extend a recently proposed sensitivity-aware PAC-Bayesian framework from deep neural networks to message passing GNNs (MPGNNs) and derive a tighter robust generalization bound in the adversarial setting. Specifically, we first quantify how sensitive the perturbations across different parameter blocks are to the network outputs by deriving the output Jacobians with respect to the weight parameters. Exploiting the fact that these Jacobian matrices have rank at most $K$ in $K$-class graph classification, we then construct Jacobian-aligned sensitivity matrices and use anisotropic Gaussian posteriors with optimized covariances to upper bound the KL divergence in a tight way. Notably, by refining the spectral-norm dependence on the learned weights and reducing the leading dimension factor from hidden-width-dependent terms to the number of classes $K$, our analysis yields much tighter robust generalization guarantees for MPGNNs, thereby guiding their designs to enhance adversarial robustness.

### [118] [Staged Factorial Screening for Budget-Constrained Micro-Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05186)
*Felipe Chavarro Polania*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在预算受限的微预训练场景下，如何在投入大量计算资源前，通过有限的尝试快速筛选出有效的模型配置（配方），是该研究的主要动机。旨在探究分阶段因子设计工作流是否能在早期阶段准确识别稳定的参数效应结构。

Method: 采用分阶段的部分因子设计（staged fractional-factorial workflow）进行实验。通过在单一GPU环境下运行613次实验，涵盖不同计算预算（2、5、10分钟）、全条件重跑、锚点验证、贪婪/随机基准测试及长周期（24小时）的锚点延续实验，并使用Benjamini-Hochberg校正来评估参数效应的稳定性。

Result: 短期预算（5-10分钟）下，部分参数（D, A, B, C）表现出统计学上显著的效应；随机搜索虽然能找到较好的配置，但缺乏因子归因能力。长周期实验表明，“桥接模型”在不同硬件上均表现出最低的样本均值，且模型排序具有硬件敏感性，证明了基于桥接模型的微预训练策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究提出了针对资源受限环境下微预训练（micro-pretraining）的高效方法论：利用短期设计实验筛选高惩罚方向，通过重复运行验证锚点（anchor），并在缩减后的空间内进行局部优化。研究强调了以“桥接模型（bridge model）”为核心的策略在不同硬件环境下具有稳健性，而非追求硬件无关的排名或通用超参数优化的全面领先。

Abstract: Budget-constrained micro-pretraining often requires triaging many candidate recipes on a shared accelerator before larger search budgets are spent. We study whether a staged fractional-factorial workflow can recover stable early effect structure in this setting. On a fixed autoresearch-derived single-GPU training loop, we run 613 experiments across pilot and follow-up screens at 2, 5, and 10 minutes; full 16-condition seeded reruns at 5 and 10 minutes; targeted seeded anchor checks; same-host greedy and matched-cost random baselines; a 60-minute bridge package; and bounded Windows A100 and Linux L40S anchor continuations through 24 hours. Main penalties from total batch, depth, and width are largest at short budgets and relax as budget increases. Within the predeclared seeded full-screen families, D, A, B, and C retain non-zero estimates at 5 and 10 minutes after within-budget Benjamini-Hochberg correction, while E does not. Random search can reach strong incumbents in this 32-condition space, but repeatedly in the same low-penalty region and without factor attribution. The 60-minute bridge anchor has the lowest mean, although that package does not separate workflow refinement from the larger bridge model's capacity advantage. In bounded 12-hour and 24-hour three-anchor continuations on both hosts, the bridge has the lowest sample mean while the non-bridge ordering stays host-sensitive. We therefore present a bounded methods result: use short designed screens to identify high-penalty directions, confirm promising anchors under repeated runs, and refine locally inside the reduced space. The evidence supports a bridge-centered recommendation through 24 hours on two hosts, not hardware-invariant ranking or general hyperparameter-optimization superiority.
