### [119] [Reactive Flux Matching: Mechanism Discovery and Adaptive Sampling of Rare Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06295)
*Rishal Aggarwal,David Ryan Koes,Nicholas M. Boffi,Eric Vanden-Eijnden*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Flux Matching 是一种无需动力学先验信息，通过机器学习从反应轨迹中直接提取主导路径（电流速度）和反应坐标（标量势）的框架，有效解决了复杂分子系统中反应机制提取和非马尔可夫投影下的建模难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管路径采样方法能够生成连接亚稳态的反应轨迹集合，但从这些复杂数据中提取清晰、可解释的反应机制依然非常困难。现有的基于承诺函数（committor-based）的方法在投影到非马尔可夫集体变量时往往失效，因此亟需一种更稳健且无需模型假设的分析框架。

Method: 引入了一种名为“通量匹配”（Flux Matching）的框架。该方法通过加权 Helmholtz-Hodge 分解，从反应轨迹数据中学习两个核心对象：一是刻画主导反应路径的“电流速度”场 $u(z)$；二是作为数据驱动反应坐标的“标量势” $h(z)$。这两个对象通过最小化类似于生成模型中流匹配（flow matching）的二次泛函来求解，无需系统动力学或平稳分布的先验知识。

Result: 验证结果表明，Flux Matching 能够准确生成电流速度轨迹，并有效应用于分子系统的速率常数计算。此外，其求得的标量势水平集可用于构建自适应接口，从而显著提升增强采样算法的效率。

Conclusion: Flux Matching 框架通过从反应轨迹数据中直接学习当前速度和反应坐标，为分子动力学中的机制分析和增强采样提供了一种鲁棒的、无需预先假设动力学模型的通用工具，在处理非马尔可夫投影时仍能保持有效性。

Abstract: Path sampling methods generate ensembles of reactive trajectories connecting metastable states, but extracting mechanistic insight from these data remains nontrivial. We introduce Flux Matching, a framework that learns two complementary objects directly from reactive trajectory data: a current velocity $u(z)$, whose streamlines trace the dominant reaction pathways, and a scalar potential $h(z)$, obtained from a weighted Helmholtz-Hodge decomposition of the reactive current, that serves as a data-driven reaction coordinate. Both minimize quadratic functionals over the reactive path ensemble, analogous to the flow matching loss in generative modeling, and require no knowledge of the underlying dynamics or stationary distribution. Unlike committor-based methods, $u$ and $h$ remain well-defined under projection onto non-Markovian collective variables, and their level sets in turn provide adaptive interfaces for improved sampling with enhanced sampling methods. Flux Matching is validated through the generation of current velocity trajectories and rate constant calculations on molecular systems.

We find that the geometry of time horizon is encoded in the residual stream at the expected localized layers. A behavioral analysis reveals that unintervened LLMs discount the future several times less steeply than humans, yet this preference is unstable across contexts, motivating explicit control rather than implicit reliance on training. Finally, we find suggestive evidence that steering vectors can shift temporal preference. Our work demonstrates how mechanistic interpretability can bring us closer to reliable control over how LLMs plan and reason

### [121] [Tangram: Unlocking Non-Uniform KV Cache for Efficient Multi-turn LLM Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06302)
*Hyungmin Kim,Minsoo Kim,Hongseok Kim,Jungwook Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Tangram 是一款专为非均匀 KV 缓存压缩设计的 LLM 推理系统，通过确定性预算分配、头组页面管理及提前（AOT）负载均衡技术，有效解决了非均匀压缩带来的系统级效率问题，显著提升了推理吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮 LLM 推理中 KV 缓存的线性增长给 GPU 内存和带宽带来了巨大压力。尽管非均匀 KV 压缩可以保留更多关键信息，但在现有系统中会引发内存碎片化、调度复杂以及内核利用率降低等严重性能问题，Tangram 旨在解决这些系统级效率瓶颈。

Method: Tangram 采用了三种核心技术：(1) 确定性预算分配：基于注意力头的固有模式分配静态内存，消除动态调度开销；(2) 头组页面管理：将具有相似保留需求的目标头进行聚类，并利用向量化页表管理，实现高效的内存回收；(3) 提前（AOT）负载均衡：利用静态预算配置文件，无需运行时开销即可实现均匀的 GPU 利用率。

Result: 实验结果表明，与现有基准系统相比，Tangram 在完全保持模型准确性的前提下，将服务吞吐量提升了最高 2.6 倍。

Conclusion: Tangram 成功解决了非均匀 KV 缓存压缩在系统实现层面的挑战，证明了通过确定性的资源管理和静态优化策略，可以在保持模型精度的前提下，显著提升多轮对话 LLM 的服务吞吐量。

Abstract: Multi-turn Large Language Model (LLM) serving is critical for consistent user experiences, yet the linear growth of the Key-Value (KV) cache imposes significant pressure on GPU memory and bandwidth. Non-uniform KV compression effectively preserves more information by considering the individual importance of each KV cache. However, such KV cache heterogeneity introduces various systemic challenges - including memory fragmentation, scheduling complexities, and diminished kernel utilization - which collectively lead to significant inefficiencies in existing LLM serving systems.
  To overcome these challenges, we present Tangram, a novel serving system designed to make Non-uniform KV caches practical. Tangram addresses systemic inefficiencies through three core techniques: (1) Deterministic Budget Allocation assigns a static memory footprint to each head based on its intrinsic pattern, entirely eliminating dynamic scheduling overhead and prefill stalls; (2) Head Group Page clusters attention heads with similar retention demands and manages them with independent, vectorized page tables, thereby maximizing physical memory reclamation; and (3) Ahead-of-Time (AOT) Load Balancing leverages static budget profiles to ensure uniform GPU utilization without runtime overhead. Experimental results show that Tangram improves throughput by up to 2.6x compared to existing baselines, while fully preserving model accuracy. Our implementation is publicly available at https://github.com/aiha-lab/TANGRAM.

</details>


### [122] [Statistically Reliable LLM-Based Ranking Evaluation via Prediction-Powered Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05308)
*Abhishek Divekar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PRECISE 是一种将少量人工标注与大规模 LLM 判决相结合的评估框架，通过 PPI 技术确保偏差校正，在降低排查评估成本的同时，显著提高了评估指标（如 Precision@K）的统计精度，并在生产环境测试中表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在排名系统评估中，高质量的人工标注获取成本极高，而单纯依赖 LLM 判决可能存在系统性偏差。作者旨在通过结合少量人类反馈和大量低成本的 LLM 评估，在减少估计偏差和标准误差的同时，降低标注成本并保持评估的统计严谨性。

Method: 提出 PRECISE 框架，扩展了“预测驱动推断”（PPI），将少量高质量人工标注与大规模 LLM 判决相结合，通过修正偏差来评估排名指标。此外，针对分层指标（如 Precision@K），将输出空间的计算复杂度从 O(2^|C|) 降低至 O(2^K)，从而使其适用于实际评估场景。

Result: 在 ESCI 基准测试中，使用 30 个真值数据配合 Claude 3 Sonnet，将 Precision@4 的标准误差降低了 21%。在生产环境部署中，利用 100 个真值数据即可准确排序系统变体，并在 A/B 测试中实现了日销售额 407 个基点的增长。

Conclusion: PRECISE 提供了一种高效、鲁棒的方法来评估排名系统，通过结合人类标注和 LLM 判决，在保证统计无偏性的同时显著提高了评估的精度。该方法成功克服了传统标注成本高昂的问题，并在实际生产场景中得到了验证。

Abstract: With PRECISE, we extended Prediction-Powered Inference to produce bias-corrected estimates of ranking evaluation metrics by combining a small human-labeled set with a large LLM-judged set. PPI is provably unbiased regardless of the LLM judge's error profile. We make it applicable to hierarchical metrics like Precision@K, where annotations are per-document but the metric is per-query, by reducing the output-space computation from O(2^|C|) to O(2^K). On the ESCI benchmark, augmenting 30 human annotations with Claude 3 Sonnet judgments reduces the standard error of Precision@4 estimates from 4.45 to 3.50 (a 21% relative reduction). In a production system, our framework correctly identified the best of three system variants from 100 human labels and 2 hours of domain-expert annotation; A/B testing confirmed this ranking with +407 bps in daily sales.

Abstract: Controllable generation with discrete diffusion models is often hindered by high computational overhead or the need for retraining. ### [124] [Learning What to Forget: Improving LLM Unlearning via Learned Token-Level Importance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06320)
*Gizem Yüce,Giorgos Nikolaou,Nicolas Flammarion*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 ATWU 的机器遗忘方法，通过联合优化模型参数与标记权重，利用“保留冲突”准则无监督地识别并移除语言模型中特定的遗忘标记，在保持模型性能的同时实现了高效的知识消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器遗忘方法在处理自回归语言模型时，通常忽视了样本内不同标记对遗忘贡献的差异（异质性），或过度依赖辅助模型、启发式规则及外部标注，导致遗忘效果与模型通用能力保持之间的权衡不佳。

Method: 提出了一种交替标记加权遗忘（ATWU）框架。该方法通过联合优化模型参数和标记权重，根据“遗忘目标与保留目标之间的冲突程度”来定义标记的遗忘特异性（forget-specificity），并利用隐藏状态上的简单线性评分器进行计算。

Result: 在 TOFU 和 RWKU 数据集上的实验证明，ATWU 在遗忘-保留权衡方面达到了最先进水平，显著优于样本级方法及其他基于启发式或辅助模型的方案。此外，ATWU 学习到的评分与真实的遗忘语义片段高度一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于“保留冲突”（retain conflict）的标准是识别语言模型遗忘内容的高效准则，无需外部监督即可实现对遗忘标记重要性的无监督学习，且计算开销极小。

Abstract: Machine unlearning aims to remove targeted knowledge from a trained model while preserving its general capabilities. For autoregressive language models, not all tokens in a forget sample are equally relevant to forgetting. Existing approaches either ignore this heterogeneity or rely on auxiliary models, heuristics, or external annotations to estimate each token's relevance for forgetting. We instead characterize it through the interaction with the retain objective: a token is forget-specific to the extent that minimizing the forget loss on that token does not conflict with retain optimality. We formalize this perspective as a joint optimization problem over the model parameters and the token weights and show that, under a natural separation condition, the resulting objective recovers the oracle forget-specific token support. Motivated by this formulation, we introduce Alternating Token-Weighted Unlearning (ATWU), a lightweight framework that jointly learns token forget-specificity and model parameters during unlearning using a simple linear scorer over the hidden states, without external token level supervision. Across TOFU and RWKU, ATWU achieves state of the art forget-retain trade-offs, outperforming sample-level methods, probability-based token weighting heuristics, and auxiliary-model-based approaches. Moreover, the learned scores align substantially better with ground truth forget-specific spans, indicating that ATWU identifies semantically meaningful token level forgetting signals. Overall, our results suggest that retain conflict provides an effective criterion for identifying what language models should forget, enabling unsupervised learning of token level forget-specificity directly from model representations with minimal computational overhead.

### [125] [PAMF: Prior-Aware Multimodal Fusion for Incomplete Time Series Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06328)
*Ziwen Kan,Wugeng Zheng,Tianlong Chen,Song Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在多个医疗多模态时间序列基准测试中，PAMF 均表现出了最强的下游任务预测性能，且在处理多样化的缺失场景下均优于现有的各类基准模型。

Abstract: In healthcare, multimodal time series tasks often operate on incomplete observations in practice, for example when ECG segments are lost because electrodes detach or an entire respiratory channel is unavailable during overnight monitoring. Such missingness typically appears in two structurally distinct patterns: within-modality missing, where values are absent within an otherwise observed modality, and modality-level missing, where an entire modality is unavailable. Existing methods typically represent unobserved data implicitly through masks or missing embeddings, without learning instance-specific missing information, and most are designed for only one missingness pattern. A natural approach is to explicitly estimate the missing data; however, existing imputation methods treat missingness uniformly despite their different structural priors, and the imputation process is often isolated from downstream tasks, preventing downstream tasks from guiding imputation toward more informative representations. To address these limitations, we present PAMF, a multimodal time-series framework that explicitly handles different missingness patterns while coupling imputation with downstream prediction through prior-aware flow matching and weight sharing. Specifically, the method initializes the flow-matching source state with type-specific priors to distinguish two missing types. It further connects imputation and classification through architecturally matched encoders with weight sharing, transferring task-relevant representations into the imputation process. Experiments on multiple multimodal healthcare time-series benchmarks show that the proposed method achieves the strongest overall downstream performance across diverse datasets and missing settings compared with existing baselines.

### [126] [Efficient Mean Curvature Computation on High-Dimensional Data Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06329)
*Alexandre L. M. Levada*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的局部平均曲率估计方法，通过代数优化和SVD近似技术，将计算复杂度从O(m⁴)显著降低，在保持高精度的同时实现了在大规模高维数据集上的快速计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的局部平均曲率估计方法（如MCBP）在处理高维数据集时，由于需要显式构造矩阵并进行全特征值分解，计算复杂度高达O(m⁴)，导致算法在大维数数据集上难以扩展。作者旨在寻找一种更高效的数学推导，以降低计算开销，使曲率特征在现代机器学习任务中具备可扩展性。

Method: 提出了两种互补的改进方案：一是通过代数恒等式消除显式构造矩阵H的过程，将计算复杂度降至O(m²)，减少了对协方差矩阵的依赖；二是针对特征值分解的O(m³)瓶颈，利用截断SVD（O(k²m)）处理局部协方差矩阵，并结合Haar测度下的外积期望值对零空间特征向量进行解析近似。整体算法复杂度优化为O(k²m + kmp²)。

Result: 在真实数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法比原实现方案提速50至300倍，且在替换原算法后精度损失可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 本文提出的高效曲率估计方法成功解决了高维数据集局部平均曲率计算的计算瓶颈，使得曲率特征能够在大规模机器学习任务中得到实际应用，极大地提升了计算效率且几乎不损失精度。

Abstract: Estimating local mean curvature at each point of a high-dimensional dataset is a key ingredient of geometry-aware machine learning algorithms, such as the Mean Curvature Boundary Points (MCBP) method. The naive implementation of this computation, based on a local shape operator approximated from k-nearest neighbor patches, involves an explicit construction of a matrix $H$ whose trace form yields an $O(m^4)$ cost per point, rendering the approach intractable for datasets with more than a few dozen features. This paper introduces two complementary contributions that together reduce this cost by several orders of magnitude. The first contribution is an exact algebraic identity. This identity, derived from the orthogonality of the eigenvectors of the covariance matrix and the cyclicity of the trace operator, eliminates $H$ entirely and reduces the per-point cost to $O(m^2)$ after the eigendecomposition. The second contribution addresses the remaining $O(m^3)$ bottleneck of the full eigendecomposition. Since the local covariance matrix has rank at most $k-1 \ll m$, we replace it with a truncated SVD of the $k \times m$ centered data matrix, an $O(k^2 m)$ operation, and derive an analytical approximation for the contribution of the null-space eigenvectors based on the expected value of their outer product under the Haar measure. The resulting estimator has total cost $O(k^2 m + k m p^2)$, where $p = k-1$. Experiments on real-world datasets confirm speedups of 50 to 300 times relative to the original implementation, with negligible loss when the fast estimator is used to replace the original version. By providing a scalable and data-driven estimate of local curvature, the proposed method establishes curvature as a practical geometric feature for a broad range of machine learning tasks, from classical to modern deep learning pipelines.

</details>


### [127] [Subspace-Aware Sparse Autoencoders for Effective Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06333)
*Seyed Arshan Dalili,Mehrdad Mahdavi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出传统稀疏自编码器因强制将多维特征拆解为一维向量而产生“特征分裂”现象。为此提出了子空间感知稀疏自编码器（SASA），通过建模多维子空间而非单一向量，解决了特征碎片化问题，在提高模型可解释性的同时显著提升了训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的稀疏自编码器（SAE）假设特征是一维的（单个解码向量），这与大语言模型中特征的多维本质不符，导致了特征分裂（feature splitting）现象——即一个真实的特征被拆分成多个共线性的潜变量，不仅增加了计算代价，也严重干扰了机械可解释性研究。

Method: 提出子空间感知稀疏自编码器（Subspace-Aware Sparse Autoencoders, SASA）。该方法使用 learned decoder subspaces 代替单一向量解码器，引入 Top-s 分组门控机制（Group Gating）实现块稀疏，并通过核范数正则化（nuclear-norm regularizer）来自动调整每个组的有效秩，以匹配特征的内在维度。

Result: 理论上，SASA 将特征重构的样本复杂度从指数级降为多项式级；实验上，在 GPT-2 和 Mistral-7B 上，SASA 在减少特征分裂和吸收的同时，提升了特征的单义性，且在仅需一半训练数据的情况下达到了优于标准 SAE 的性能表现。

Conclusion: SASA通过引入子空间解码器和块稀疏约束，成功克服了传统稀疏自编码器（SAE）中特征分裂的几何与优化缺陷。该方法不仅在理论上证明了能以多项式样本复杂度恢复高维特征，且在LLM的实际应用中显著提升了特征的单义性与可解释性，同时提高了训练效率。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) are widely used for mechanistic interpretability in large language models, yet their formulation assigns each latent feature a single decoder direction, implicitly assuming features to be one-dimensional. We show that this assumption mismatches with the multi-dimensional structure of model features, provably inducing feature splitting through two distinct mechanisms. Geometrically, reconstructing a feature of intrinsic dimension $d_i \ge 2$ to error $\varepsilon$ with single-direction decoders forces a number of atoms that is exponential in $d_i$. From an end-to-end optimization perspective, this splitting is not merely possible but actively preferred. We prove that there exists a continuous path from the true $d_i$-dimensional basis to a strictly lower risk of the $\ell_1$-regularized SAE objective, whose descent directions drive any trained dictionary into that exponential regime. A single coherent feature is therefore fragmented across many near-collinear latents, producing spurious multiplicity and obscuring the intrinsic geometry. Motivated by this, we introduce Subspace-Aware Sparse Autoencoders (SASA), which replace single-vector decoders with learned decoder subspaces, enforce block sparsity via Top-$s$ group gating, and adapt each group's effective rank with a nuclear-norm regularizer. We then show that once the block size satisfies $r \ge d_i$, a single group not only can represent the entire feature slice but is the global minimizer of the SASA objective. This consolidation yields a sample complexity polynomial in $d_i$ rather than exponential -- a decisive advantage given that every training activation costs an LLM forward pass. Empirically, on GPT-2 and Mistral-7B, SASA reduces feature splitting and absorption, improves monosemanticity and interpretability, and matches or exceeds standard SAEs while training on roughly half the token budget.

### [128] [Quantifying the Privacy of Counterfactuals by Leveraging Membership Inference Attacks Against Synthetic Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06334)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然反事实解释有助于提升机器学习模型决策的可解释性，但这类解释可能被攻击者利用，通过反事实数据反向推断出原始训练集中的成员信息，从而造成隐私泄露。本文旨在揭示这种潜在的攻击路径。

Method: 研究人员利用针对合成数据的成员推理攻击方法，评估了其在反事实数据上的有效性；并进一步提出了即便在无法直接访问目标模型、仅拥有反事实数据集合的情况下，依然可以成功实施成员推理攻击的分析方法。

Result: 实验结果表明，针对合成数据设计的成员推理攻击同样适用于反事实数据。此外，即便攻击者无法访问模型，仅依靠收集到的反事实样本集，依然能有效地进行成员推理攻击，证明了反事实解释在隐私保护方面的脆弱性。

Abstract: Counterfactuals are typically used in high-stakes decision areas to explain a machine learning model by showing how changes to the user profiles result in the desired outcome. However, explaining the model's decisions through counterfactuals can also be exploited by an adversary to conduct privacy attacks against the model or its training data. Drawing on the analogy that counterfactuals provide realistic substitutes for real training data, similar to synthetic data, we demonstrate in this paper how it is possible to successfully perform privacy attacks on counterfactuals by drawing on the attacks developed against synthetic data. More precisely, we investigate the effectiveness of the membership inference attacks designed for synthetic data on various types of counterfactuals. Additionally, while existing membership inference attacks against counterfactuals usually require to be able to query the model, we show how it is possible to perform successful membership inference attacks using only a set of counterfactuals, with no access to the model from which they are generated. Our results demonstrate that model developers should be more cautious when releasing counterfactuals to various users, as it can lead to a privacy breach.

### [129] [Bridging Domain Expertise and Generalization for Performance Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06335)
*Shuxuan Li,Zhilin Zhao,Quyu Kong,Wei-Shi Zheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对分布偏移场景下模型性能难以准确评估的问题，本文提出了 FRAP 方法。通过融合外部基础模型与基准模型的预测信息，FRAP 构建了更可靠的参考基准，显著提升了在无标签测试集上的模型性能估计效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分布偏移（Distribution Shift）场景下，现有模型性能评估方法仅依赖模型自身的预测输出。然而，当面临分布偏移时，这些模型自身的偏差会被放大，导致其预测输出与真实性能之间的相关性减弱，无法实现准确的无标签性能估计。

Method: 提出了一种名为“融合参考对齐预测”（Fused Reference Alignment Prediction, FRAP）的方法。该方法首先通过温度缩放校准（Temperature-scaled calibration）最小化外部基础模型与基准模型预测分布之间的差异；随后，利用基于置信度的加权机制将两者的预测融合为“参考分布”；最后，通过衡量基准模型预测与该参考分布的契合度来评估性能。

Result: 在多个不同的数据集和架构上进行的广泛实验表明，与现有的主流性能评估方法相比，FRAP 在分布偏移环境下能够实现一致且显著的性能评估准确度提升。

Conclusion: FRAP 通过融合基础模型（Foundation Model）的鲁棒性与基准模型（Base Model）的领域专业知识，提供了一种在分布偏移下更准确、更可靠的模型性能评估框架。该方法有效地克服了仅依赖基准模型预测所带来的偏差放大问题。

Abstract: Performance estimation under distribution shift aims to predict how a model behaves on an unlabeled test set whose distribution differs from the training data, a scenario that requires reliable indicators that can faithfully reflect model behavior without ground-truth labels. Existing approaches rely solely on the outputs of the given model whose biases are amplified once the distribution shifts, weakening the correlation with the true performance. Motivated by this limitation, we propose Fused Reference Alignment Prediction (FRAP), which leverages the complementary strengths of an external foundation model and the base model to construct a more reliable surrogate of the ground-truth labels. FRAP aligns the prediction distribution of the foundation model with that of the base model by applying temperature-scaled calibration that minimizes their divergence. The aligned predictions are fused through confidence-based weighting into a refined reference distribution that integrates robustness from the foundation model and domain-specific expertise from the base model, and performance estimation is obtained by measuring how closely the base model predictions agree with this reference. Extensive experiments across diverse datasets and architectures show that FRAP provides consistent and substantial improvements over representative performance-estimation methods under distribution shift.

### [130] [Less is MoE: Trimming Experts in Domain-Specialist Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05538)
*Haoze He,Xinkai Zou,Xuan Jiang,Xingyuan Ding,Ao Qu,Juncheng Billy Li,Heather Miller*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种针对MoE模型的Fisher-MoE压缩技术，通过识别并保留FFN中对任务至关重要的中间维度，在实现显著模型压缩与加速的同时，成功解决了现有压缩方法导致通用任务性能失效的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的MoE模型压缩方法在处理通用任务时往往会造成灾难性的性能下降。研究发现，这是因为传统方法忽略了模型能力分布的粒度，导致关键能力在专家级剪枝中被误删，而这些能力实际上高度集中在FFN稀疏的中间维度中。

Method: 提出了一种名为Fisher-MoE的压缩框架。该方法跳出传统的专家级剪枝，转而深入到FFN内部的中间维度层级，利用Fisher重要性指标对这些维度进行排序并剔除。相较于基于激活值、路由分数或权重大小的基线方法，Fisher重要性能更精准地识别任务关键维度。

Result: 在保持相同50%的压缩比下，Fisher-MoE显著优于现有方法。它在维持模型性能的同时，减少了约45%的权重内存占用，并将推理吞吐量提高了21%。实验证明，即使仅删除极少数关键维度也会导致特定任务性能崩塌，验证了该粒度划分的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，FFN中间维度是MoE模型中能力分布的核心单元。通过基于Fisher重要性的维度级剪枝，可以在保持模型核心能力的同时，显著降低模型权重大小并提升推理吞吐量，为大规模MoE模型的轻量化部署提供了高效路径。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models achieve strong performance through conditional computation, but their large parameter footprint poses deployment challenges. Prior MoE compression approaches catastrophically fail when evaluated on general-purpose benchmarks beyond commonsense reasoning. We trace this failure to the granularity of compression: important capabilities are distributed across experts but concentrated in FFN sparse intermediate dimensions. To identify these dimensions, we use Fisher importance which outperforms activation-, router-score-, and magnitude-based alternatives, and identifies tiny sets of task-critical dimensions: in Qwen1.5-MoE, removing as few as 12 of 1.35M routed-FFN intermediate dimensions collapses GSM8K accuracy while largely preserving factual-knowledge performance. Building on this, we propose Fisher-MoE, which operates within FFN to remove intermediate dimensions ranked by Fisher importance. At the same 50% MoE compression ratio, Fisher-MoE preserves model capability, while reducing weight memory by ~45% and improving inference throughput by 21%. These findings suggest intermediate dimension granularity is an effective unit for both compression and ranking where capability concentrates in MoE models.

</details>


### [131] [Equivariant Neural Belief Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06344)
*Zehua Cheng,Wei Dai,Jiahao Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了等变神经置信传播（ENBP），解决了现有等变网络无法处理高阶张量和多模态不确定性的问题，在分子构象生成和多体机器人推断中实现了极高的计算效率、准确性和物理一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的等变网络通常只能处理标量和向量，无法表示各向异性的不确定性（需要秩2精度张量）。此外，单分量消息传递导致多模态能量景观塌陷，无法表示复杂的概率分布。因此，需要一种能够保持SE(3)对称性并具备处理复杂概率分布能力的神经网络框架。

Method: 提出等变神经置信传播（ENBP），这是一种基于因子图的框架。其核心方法包括：1. 使用等变高斯混合模型作为消息传递单元，其充分统计量在SE(3)下精确变换；2. 通过等变外积构建秩2精度矩阵；3. 利用可微谱分解处理精度矩阵；4. 采用与SE(3)可交换的贪婪KL散度混合模型约简算法，以保证计算的可控性。

Result: 在GEOM-QM9和GEOM-Drugs数据集上，ENBP实现了98.9%的构象覆盖率，误差仅为0.090埃，推理速度比扩散模型基线快100倍以上；在多体机器人推断任务中，传统BP算法在15个智能体时发散，而ENBP保持收敛且碰撞率极低，等变误差达到机器精度水平（~10⁻⁷）。

Conclusion: ENBP成功将等变神经网络与因子图推理相结合，为处理空间嵌入变量的概率推断提供了一种高效、高精度且满足SE(3)对称性的新方法。它不仅在分子构象生成中显著提升了速度与准确度，还在高维机器人多体推断任务中展现了超越传统算法的稳定性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Probabilistic inference over spatially embedded variables requires beliefs that respect $SE(3)$ symmetry, yet existing equivariant networks produce only scalars and vectors -- not the rank-2 precision tensors needed for anisotropic uncertainty, and single-component messages collapse multi-modal energy landscapes to physically meaningless averages. We introduce Equivariant Neural Belief Propagation (ENBP), a factor-graph framework whose messages are equivariant Gaussian mixture models with sufficient statistics that transform exactly under $SE(3)$. Rank-2 precision matrices are synthesised via equivariant outer products, ingested through differentiable spectral decomposition, and kept tractable by a greedy KL-based mixture reduction that provably commutes with $SE(3)$. On GEOM-QM9 and GEOM-Drugs, ENBP achieves 98.9% conformational coverage at 0.090 $\mathring{A}$ error with sub-second latency -- over $100\times$ faster than diffusion baselines at higher accuracy. On multi-body robotic inference, vanilla loopy BP diverges at 15+ agents while ENBP converges with near-zero collision rates and machine-precision equivariance error (${\sim}10^{-7}$ vs.\ $10^{-1}$ for augmented baselines).

Abstract: The paradigm of global weather forecasting is rapidly shifting with the emergence of Machine Learning Weather Prediction models (MLWP). Results reveal a regime-dependent skill profile. During the austral winter, GraphCast underperforms in the medium range (lead days 2-7) for $Z_{500}$ when resolving fast-propagating baroclinic systems over southern Brazil, but regains an advantage in the extended range, where its inherent smoothing of chaotic small-scale variability becomes beneficial under deterministic skill metrics. Conversely, during the austral summer wet season, GraphCast accurately captures large-scale moisture transport while intrinsically dampening the high-frequency convective variability that degrades deterministic NWP temperature forecasts. These findings establish a baseline for Brazil and define the specific physical boundaries that will guide future ``tropicalization'' efforts, aiming to optimize these foundational AI models for regional resilience.

### [134] [End-to-End Subgraph Detection with GraphDETR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06364)
*Dexiong Chen,Till Hendrik Schulz,Karsten Borgwardt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GraphDETR是一种基于Transformer的新型子图检测框架，通过将检测问题转化为集合预测任务，实现了高效、端到端的模式匹配，打破了传统组合方法在处理规模上的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的子图检测方法（基于子图同构）属于NP完全问题，受限于计算复杂度，难以在大规模图或大规模模式中应用。作者旨在利用深度学习方法提升子图检测在复杂模式和大规模图上的效率与适用性。

Method: 提出了一种名为GraphDETR的深度学习框架，其核心是将子图检测建模为集合预测问题（类似于计算机视觉中的DETR）：首先使用图神经网络（GNN）对目标图进行编码，随后利用一组可学习的查询向量（query vectors）通过Transformer解码器进行处理，最终通过二部匹配（bipartite matching）实现端到端的训练和模式预测。

Result: 实验证明GraphDETR能有效检测包含高达50个节点的多种模式（如分子结构、环、团和模糊模式），并能在1000个节点的目标图中高效运行。在ChEMBL数据集的分子官能团检测任务上，该模型表现出色，达到了91.2的AP100指标。

Conclusion: GraphDETR通过引入集合预测范式，证明了基于深度学习的Transformer架构能够有效处理图中的子图检测问题，且比传统组合算法更具扩展性和鲁棒性，特别是在处理近似匹配和复杂模式识别方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: Subgraph detection seeks to identify whether and where instances of query patterns occur within a larger graph. This problem is fundamental across scientific domains and is closely related to subgraph isomorphism, which is NP-complete, limiting combinatorial approaches to small patterns or moderately sized graphs. We introduce GraphDETR, a deep learning framework that formulates subgraph detection as a set prediction problem, analogous to DETR in object detection. GraphDETR encodes the target graph with a graph neural network, and employs a fixed set of learnable query vectors, decoded via a transformer decoder, to predict all pattern occurrences jointly in a single forward pass. This is enabled by training the model end-to-end with bipartite matching. Unlike traditional combinatorial methods that only solve exact structural matching, GraphDETR naturally extends to approximate matching, enabling detection beyond exact pattern correspondence. Empirically, we show that GraphDETR can detect diverse patterns, such as molecular structures, cycles, cliques, and fuzzy patterns of up to 50 nodes, in target graphs with up to 1000 nodes. We further evaluate on molecular functional group detection over the ChEMBL dataset, where GraphDETR predicts the complete set of functional groups per molecule, achieving a strong performance of $\text{AP}_{100} = 91.2$.

### [135] [Learned Response-Field Inertia Operator for HEC-RAS 2D Water-Surface Elevation Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06385)
*Edward Holmberg,Elias Ioup,Md Meftahul Ferdaus,Mahdi Abdelguerfi,Julian Simeonov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种名为LRFIO的原生网格代理模型，通过在非均匀计算单元上进行基于增量的推断，不仅消除了网格转换误差，还通过自适应的复杂性控制实现了与原始求解器高度一致且极速的水面高程预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统水文模型（如HEC-RAS 2D）在进行水面高程（WSE）预测时计算开销巨大。现有的代理模型常因栅格重映射引入误差或信息获取混淆而性能受限。本研究旨在开发一种既能保持求解器一致性，又能避免网格转换误差，且具备高效计算能力的“原生网格”代理模型，以解决大规模水文模拟的实时性需求。

Method: 研究提出了一种名为“学习响应场惯性算子”（LRFIO）的代理模型。该方法直接在原始非均匀计算网格上操作，避免了栅格重映射误差。其核心逻辑包括：1. 采用基于增量的预测策略；2. 建立包含持久性、全局校准惯性和分段响应场惯性的分层响应体系；3. 引入复杂性选择器，仅在验证证据充分时保留神经化惯性等复杂组件，从而实现自适应的模型复杂度控制。

Result: 在四个不同的HEC-RAS 2D基准测试中，LRFIO表现出强大的自适应能力，验证遗憾度（validation regret）最大仅为4.30%。部署测试显示，其推断时间在0.003秒至0.242秒之间，在Beaver Bayou案例中实现了较原始HEC-RAS求解器约2.75万倍的加速比。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，基于原生网格的增量预测是一种高效且稳健的求解器一致性水面高程预测方案。通过分层策略和经验驱动的复杂性选择（LRFIO），研究证实了无需盲目增加模型复杂度，仅在必要时引入神经计算或空间复杂度即可实现优异的预测性能，从而在保证精度的同时大幅提升计算效率。

Abstract: This article presents a cross-dataset evaluation of learned native-cell surrogate models for solver-consistent water-surface elevation (WSE) prediction in HEC-RAS 2D. To avoid raster remapping error and information-access confounding, surrogates are evaluated directly on the original nonuniform computational cells under an explicit policy that separates static project inputs, current hydraulic state, project-input forcing, calibration-derived quantities, and future solver-output targets. We introduce the Learned Response-Field Inertia Operator (LRFIO), a no-forcing, increment-based learned surrogate that calibrates an inertial response operator from solved HEC-RAS trajectories and deploys the retained operator through closed-form native-cell rollout. LRFIO evaluates a base-case-first response hierarchy consisting of persistence, global calibrated inertia, and segmented response-field inertia. Segmentation, residual correction, and neuralized inertia are treated as learnable modeling choices, with added complexity retained only when validation evidence justifies its cost. Evaluated across four diverse HEC-RAS 2D benchmarks, LRFIO retains different response structures for different domains, demonstrating adaptive learned complexity. The selector audit shows controlled complexity with a maximum validation regret of 4.30%. During deployment, retained rollout times range from 0.003 s to 0.242 s, and the Beaver Bayou measured-solve comparison gives an estimated 2.75 x 10^4 horizon-normalized speedup over HEC-RAS. These results indicate that the current native-cell increment is a strong solver-conditioned predictive scaffold and that added response-field, neural, or spatial complexity should be retained only when empirically justified.

### [136] [Proper Scoring Rules for Right-Censored Survival Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06393)
*Jef Jonkers,Glenn Van Wallendael,Luc Duchateau,Sofie Van Hoecke*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文针对右删失数据提出了一种通用的真确评分框架，通过将预测分布映射到观测空间，实现了对CRPS、Brier等经典指标的系统性扩展，解决了生存分析中模型评估偏差及排序不一致的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的真确评分规则（Proper scoring rules）在处理右删失（right-censored）生存数据时存在局限性，导致这些规则无法直接应用。现有的评估方法往往缺乏统一的理论框架，或在特定删失机制下存在性能缺陷，因此需要一种能系统性推广到删失数据的新方法。

Method: 论文提出了一种“映射”方法，首先将预测分布通过删失机制进行映射，然后在诱导的观测数据分布上应用原始的真确评分规则。根据删失时间的分布特征，该方法分为固定删失时间的局部评分和随机删失下的边缘化评分。此外，研究还将此原则扩展至多变量生存建模的样本学习目标，即“删失回归”（censored engression）。

Result: 理论上证明了边缘化评分在条件独立删失假设下是“真确的”（proper），在可识别区域是“严格真确的”。实验结果表明，该方法在多种删失方案下能正确对预测模型进行排序，避免了预测依赖型加权评分中可能出现的排序反转问题；同时，“删失回归”在处理多变量生存数据时也显著优于简单的朴素训练方法。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种基于映射机制的通用框架，用于右删失生存数据的概率预测评估。该框架不仅统一了现有的评分规则（如似然和IPCW），还推导出了CRPS、Brier分数等指标的删失版本，为生存分析中的模型评估和训练提供了更严谨、更具鲁棒性的理论支持。

Abstract: Proper scoring rules provide a rigorous theoretical basis for the training and evaluation of probabilistic forecasts. However, in the presence of right censoring, the event time is only partially observed, rendering conventional scoring rules inapplicable in their standard form. We propose a framework for proper scoring of right-censored survival outcomes based on a simple idea: first, map the predictive distribution through the censoring mechanism, then apply the underlying proper score on the induced observed-data law. This yields localized scores for fixed censoring times and marginalized scores when the censoring time is random or only partially observed. The resulting construction recovers familiar right-censored likelihood and IPCW-type criteria within a coherent framework, while also yielding right-censored versions of the CRPS, pinball loss, Brier score, and energy score. We show that the marginalized score is proper under conditional independent censoring and strictly proper on the identifiable region. The same principle also leads to censored engression, a sample-based learning objective for multivariate right-censored survival modeling. In experiments, our scores correctly rank the oracle forecast across several censoring regimes, whereas forecast-dependent plug-in weighted scores can exhibit ranking reversals. Censored engression likewise substantially improves over naive training on censored outcomes.

### [137] [The Post-GCN Decade Revisited: Curvature-Stratified Evaluation of Relational Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06397)
*Shuo Wang,Xiangyu Wang,Quanxin Wang,Bailin Wu,Bokui Wang,Shunyang Huang,Boyan Deng,Haonan Liu,Ruiyi Fang,Zhenxiang Xu,Boyu Wang,Zhao Kang*

TL;DR: 该论文指出关系学习评估中的几何偏差问题，引入了基于曲率分层的评估协议，证明了模型性能受数据集几何结构的制约，并提供了更科学的评估工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的关系学习评估过分依赖平均性能的平铺式排行榜，假设不同数据集具有统一结构，这导致了系统性偏差，掩盖了与几何结构相关的性能差异，并可能产生误导性的泛化能力结论。

Method: 提出了一种“曲率分层评估框架”（Curvature-stratified evaluation framework），将数据集根据曲率（正、负、近零）进行划分。研究者通过该框架在14个数据集上对18个代表性模型（包括GCN、图基础模型及表格学习方法）进行了评估。

Result: 实验发现，模型排名在同一曲率区间内表现稳定，但在不同区间间发生显著变化，证明模型性能高度依赖于几何结构。此外，研究揭示了在某些特定曲率区间内，图基础模型（GFMs）相比几何对齐的图神经网络（GNNs）收益递减。

Conclusion: 研究表明，现有的关系学习评价方法因忽略了数据集的几何属性而存在系统性偏差。模型表现与数据集的固有几何结构（如曲率）密切相关，因此建立一种基于曲率分层的几何感知评估协议对于实现更准确、可解释的模型评估至关重要。

Abstract: Current evaluation practices in relational learning rely heavily on flat leaderboards that average performance across heterogeneous datasets, implicitly assuming a uniform underlying structure. We show that this assumption introduces systematic bias: it obscures geometry-dependent performance variations and can lead to misleading conclusions about model generalization. In this work, we identify intrinsic geometry as a key latent factor governing model effectiveness. We demonstrate that conventional aggregated metrics mask critical performance trade-offs that only become visible when datasets are stratified by their geometric properties. To address this issue, we introduce a curvature-stratified evaluation framework that partitions datasets into positive, negative, and near-zero curvature regimes. Our benchmark evaluates 18 representative models including Graph Convolutional Networks (GCNs), Graph Foundation Models (GFMs), and tabular learning methods across 14 datasets. We find that model rankings are highly stable within each curvature regime but shift significantly across regimes, indicating that performance is fundamentally geometry-dependent rather than universally transferable. Notably, we identify regimes where GFMs offer diminishing returns compared to geometry-aligned GNNs. Based on these findings, we propose a geometry-aware evaluation protocol that yields more reliable and interpretable comparisons than standard aggregated benchmarks. We release all code, curvature-stratified dataset splits, and evaluation tools to support reproducible and rigorous assessment of future relational learning methods. Code and datasets are provided in our project homepage: https://sirbabbage.github.io/CurvBench_HOME/.

</details>


### [138] [Double Preconditioning (DoPr): Optimization for Test-Time Performance, not Validation Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06418)
*Thomas T. Zhang,Alok Shah,Yifei Zhang,Vincent Zhang,Nikolai Matni,Max Simchowitz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对自回归生成和决策任务中常见的“测试时反馈（TTF）”误差累积问题，本文提出了一种结合梯度级和激活级预处理的新型优化器 DoPr，在不显著降低验证损失的前提下，有效提升了模型在下游任务中的实际表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在深度学习应用中，许多模型训练时使用单步预测损失，但在部署时却采取自回归方式生成。这种“训练-推理”范式的不匹配会导致测试时反馈（TTF）现象，即随着任务序列长度增加，模型预测误差不断累积，导致验证集损失与下游任务性能指标不一致。

Method: 引入了一种名为“双预处理（DoPr）”的新型优化范式。该方法结合了梯度级预处理（如 Adam 或 Muon）与激活级预处理（AP，如 KFAC），旨在直接应对测试时误差累积的问题，作为一种可插拔的干预手段。

Result: 实验表明，DoPr 方法能在多种存在 TTF 的场景中显著提升模型的下游性能。值得注意的是，这种性能提升并不总是伴随着验证集损失的下降，这揭示了现有模型评估方法的局限性。

Conclusion: 本文提出通过优化范式（而非单纯修改数据、架构或目标函数）来缓解测试时反馈（TTF）带来的误差累积问题。双预处理（DoPr）方法证明了优化器设计对于提升下游任务性能至关重要，并挑战了仅依靠验证集损失函数评估模型的传统做法。

Abstract: Many modern applications of deep learning involve training a neural network via a one-step prediction loss (e.g., $L^2$ regression, cross-entropy), but deploy the network by rolling out along its own predictions. Key examples include autoregressive language modeling, flow-based generative modeling, and robot policy learning. It is well-documented that these settings induce a phenomenon we call test-time feedback (TTF): the mismatch between the training/validation loss and downstream metrics of interest, such as task success rate and generation quality, which grows with task length. While data curation, architecture, and objective design have been proposed to combat train-test shift in TTF settings, this paper proposes optimization as a new design axis to mitigate error accumulation. Specifically, we introduce a new optimization paradigm called double-preconditioning (DoPr) uniquely tailored to the challenges of TTF. DoPr combines gradient-wise preconditioning, as in Adam and Muon, with activation-wise preconditioning (AP), such as in KFAC. We show that the addition of AP yields a drop-in intervention for increasing downstream model performance across a range of TTF settings. Interestingly, these gains in test-time performance do not consistently accompany improvements in validation loss, opening new questions about how to properly evaluate models trained with one-step supervised objectives.

### [139] [CaliDist: Calibrating Large Language Models via Behavioral Robustness to Distraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05799)
*Mohammad Anas Jawad,Cornelia Caragea*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有 LLM 校准方法忽略“行为鲁棒性”的问题，本文提出了 CaliDist 方法。它通过测量模型在语义干扰下的预测稳定性，自适应地调整模型置信度，在多个基准测试中大幅降低了校准误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的校准方法主要关注预测概率与准确率的一致性，却忽略了模型在面对无关或误导性信息时的“行为鲁棒性”。作者认为模型真正的置信度应当反映其在受到干扰时的稳定性，而非仅仅是在干净输入上的表现。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CaliDist 的事后校准方法。该方法通过在输入提示词中加入语义干扰物（distractors），量化并评估模型在面临“认知压力”时的预测变化和不确定性波动。随后，利用这种稳定性指标作为修正因子，对模型原始的置信度得分进行自适应缩放。

Result: 在七个自然语言理解基准测试和六种大语言模型上进行的实验表明，CaliDist 在预期校准误差（ECE）和 Brier 分数上均优于现有的强基线模型。平均而言，CaliDist 将 ECE 从 23% 显著降低至 7%，实现了约 70% 的相对性能提升。

Conclusion: 研究表明，行为鲁棒性是衡量大语言模型可信度的关键维度。通过引入行为稳定性作为校准信号，CaliDist 方法能够显著提高模型预测的置信度准确性，证明了将对抗干扰下的行为稳定性纳入校准过程是提升模型校准性能的有效策略。

Abstract: Existing calibration methods for Large Language Models (LLMs) often overlook a critical dimension of trustworthiness: a model's {\em behavioral robustness} to irrelevant or misleading information. In this paper, we argue that a model's true confidence should reflect its stability under cognitive pressure. We introduce \textsc{CaliDist}, a novel post-hoc calibration approach that directly measures and penalizes a model's susceptibility to distraction. \textsc{CaliDist} quantifies how an LLM's predictions and uncertainty change when its input prompt is perturbed with semantic \textit{distractors}. This stability (or lack thereof) signal is then used to adaptively scale the model's initial confidence score. Our extensive experiments on seven Natural Language Understanding classification benchmarks using six distinct LLMs show that \textsc{CaliDist} consistently achieves lower Expected Calibration Error (ECE) and Brier Score compared with strong baselines. Remarkably, our method reduces the ECE from 23\% to 7\% on average--a relative improvement of 70\%--demonstrating that behavioral stability is a powerful signal for calibration. We make our code and datasets available at github.com/m-anas-j/CaliDist.

### [140] [Gradient Descent with Large Step Size Restores Symmetry in Deep Linear Networks with Multi-Pathway](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05219)
*Hee-Sung Kim,Sungyoon Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了离散梯度下降的步长对深度神经网络“路径特化”的影响：与梯度流预测的单一路径支配不同，大步长的梯度下降通过边缘稳定性诱导网络将特征分布在多个路径上，从而促进共享表示的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多基于梯度流（GF）模型，认为深度学习中的多路径网络倾向于“赢家通吃”式的路径特化（即每个特征集中在单一路径）。然而，该理论无法解释实际训练中观察到的现象，因此作者旨在探究离散梯度下降（尤其是较大步长）如何改变这种对称性破缺的预测，并解释深度如何塑造路径竞争。

Method: 通过数学证明和理论分析，对比连续时间梯度流（Gradient Flow）与离散时间梯度下降（Gradient Descent）在多路径深度线性网络中的训练动态；分析了尖锐极小值（Sharp Minima）与步长及网络结构之间的关系，并探讨了训练后期“边缘稳定性”造成的振荡对参数分布的影响。

Result: 证明了单路径解在离散GD中对应于尖锐极小值；发现分配信号到多个路径可以降低损失函数的平滑度（减少尖锐程度）；揭示了训练过程分为两个阶段：早期遵循GF的对称性破缺，后期通过“边缘稳定性”产生的振荡实现特征在多路径间的重分配。

Conclusion: 研究表明，深度学习中训练动态受离散梯度下降（GD）步长的显著影响。虽然梯度流（GF）预测了单一路径的特化（赢家通吃），但具有较大步长的梯度下降会利用“边缘稳定性”（Edge of Stability）现象，驱使网络进入再平衡阶段，最终倾向于产生共享的特征表示而非单一路径的支配地位。

Abstract: Recent analyses of multi-pathway Deep Linear Networks use Gradient Flow to predict a "winner-takes-all" specialization in which path symmetry breaks and each feature concentrates in a single pathway. In this work, we show that discrete Gradient Descent (GD) with a large step size tells a different story. We prove that single-path solutions are sharp minima, whereas distributing signals across pathways reduces sharpness by a factor that decreases with both the number of pathways and depth. Consequently, while early training reproduces the depth-driven symmetry breaking predicted by GF, oscillations at the Edge of Stability subsequently override this tendency and drive the network into a re-balancing phase, where signals redistribute across pathways. Together, these results clarify how depth shapes pathway competition and explain why large-step GD favors shared representations rather than persistent single-pathway dominance.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的贝叶斯网络构建方法多基于单一优化，难以处理复杂系统中因果关系的多样性与不确定性，且往往忽略了数据中隐含的多种因果链可能。因此，需要一种能够更忠实地呈现数据、构建多个一致性因果图谱的框架。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于熵的推理方法，通过构建最大熵图集合（maximum-entropy ensemble of graphs）来代表因果关系。该方法在模拟的2节点和20节点线性结构方程模型（SEM）数据上进行了验证，旨在捕捉数据中固有的结构模糊性，而非仅依赖单一的最优解。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法能够有效地量化因果关系中的结构模糊性。与传统的优化方法相比，该方法揭示了许多被视为“最优”的DAG实际上包含了一些在拓扑上并不具备统计一致性的因果伪影。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于优化的单一DAG构建方法往往会产生与数据并不完全一致的因果伪影。相比之下，基于熵的推理方法能够生成与数据一致的因果关系图集（atlases），从而更准确地量化因果结构中的固有不确定性。

Abstract: Data-driven causal relationship identification is pertinent to advancing understanding of complex systems both within and beyond science. Bayesian networks offer a probabilistic method for modelling generic causal relationships via directed acyclic graphs (DAGs). However, typical techniques for constructing Bayesian networks rely on optimization, which can be ill-suited for learning causal relationships because the underlying data may admit multiple chains of causation. More data-faithful representations of causal relationships would provide frameworks for constructing multiple causal maps that are consistent with the variability that is inherent in underlying data. Here, we show that entropy-based inference generates atlases of plausible causal relationships that are consistent with underlying data. On simulated noisy data of 2- and 20-node linear structural equation models, we sample a maximum-entropy ensemble of graphs that allow us to quantify the inherent structural ambiguity in underlying causal relationships. Our method shows that "optimized" DAGs can contain causal artifacts are not consistent across equivalently accurate topologies.

Conclusion: 该研究证明了高效多模态推理可以通过可微分算子搜索（Differentiable Operator Search）来实现，而非依赖人工设计。这种方法不仅能够复现现有的主流技术，还能发现更优的混合策略，为构建高效视觉模型提供了新的自动化范式。

Abstract: Efficient multimodal foundation models often rely on manually designed token-reduction operators, such as pruning, merging, pooling, and adaptive reweighting. Although these operators appear different, we show that they can be interpreted as distinct regimes of a shared operator space. Based on this view, we introduce Efficient Operator Search, a differentiable framework that jointly searches where to reduce tokens, how many tokens to retain, and how reduced token information should be processed. The proposed search space parameterizes layer activation, retention budget, and operator behavior, while the search policy optimizes task performance under one-sided budget and cost constraints. This formulation recovers representative hand-designed baselines as special cases and further discovers hybrid operators beyond isolated manual designs. Experiments on multimodal benchmarks show that the searched operators achieve competitive accuracy-efficiency trade-offs, especially under aggressive visual-token reduction. These results suggest that efficient multimodal inference can be reframed from manual operator design to differentiable operator search.

Abstract: Multiple Instance Learning (MIL) addresses problems where supervision is available at the level of bags of instances and has been successfully applied in fields ranging from computational pathology to satellite imagery. Nevertheless, existing algorithms struggle in the low-label regime that characterizes many real-world applications. Flexible models overfit and rigid ones fail to adapt to the task at hand. We show that pretraining an in-context learner with a Perceiver-style architecture on synthetic data yields a model that can solve new tasks from a handful of labeled bags. At inference time, classification happens in a single forward pass and requires no gradient updates. We propose and investigate different synthetic data generators for bag-structured data and find that they capture complementary inductive biases. ### [144] [Policy-Conditioned Counterfactual Credit for Verifiable Reinforcement Learning of Long-Horizon Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05263)
*Renwei Meng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 CVT-RL 的强化学习算法，通过反事实评估和多重约束机制，解决了语言智能体在长程推理任务中产生的信念漂移、证据链不可靠及“捷径”作弊问题，显著提升了模型的推理可信度和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长程语言智能体强化学习方法通常依赖于相关性奖励，导致智能体容易产生“信念漂移”、依赖不支持的证据链，或者采取仅能通过终端检查的“捷径”（hack），缺乏对推理过程真实贡献的准确评估。

Method: 提出了 CVT-RL 算法，核心包含三个部分：1. 带有干预有效性门控的策略梯度学习；2. 策略条件下的反事实贡献（PCCC）估计器，用于评估单步操作对最终结果的真实贡献；3. 基于增强拉格朗日乘子法的约束机制，用于抑制不支持的断言、跳过验证、工具篡改及不安全调用。

Result: 在长上下文问答、ALFWorld、ScienceWorld 及 Web 工具任务中，CVT-RL 将任务成功率从基线的 75.4% 提升至 78.9%，证据 F1 值从 78.9 提高到 82.8，并将“作弊”行为（hacking）比例从 7.2% 降低至 3.9%。人机审计与攻击测试进一步验证了该方法的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: CVT-RL 通过引入反事实贡献评估和多维度的约束机制，为长程语言智能体提供了一种更可靠、更稳健的强化学习路径，有效减少了模型幻觉和恶意“作弊”行为，提升了推理和工具使用的真实性。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves reasoning and tool use, yet long-horizon language agents still learn unsupported evidence chains, belief drift, and shortcut actions that satisfy terminal checks. Existing process rewards are mostly correlational: they reward retrieval-, reflection-, or verification-like steps without estimating whether the step contributes to final verified success under a specified intervention. We propose CVT-RL, a constrained policy-gradient algorithm with dense verifiable rewards, intervention-validity gating, and a policy-conditioned counterfactual contribution (PCCC) estimator. Deletion, semantic substitution, evidence substitution, and tool-output perturbation define separate controlled interventions; continuations are sampled from a frozen reference policy, and a selection-adjusted doubly robust estimator augments the advantage. Belief control uses only prefix-observable labels, while an augmented Lagrangian constrains unsupported claims, skipped verification, tool tampering, and unsafe calls. On long-context QA, ALFWorld, ScienceWorld, and web/tool tasks, CVT-RL improves average task success from 71.8% for compute-matched non-causal RL and 75.4% for an information-matched counterfactual-process baseline to 78.9%, improves evidence F1 from 78.9 to 82.8 over the information-matched baseline, and reduces measured hacking from 7.2% to 3.9%. Independent human audit estimates 4.6% hacking for CVT-RL versus 8.1% for the information-matched baseline, and adaptive detector-evasion attacks raise hacking only to 7.1%. Stratified bootstrap and mixed-effects tests give p<0.01 after Holm correction for all primary metrics. Carefully scoped counterfactual credit, paired with validity gating, diagnostics, and verifiable constraints, provides a reproducible route toward more reliable long-horizon RL for language agents.

*Christie Djidjev,Nicholas Kaminski*

TL;DR: 针对 AI-RAN 环境中多个 AI 控制功能间的隐性干扰问题，本文提出了一种从连续网络遥测数据中识别参数与 KPI 间真实依赖关系的机器学习框架，通过合成数据验证了其有效性，并强调了阈值校准在事件检测中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 AI-RAN 和 O-RAN 等架构中，多个 AI 控制功能并发运行，它们之间产生的复杂干扰难以仅从原始网络数据中直观捕捉。现有管理机制缺乏一种可靠且可解释的依赖结构来明确参数与性能指标（KPI）之间的影响关系，因此需要一种机制从噪声数据中准确识别真实的控制交互事件。

Method: 本文采用了一种基于机器学习的依赖关系恢复流水线，将连续数据转换为二进制事件指标的问题建模为显著性检测问题。研究者引入了一个带有隐藏依赖关系的合成闭环流量生成器，通过对该受控遥测数据的分析，验证了依赖关系发现算法的有效性，并重点探讨了阈值校准对事件检测质量的影响。

Result: 实验结果表明，在背景噪声与控制信号区分度足够的前提下，该流水线能够可靠地从连续遥测轨迹中还原出隐藏的依赖结构；同时研究发现，阈值校准是影响事件检测准确性的决定性因素。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种将连续遥测数据转化为二进制事件指标的有效框架，证明了通过显著性检测识别 AI-RAN 中复杂参数与 KPI 间依赖关系的潜力和可行性，并指出阈值校准是确保该系统可靠性的核心因素，为自适应无线网络的可解释性控制奠定了基础。

Abstract: Next-generation wireless networks are expected to rely on multiple concurrent AI-driven control functions that optimize different network objectives simultaneously, particularly in AI-integrated and open radio access network architectures such as AI Radio Access Network (AI-RAN) and Open Radio Access Network (O-RAN). When these functions interact, they can interfere with one another in ways that are difficult to detect from raw network data alone. A key missing piece for managing such interactions is a reliable, interpretable dependency structure that captures which control parameters are actively influencing which network performance outcomes at any given time. This paper focuses on the event-detection step needed to support such dependency learning by converting noisy continuous telemetry into binary indicators of parameter activity and KPI response. The central difficulty is that not every fluctuation in the data reflects a genuine control interaction, so the method must distinguish real parameter-outcome relationships from background variation. Because real AI-RAN traffic traces with known parameter-KPI ground truth are difficult to obtain, we introduce a synthetic closed-loop traffic generator with planted latent dependencies. We use this controlled telemetry to evaluate a machine-learning-based dependency recovery pipeline that formulates the conversion of continuous traces into binary event indicators as a significance-detection problem. Experimental evaluation shows that the proposed pipeline reliably recovers the latent dependency structure from noisy continuous traces when the signal is sufficiently separated from background variation, while highlighting threshold calibration as the key factor controlling event-detection quality. These results constitute a foundational step toward interpretable dependency learning for adaptive AI-RAN control systems.

### [146] [Agentic Monte Carlo: Simulating Reinforcement Learning for Black-Box Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05296)
*Dae Yon Hwang,Raunaq Suri,Valentin Villecroze,Anthony L. Caterini,Jesse C. Cresswell,Noël Vouitsis,Brendan Leigh Ross*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对黑盒 LLM 代理无法进行传统强化学习的问题，本文提出了一种基于序列蒙特卡洛（SMC）的优化方法（AMC），通过在推理阶段引导采样，在不改变模型参数的情况下实现了与强化学习相当的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习（RL）方法通常需要访问模型参数（如开源模型），而对于通过 API 调用的黑盒 LLM 代理，由于无法进行参数更新，现有的 RL 优化方法不再适用。因此，如何对黑盒代理进行有效的强化学习式优化成为一个关键挑战。

Method: 本文提出了“代理蒙特卡洛”（Agentic Monte Carlo, AMC）方法。该方法利用强化学习与贝叶斯推理之间的等价性，将最优策略视为轨迹的后验分布，并以固定的黑盒 LLM 作为先验。通过训练一个值函数（Value Function）来引导序列蒙特卡洛采样，从而在不修改底层模型参数的前提下实现推理阶段的策略优化。

Result: 在 AgentGym 基准测试的三个不同环境中，AMC 均表现出显著优于传统提示词工程（Prompting）的效果。实验结果表明，随着推理时计算资源（test-time compute）的增加，AMC 的性能甚至可以超过基于参数更新的组相对策略优化（GRPO）方法。

Conclusion: Agentic Monte Carlo (AMC) 证明了在不改变黑盒模型参数的情况下，通过序列蒙特卡洛方法进行原则性的强化学习式优化是切实可行的。该方法通过在推理时分配更多计算资源，能够有效提升黑盒代理的性能，为黑盒大模型的优化开辟了新的研究路径。

Abstract: LLM agents operate in two distinct regimes: open-weight agents amenable to reinforcement learning (RL) and black-box agents whose behaviour must be controlled purely at test time. Although black-box agents are often backed by state-of-the-art proprietary LLMs, API-only access precludes parameter-level optimization, rendering most RL methods inapplicable. To address this limitation, we turn to a known equivalence between RL and Bayesian inference. We propose Agentic Monte Carlo (AMC) to directly sample from the optimal policy of a black-box agent rather than training it through RL. The optimal policy is a posterior over trajectories whose prior we define as the fixed black-box LLM agent. We employ Sequential Monte Carlo to sample from this posterior by learning a value function to steer the agent while leaving the underlying black-box model unchanged. We validate AMC on three diverse environments from the AgentGym benchmark, demonstrating significant improvements over prompting baselines and even outperforming Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) as we scale the test-time compute of our method. AMC demonstrates the feasibility of performing principled RL-style optimization of black-box LLM agents. Code is available at https://github.com/layer6ai-labs/Agentic-Monte-Carlo

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种预处理（PC）层，即通过多项式预处理对权重矩阵进行参数化。该模块在训练过程中重塑权重矩阵的奇异值谱，训练完成后可将预处理权重合并回原架构，保持推理成本不变。理论上，通过证明控制每层奇异值有助于深度线性网络中梯度下降的几何收敛，为该方法提供了支撑。

Conclusion: 通过低阶多项式预处理层，可以在不增加推理开销的前提下，显著提升大语言模型的训练稳定性和收敛速度。该研究为优化权重矩阵的奇异值谱提供了一种高效的理论与工程方案。

Abstract: We propose a preconditioning (PC) layer, a weight parameterization via polynomial preconditioner that ensures stable weight conditioning throughout LLM training. The PC module reshapes the singular-value spectrum of weight matrices via low-degree polynomial preconditioning. After training, the preconditioned weights can be merged back into the original architecture, incurring no inference overhead. We demonstrate the advantage of the proposed PC layer over standard transformers in Llama-1B pre-training, for both the AdamW and Muon optimizers. Theoretically, we justify this spectrum-control principle by proving that uniformly bounding each layer's singular values ensures geometric convergence of gradient descent to global minima, for certain deep linear networks. Our code is available at https://github.com/Empath-aln/PC-layer.

### [148] [RREDCoT: Segment-Level Reward Redistribution for Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06475)
*Mykyta Ielanskyi,Kajetan Schweighofer,Lukas Aichberger,Sepp Hochreiter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 RREDCoT 的方法，通过模型自近似奖励重分配来解决推理模型在训练中遇到的长思维链延迟奖励高方差问题，在保证高效性的同时优化了信用分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理模型训练（如使用 GRPO）面临延迟奖励问题，导致强化学习过程方差极大。传统的蒙特卡洛（MC）采样虽能进行信用分配，但因计算开销过大而不适用于长上下文下的实时训练。因此，需要一种高效的、无需额外生成的奖励重分配机制来降低方差并提升训练效率。

Method: 提出了 RREDCoT (Reward REDistribution for Chain of Thoughts) 方法。该方法利用模型自身来近似最优奖励重分配，无需额外的生成过程，通过对思维链（CoT）进行分段并估计状态价值，从而实现训练时的细粒度信用分配，避免了蒙特卡洛采样的高计算开销。

Result: 研究表明，RREDCoT 能够以较低的计算成本实现比蒙特卡洛采样及多种归因方法更有效的信用分配。实验分析了思维链的分段策略及状态价值估计对重分配效果的影响，证明了该方法在优化长思维链推理表现方面的优势。

Conclusion: RREDCoT 通过利用模型自身近似最优奖励重分配，有效地解决了长思维链中延迟奖励带来的高方差问题，为在大规模推理模型训练中进行高效的信用分配提供了一种可行方案。

Abstract: Recent advancements in reasoning language models have been driven by Reinforcement Learning (RL) fine-tuning. Most often, these rely on the Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) algorithm or modifications thereof to steer the models to produce Chain-of-Thought (CoT) traces. The final answer can only be verified, and the reward assigned, after the CoT trace is complete, making it a delayed reward problem. GRPO and its modifications correspond to Monte Carlo methods in standard RL, which are known to suffer from high variance. A possible solution to this problem is the redistribution of rewards through credit assignment, where segments of the CoT trace that are important for arriving at the desirable solution are emphasized by assigning a higher reward. While Monte Carlo sampling can be used to provide an unbiased estimate of intermediate state values, its computational overhead makes it unsuitable for train-time credit assignment in long contexts at high granularity. We introduce RREDCoT (Reward REDistribution for Chain of Thoughts), which utilizes the model itself to approximate the optimal reward redistribution without additional generation. We investigate the advantages of our method compared to MC sampling and several attribution methods. We further analyze several aspects relevant to the construction of the redistribution such as segmentation of CoT traces and state value estimation.

### [149] [Compress-Distill: Reasoning Trace Compression for Efficient Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05988)
*Maxime Griot,Paul Steven Scotti,Tanishq Mathew Abraham*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了推理链（CoT）的后验压缩技术，发现通过压缩轨迹可以显著提升训练速度和推理效率，学生模型能保持约96%的原始准确率，实现了精度与效率的有效权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理模型生成的长思维链（Chain-of-Thought）蒸馏成本高昂，且会导致学生模型输出过于冗长，因此探索如何通过后验压缩来优化训练效率和推理输出长度。

Method: 使用Qwen3.5-397B-A17B和gpt-oss-120B作为教师模型生成大量高质量推理轨迹，随后利用指令微调模型对这些轨迹进行后验压缩（缩减至原始长度的8.6%-21.0%），并通过对比实验评估其对学生模型训练效率及下游任务精度的影响。

Result: 压缩后的推理轨迹可将训练Token减少至原始的12%-30%，训练速度提升2.0-7.6倍，推理输出缩短3-19倍；尽管raw轨迹在准确性上仍保持领先，但模型压缩方法优于简单的截断法，尤其在小模型上表现更佳。

Conclusion: 推理链（CoT）压缩在准确性和效率之间提供了一个权衡方案，而非无损改进。学生模型在保留原始数据约96%精度的同时，能显著提高推理效率，且在小参数模型上表现优于简单的长度截断。

Abstract: Reasoning models produce long chain-of-thought traces that are costly to distill and encourage verbose student outputs. We study post-hoc compression of such traces before knowledge distillation. Two teachers, Qwen3.5-397B-A17B and gpt-oss-120B, generate about 283k correct traces each; two instruction-tuned models then compress them to 8.6-21.0% of their original character length. Across a 48-run main grid plus seven Qwen-teacher truncation ablations, compressed traces reduce training tokens to 12-30% of raw, speed up training by 2.0-7.6x, and shorten inference outputs by 3-19x with smaller reductions under the shorter gpt-oss teacher. However, raw traces retain the highest downstream accuracy at every scale and for both teachers. A length-matched raw-trace truncation ablation shows that compression is not merely benefiting from a smaller token budget: model-compressed traces usually beat or match naive truncation, especially for smaller students, while maintaining shorter inference outputs. Overall, reasoning-trace compression offers an accuracy-efficiency trade-off rather than a free improvement: students retain up to 96% of raw-trace accuracy while gaining up to 18x higher per-token efficiency, and at the 0.8B scale under LoRA compressed traces narrow the raw-vs-compressed gap but do not exceed raw.

### [150] [Pretraining Recurrent Networks without Recurrence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06479)
*Akarsh Kumar,Phillip Isola*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决RNN中BPTT算法计算缓慢且难以处理长序列的问题，本文提出了监督记忆训练（SMT）。SMT通过将RNN训练转化为时间并行的监督学习任务，成功实现了稳定的O(1)梯度路径，在提升训练效率的同时显著增强了模型处理长程依赖的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RNN训练方法——时间反向传播（BPTT）存在严重的局限性：一是计算必须按时间顺序进行，限制了并行化能力；二是面临梯度消失或梯度爆炸问题，导致模型难以学习长距离依赖关系。因此，需要一种能够脱离时间顺序、高效训练非线性RNN的新方法。

Method: 提出了监督记忆训练（SMT）方法。该方法不再直接对整个循环序列进行反向传播（BPTT），而是将训练简化为对单步记忆转换标签（m_t, x_{t+1} -> m_{t+1}）的监督学习。通过训练一个基于Transformer的编码器，利用预测状态目标来获取记忆标签，从而实现时间维度上的并行训练，并将梯度路径缩短为恒定的O(1)。

Result: 实验结果表明，在语言建模和像素序列建模等任务中，使用SMT预训练的多种RNN架构表现均优于BPTT。SMT在实现时间并行训练的同时，显著提升了模型学习长距离依赖的能力。

Conclusion: SMT通过将循环神经网络的训练转化为监督学习问题，成功克服了BPTT在并行化和梯度消失/爆炸方面的局限性。它不仅提升了模型对长距离依赖的捕捉能力，还支持时间维度的并行训练，为处理大规模时序数据提供了更高效的训练范式。

Abstract: Training recurrent neural networks (RNNs) requires assigning credit across long sequences of computations. Standard backpropagation through time (BPTT) addresses this problem poorly: it is sequential in time, limiting parallelism, and suffers from vanishing or exploding gradients, making long-range associations difficult to learn. We propose Supervised Memory Training (SMT), a method for training nonlinear RNNs that sidesteps recurrent credit propagation entirely by reducing RNN training to supervised learning on one-step memory transition labels $(m_t, x_{t+1}) \rightarrow m_{t+1}$. SMT acquires these memory labels by training a Transformer-based encoder on a predictive state objective--retaining only information from the past necessary to predict the future. By decoupling what to remember from how to update memory, SMT enables time-parallel RNN training with a stable $O(1)$ length gradient path between any two tokens--without ever unrolling the RNN. We find that SMT outperforms BPTT when pretraining various RNN architectures on tasks like language modeling and pixel sequence modeling. SMT enables nonlinear RNNs to better capture long-range dependencies and train in parallel, potentially unlocking the scaling of models that build temporal abstractions of past experience.

</details>


### [151] [Regret Minimization with Adaptive Opponents in Repeated Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06486)
*Mingyang Liu,Asuman Ozdaglar,Tiancheng Yu,Kaiqing Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对重复博弈中传统后悔指标无法处理适应性对手的问题，本文提出了“重复策略后悔”（RP-Regret），并设计了多种优化算法，成功在保持对抗性的同时提升了博弈的合作水平与收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的在线学习“外部后悔”指标无法有效捕捉重复博弈中对手根据历史记录进行适应性反应的特点，导致在多智能体交互中往往表现不佳。因此，需要一种能够体现博弈参与者反事实推理能力的、更符合博弈论性质的后悔定义。

Method: 1. 引入了“重复策略后悔”（RP-Regret）作为新的博弈论评价指标，以取代传统的外部后悔；2. 识别了实现子线性RP-Regret的必要条件（涉及比较策略的变化率及博弈者与对手的记忆限制）；3. 针对RP-Regret非凸的特性，提出了三种优化策略：基于优化预言机的算法、基于线性化凸替代函数的算法，以及针对慢速变化对手的直接最小化算法。

Result: 研究证明了在特定条件下RP-Regret可以实现子线性收敛。通过实验验证，在如“猎鹿博弈”（Stag-Hunt）等经典博弈中，使用RP-Regret算法能够引导博弈者达成收益更高的合作策略。此外，该方法还能学习到重复博弈中的子博弈完美均衡。

Conclusion: 本文提出的RP-Regret为研究重复博弈中适应性对手提供了一个更为贴切的框架。通过最小化该指标，博弈者不仅能更有效地应对对手的适应性策略，还能在多智能体系统中促成更具合作性、高收益的子博弈完美均衡。

Abstract: In this paper, we study regret minimization in repeated games with \emph{adaptive} opponents who can respond based on histories of play. The standard metric of \emph{external regret} in online learning is known to fail to capture such adaptivity. To account for players' counterfactual reasoning, we introduce {\tt Repeated Policy Regret (RP-Regret)}, a game-theoretic metric that measures the difference between the \emph{realized} and the \emph{best-in-hindsight} accumulated utility when all players can \emph{respond} to the history of play. Compared to existing regret notions in this setting, ours is native to repeated game playing, enabling stronger comparators and opponents with fewer constraints, while maintaining the possibility of finding better equilibria when all players minimize it. We first identify necessary conditions for obtaining {\tt RP-Regret} sublinear in time, on the variation of the player's comparator strategies in the regret definition and on the memories of both the comparator and opponents' strategies. We then study additional conditions and provable algorithms to minimize {\tt RP-Regret}, which is by definition \emph{non-convex} in the strategy space. To address this challenge, we propose three algorithms: (i) one based on an optimization oracle, as assumed in some prior work in online non-convex learning; (ii) one that minimizes a convex and \emph{linearized} surrogate of {\tt RP-Regret} at each iteration; (iii) one that directly minimizes {\tt RP-Regret} when opponents change strategies slowly. Furthermore, when all players can run algorithms to minimize the {\tt RP-Regret} (or its linearized variant), certain subgame perfect equilibria of the repeated game can be learned. We also provide experiments showing that minimizing our regret notions can lead to more cooperative solutions with higher utility in games such as Stag-Hunt.

</details>


### [152] [Pattern Selectivity is Not Task-Causal Structure: A Cross-Architecture Mechanistic Study of Composed-Task Circuits in 1B-Class Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05378)
*Yongzhong Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过统一的因果消融实验发现，同样的任务在不同的语言模型中由完全不同的注意力电路实现，表明模型内部的计算机制高度依赖于具体的训练过程和架构，不具备跨模型的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究一种标准化的机械解释性方法（识别任务选择性回路并进行因果消融验证）是否能在不同的模型架构（如稠密模型与混合专家模型）之间产生一致的机械论解释，从而验证当前大模型可解释性研究中“电路”概念的普适性和稳定性。

Method: 研究采用了一种统一的“筛选与消融”（screen-and-ablate）实验方案：首先根据任务模式选择性识别注意力头回路，随后通过与匹配随机基准对照的因果消融法进行验证。实验覆盖了四种任务（IOI、大于判断、后继序列、变量绑定）及三种不同的1B级语言模型（Pythia、OLMo、OLMoE）。此外，作者建立了一套包含五类结果（主要原因、次要原因、相关性、干扰项、空值）的量化分类评价体系。

Result: 实验结果表明，在12个任务-模型测试单元中，没有两个单元共享相同的核心因果回路。尽管模型表现出的行为能力一致，但其背后的注意力模式实现方式各异。该研究证明了当前通用的回路识别方法在跨模型迁移时存在不确定性，并发现MoE模型往往依赖于前置词（prev-token）位置基底来构建复合任务的逻辑电路。

Conclusion: 该研究指出，模型内部的机制解释性不具备跨模型家族的通用性。即便是在完成相同任务且具备相似行为能力的情况下，不同模型也可能采用截然不同的注意力模式来实现相同的逻辑。此外，作者提出了一种基于MoE架构的前置词基底假设，强调了模型架构对电路形成的重要影响。

Abstract: We test whether a single screen-and-ablate recipe -- identify attention-head circuits by task-pattern selectivity, then verify by causal ablation against a matched-random null -- produces consistent mechanistic claims across model families. The recipe ports across pipelines; the specific circuit it identifies does not. Across four composed tasks (indirect-object identification, greater-than, successor sequences, variable binding) and three 1B-class language models from distinct training pipelines (Pythia 1B / Pile / dense; OLMo 1B / DCLM / dense; OLMoE 1B-7B / DCLM / mixture-of-experts), we run a unified protocol with the matched-random null sampled across ten seeds per cell. The resulting 12 (task, model) cells contain no two that share the same primary causal screen at comparable effect size: the same task, with the same behavioral capability, is implemented through different attention-pattern types across models.
  We introduce a five-category screen-outcome taxonomy -- primary cause, secondary cause, correlate, interferer, null -- with quantitative thresholds, and show that all five outcomes appear in the panel. We propose a falsifiable hypothesis: the MoE model in our panel builds composed-task circuits on top of a foundational previous-token positional substrate (the prev-token-circuit ablation is the strongest causal screen on 3 of 4 tasks for OLMoE 1B-7B), with the IOI exception consistent with IOI being a final-position name-copying task whose structure directly probes a different pattern. The hypothesis comes with explicit predictions for other MoE language models.
  We frame the methodology honestly: the spectral participation-ratio signal from the companion methodology paper is a general indicator of specialized computation; what makes a finding task-specific is the task-pattern screen plus a per-model causal verification.

</details>


### [153] [TailLoR: Protecting Principal Components in Parameter-Efficient Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06494)
*Marius Dragoi,Ioana Pintilie,Alexandra Dragomir,Antonio Barbalau,Florin Brad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TailLoR 是一种持续学习的新型微调方法，通过锁定预训练权重的奇异向量，仅对长尾谱坐标进行低秩更新，并利用谱惩罚机制有效降低任务间的负面干扰，实现了高效的知识迁移与保留。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有持续学习中的参数高效微调方法在面对序列任务时常面临严重的干扰（Interference）问题，导致模型在学习新任务时遗忘旧知识。研究旨在通过探索预训练模型的谱结构，寻找一种能减少任务间冲突的参数优化策略。

Method: 提出 TailLoR 方法：1. 使用预训练权重的奇异向量矩阵 U 和 V 作为固定参考坐标系；2. 仅对奇异值矩阵进行低秩更新；3. 引入软谱惩罚（soft spectral penalty）机制，抑制对主导奇异方向的更新，从而引导模型将参数调整聚焦于长尾（低显著性）的谱坐标。

Result: TailLoR 在持续学习场景下展现了优异的性能，能够有效减少任务间的干扰，并确保模型在保持旧任务能力的同时，具备良好的新任务适应性。相比传统的低秩微调方法，该方法在参数效率和学习稳定性上表现更佳。

Conclusion: 通过利用预训练权重的奇异值分解（SVD）基底作为固定参考系，TailLoR 提供了一种高效且抗干扰的持续学习微调策略。该方法证明了在非主导奇异谱坐标中进行微调是实现任务间知识保留与新任务适应平衡的关键。

Abstract: Parameter-efficient finetuning methods based on spectral decomposition have enabled progress in Continual Learning. In this paper we introduce TailLoR, which utilizes the singular bases U and V of the pre-trained weights as a fixed reference frame to learn a low-rank update applied to the singular value matrix. A soft spectral penalty discourages updates aligned with dominant singular directions, reducing interference while routing fine-grained adaptation into the highly flexible, long-tail spectral coordinates.

</details>


### [154] [Selective-Advantage Entropy-Adaptive Horizon GRPO: Asymmetric Token-Level Discounting for Efficient Reinforcement Learning of Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05434)
*Chirag Chawla,Rohan Charudatt Salvi,Madhav S. Baidya*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对GRPO算法进行了改进，引入了基于不确定性的自适应折扣和选择性优势机制，在提升推理任务模型准确率的同时，大幅降低了训练过程的波动性与方差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的组相对策略优化（GRPO）算法在处理推理任务时，对所有token位置和采样轨迹的处理过于对称，未能在模型不确定性与优化稳定性之间取得平衡，容易导致训练过程不稳定或收敛至次优解。

Method: 提出了两种针对GRPO的扩展方法：1. 自适应视界GRPO (AH-GRPO)：引入基于累积熵的折扣机制，在模型不确定时减小有效优化视界；2. 选择性优势AH-GRPO (SA-AH-GRPO)：将上述折扣机制仅应用于优势为负的采样轨迹，同时保持对优势为正（成功）轨迹的完整优化信号。

Result: 在GSM8K数学推理基准测试中，SA-AH-GRPO在Qwen 2.5-3B模型上达到了0.858的Pass@1峰值，并将训练方差降低至0.0246（相比传统GRPO降低了3.6倍）；在1.5B模型上也取得了超过零样本基准的性能表现，证明了该方法在提升模型性能与训练稳定性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，非对称折扣策略能够有效保留正确推理路径的完整梯度信号，防止模型出现熵坍缩，并显著提升强化学习过程的稳定性。这一发现为结构化生成任务中基于可验证奖励的强化学习提供了一种具有原则性的归纳偏置。

Abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) has emerged as an effective reinforcement-learning algorithm for aligning language models on reasoning tasks, but it treats every token position and every sampled rollout symmetrically. We introduce two complementary extensions: (i) Adaptive-Horizon GRPO (AH-GRPO), which weights each token's policy gradient using a cumulative entropy-based discount that reduces the effective horizon when the model is uncertain, and (ii) Selective-Advantage AH-GRPO (SA-AH-GRPO), which applies this discounting only to negative-advantage rollouts, leaving positive-advantage, successful trajectories unattenuated. We evaluate standard GRPO with alpha = 0, AH-GRPO with alpha = 0.5, and SA-AH-GRPO with alpha = 0.5 on the GSM8K mathematical reasoning benchmark using both Qwen 2.5-1.5B-Instruct and Qwen 2.5-3B-Instruct fine-tuned with LoRA. On the 3B model, SA-AH-GRPO achieves Pass@1 = 0.858 at its peak at step 30 and maintains 0.846 at 180 steps, with training variance reduced to 0.0246, a 3.6 times reduction relative to GRPO while matching its peak accuracy. On the 1.5B model, SA-AH-GRPO achieves a peak Pass@1 of 0.686, improving over the zero-shot baseline of 0.637. Our analysis shows that asymmetric discounting preserves the full gradient signal on correct solutions, prevents entropy collapse, and substantially stabilises training, suggesting a principled inductive bias for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards on structured generation tasks.

</details>


### [155] [GOTabPFN: From Feature Ordering to Compact Tokenization for Tabular Foundation Models on High-Dimensional Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05441)
*Al Zadid Sultan Bin Habib,Md Younus Ahamed,Prashnna Kumar Gyawali,Gianfranco Doretto,Donald A. Adjeroh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 GOTabPFN，通过创新的特征排序（GO-LR）和压缩技术（NSC），使小型表格模型能高效处理高维小样本任务，突破了传统模型在有限算力下的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对现有表格基础模型在面对高维、小样本（HDLSS）数据时，因受限于 token 预算而难以发挥性能的问题，寻求一种无需重训练大型基座模型的轻量化适配方案。

Method: 提出了图引导排序与局部细化（GO-LR）算法，将其转化为带权最小线性排列问题；设计了神经启发子单元压缩（NSC）模块，将相邻特征聚合为元特征，以适配 TabPFN 的输入限制。

Result: 在多个表格基准测试中，GOTabPFN 在严格的 token 限制下表现出比现有方法更优的预测准确性和训练稳定性。

Conclusion: 通过整合特征排序优化与神经启发式压缩机制，GOTabPFN 成功解决了小型表格基础模型在处理高维小样本数据时的性能瓶颈，证明了在有限计算预算下实现高效推理的可行性。

Abstract: We investigate how to make small tabular foundation models effective for High-Dimensional, Low-Sample Size (HDLSS) tabular prediction without retraining large backbones. We introduce Graph-guided Ordering with Local Refinement (GO-LR), show its equivalence to weighted Minimum Linear Arrangement, and interpret the practical solver as a TSP-path-style surrogate. We propose GOTabPFN,which builds on GO-LR, and a Neuro-Inspired Subunit Compression (NSC) unit to pool locally adjacent ordered features into meta-features, yielding a compact representation that makes TabPFN-style prediction practical in HDLSS regimes. Across tabular benchmarks, GOTabPFN improves stability and accuracy under tight token budgets.
